hutvātha śālitoyena astreṇa prokṣayecchilāṃ
rakṣāṃ kṛtvā nṛsiṃhena mūlamantreṇa pūjayet
hutvā pūrṇāhutiṃ dadyāttato bhūtabaliṃ guruḥ
atra ye saṃsthitāḥ sattvā yātudhānāś ca guhyakāḥ
siddhādayo vā ye cānye tān sampūjya kṣamāpayet
viṣṇubimbārthamasmākaṃ yātraiṣā keśavājñayā
evaṃ prabodhitāḥ sattvā yānti tṛptā yathāsukhaṃ
oṃ namaḥ sakalalokāya viṣṇave prabhaviṣṇave
viśvāya viśvarūpāya svapnādhipataye namaḥ
svapne sarvāṇi kāryāṇi hṛdisthāni tu yāni me
oṃ oṃ hrūṃ phaṭ viṣṇave svāhā
prātararghyaṃ śilāyāṃ tu datvāstreṇāstrakaṃ yajet
kuddālaṭaṅkaśastrādyaṃ madhvānyāktamukhañcaret
ātmānaṃ cintayedviṣṇuṃ śilpinaṃ viśvakarmakaṃ
śastraṃ viṣṇvātmakaṃ dadyāt mukhapṛṣṭhādi darśayet
jitendriyaḥ ṭaṅkahastaḥ śilpī tu caturasrakāṃ
śilāṃ kṛtvā piṇḍikārthaṃ kiñcinnyūnāntu kalpayet
rathe sthāpya samānīya savastrāṃ kāruveśmani
vāsudevādipratimālakṣaṇavidhiḥ
bhagavānuvāca
vāsudevādipratimālakṣaṇaṃ pravadāmi te
prāsādasyottare pūrvamukhīṃ vā cottarānanāṃ
śilāṃ śilpī tu navadhā vibhajya navame 'ṃśake
sūrpabhaktaiḥ śilāyāṃ tu bhāgaṃ svāṅgulamucyate
dvyaṅgulaṃ golakaṃ nāmnā kālanetraṃ taducyate
bhāgamekaṃ tridhā bhaktvā pārṣṇibhāgaṃ prakalpayet
bhāgamekaṃ tathā jānau grīvāyāṃ bhāgameva ca
mukuṭaṃ tālamātraṃ syāttālamātraṃ tayā mukhaṃ
tālenaikena kaṇṭhantu tālena hṛdayaṃ tathā
nābhimeḍhrāntarantālaṃ dvitālāvūrukau tathā
tāladvayena jaṅghā syāt sūtrāṇi śṛṇu sāmprataṃ
kāryaṃ sūtradvayaṃ pāde jaṅghāmadhye tathāparaṃ
jānau sūtradvayaṃ kāryamūrūmadhye tathāparaṃ
meḍhre tathāparaṃ kāryaṃ kaṭyāṃ sūtrantathāparaṃ
hṛdaye ca tathā kāryaṃ kaṇṭhe sūtradvayaṃ tathā
lalāte cāparaṃ kāryaṃ mastake ca tathāparaṃ
mukuṭopari kartavyaṃ sūtramekaṃ vicakṣaṇaiḥ
kakṣātrikāntareṇaiva ghaṭ sūtrāṇi pradāpayet
lalāṭaṃ nāsikāvaktraṃ kartavyañcaturaṅgulaṃ
grīvākarṇau tu kartavyau āyāmāccaturaṅgulau
aṣṭāṅgulaṃ lalāṭantu vistāreṇa prakīrtitam
dvyaṅgulau pṛthukau karṇau karṇāpāṅgārdhapañcame
bhrūsamena tu sūtreṇa karṇaśrotraṃ prakīrtitam
viddhaṃ ṣaḍaṅgulaṃ karṇamaviddhañcaturaṅgulam
gandhapātraṃ tathāvartaṃ śaṣkulīṃ kalpayettathā
avyāttamevaṃ syādvaktraṃ vyāttaṃ tryaṅgulamiṣyate
nāsāvaṃśasamucchrāyaṃ mūle tvekāṅgulaṃ matam
ucchrāyā dvyaṅgulaṃ cāgre karavīropamāḥ smṛtāḥ
antaraṃ cakṣuṣoḥ kāryaṃ caturaṅgulamānataḥ
dvyaṅgulaṃ cākṣikoṇaṃ ca dvyaṅgulaṃ cāntaraṃ tayoḥ
tārā netratribhāgeṇa dṛktārā pañcamāṃśikā
tryaṅgulaṃ netravistāraṃ droṇī cārdhāṅgulā matā
bhrūmadhyaṃ dvyaṅgulaṃ kāryaṃ bhrūdairghyaṃ caturāṅgulam
ṣaṭtriṃśadaṅgulāyāmammastakasya tu veṣṭanam
mūrtīnāṃ keśavādīnāṃ dvātriṃśadveṣṭanaṃ bhavet
pañcanetrā tvadhogrīvā vistārādveṣṭanaṃ punaḥ
triguṇantu bhavedūrdhvaṃ vistṛtāṣṭāṅgulaṃ punaḥ
grīvātriguṇamāyāmaṃ grīvāvakṣontaraṃ bhavet
skandhāvaṣṭāṅgulau kāryau trikalāvaṃśakau śubhau
saptanetrau smṛtau bāhū prabāhū ṣoḍaśāṅgulau
bāhudaṇḍordhvato jñeyaḥ pariṇāhaḥ kalā nava
saptadaśāṅgulo madhye kūrpārordhe ca ṣoḍaśa
nāhaḥ prabāhumadhye tu ṣoḍaśāṅgula ucyate
agrahaste parīṇāho dvādaśāṅgula ucyate
vistareṇa karatalaṃ kīrtitaṃ tu ṣaḍaṅgulam
dairghyaṃ saptāṅgulaṃ kāryaṃ madhyā pajcāṅgulā matā
tarjanyanāmikā caiva tasmādardhāṅgulaṃ vinā
kaniṣṭhāṅguṣṭhakau kāryau caturaṅgulasammitau
dviparvoṅguṣṭhakaḥ kāryaḥ śeṣāgulyastriparvikāḥ
sarvāsāṃ parvaṇordhena nakhamānaṃ vidhīyate
vakṣaso yat pramāṇantu jaṭharaṃ tatpramāṇataḥ
aṅgulaikaṃ bhavennābhī vedhena ca pramāṇataḥ
tato meḍhrāntaraṃ kāryaṃ tālamātraṃ pramāṇataḥ
nābhimadhye prīṇāho dvicatvāriṃśadaṅgulaiḥ
antaraṃ stanayoḥ kāryaṃ tālamātraṃ pramāṇataḥ
catuḥṣaṣṭyaṅgulaṃ kāryaṃ veṣṭanaṃ vakṣasaḥ sphuṭam
pariṇāhas tathā kaṭyā catuḥpañcāśadaṅgulaiḥ
vistāraścorumūle tu procyate dvādaśaṅgulaḥ
vistṛtāṣṭāṅgulaṃ jānutriguṇā pariṇāhataḥ
jaṅghāmadhye tu vistāraḥ saptāṅgula udāhṛtaḥ
triguṇā paridhiścāsya jaṅghāgraṃ pañcavistarāt
triguṇā paridhiścāsya pādau tālapramāṇakau
gulphāt pūrvaṃ tu kartavyaṃ pramāṇāccaturaṅgulam
pañcāṅgulastu nāhosya dīrghā tadvat pradeśinī
aṣṭamāṣṭāṃśatonyūnaḥ śeṣāṅgulyaḥ krameṇa tu
sapādāṅgulamutsedhamaṅguṣṭasya prakīrtitaṃ
yavonamaṅgulaṃ kāryamaṅguṣṭhasya nakhaṃ tathā
ardhāṅgulaṃ tathānyāsāṃ kramān nyūnaṃ tu kārayet
aṅgulau vṛṣaṇau kāryau meḍhraṃ tu caturaṅgulam
pariṇāhotra koṣāgraṃ kartavyañcaturaṅgulam
ṣaḍaṅgulaparīṇāhau vṛṣaṇau parikīrtitau
pratimā bhūṣaṇāḍhyā syādetaduddeśalakṣaṇam
anayaiva diśā kāryaṃ loke dṛṣṭvā tu lakṣaṇam
vāme śaṅkhaṃ gadādhastādvāsudevasya lakṣaṇāt
śrīpuṣṭau vāpi kartavye padmavīṇākarānvite
ūrumātrocchitāyāme mālāvidyādharau tathā
prabhāmaṇḍalasaṃsthau tau prabhā hastyādibhūṣaṇā
padmābhaṃ pādapīṭhantu pratimāsvevamācaret
piṇḍikālakṣaṇakathanaṃ
bhagavānuvāca
piṇḍikālakṣaṇaṃ vakṣye dairghyeṇa pratimāsamā
ucchrāyaṃ pratimārdhantu catuḥṣaṣṭipuṭāṃ ca tām
tyaktvā paṅktidvayaṃ cādhastadūrdhvaṃ yattu koṣṭhakam
ūrdhvaṃ paṅgktidvayaṃ tyaktvā adhastād yattu koṣṭhakam
mekhalā bhāgamātrā syāt khātaṃ tasyārdhamānataḥ
bhāgaṃ bhāgaṃ parityajya pārśvayorubhayoḥ samaṃ
datvā caikaṃ padaṃ vāhye pramāṇaṃ kārayed budhaḥ
nānāprakārabhedena bhadreyaṃ piṇḍikā śubhā
aṣṭatālā tu kartavyā devī lakṣmīstayā striyaḥ
karṇapāśo dhikaḥ kāryaḥ sṛkkaṇīsamasūtrataḥ
namraṃ kalāvihīnantu kuryādaṃśadvayaṃ tathā
grīvā sārdhakalā kāryā tadvistāropaśobhitā
netraṃ vinā tu vistārau ūrū jānū ca piṇḍikā
aṅghripṛṣṭhau sphicau kaṭyāṃ yathābhāgaṃ prakalpayet
saptāṃśonās tathāṅgulyo dīrghaṃ viṣkambhanāhataṃ
netraikavarjitāyāmā jaṅghorū ca tathā kaṭiḥ
madhyapārśvaṃ ca tadvṛttaṃ ghanaṃ pīnaṃ kucadvayaṃ
tālamātrau stanau karyau kaṭiḥ sārdhakalādhikā
lakṣma śeṣaṃ purāvatsyāt dakṣiṇe cāmubujaṃ kare
dīrghaghoṇastu garuḍaś cakrāṅgādyānatho vade
śālagrāmādimūrtilakṣaṇakathanaṃ
bhagavānuvāca
śālagrāmādimūrteś ca vakṣyehaṃ bhuktimuktidāḥ
kṛṣṇo nārāyaṇo nābhyunnataḥ śuṣiradīrghavān
parameṣṭho sābjacakraḥ pṛṣṭhacchidrakaś ca vindumān
sthūlacakro 'sito viṣṇurmadhye rekhā gadākṛtiḥ
nṛsiṃhaḥ kapikaḥ sthūlavakraḥ syāt pañcavindukaḥ
varāhaḥ śaktiliṅgaḥ syāt taccakrau viṣamau sṛtau
indranīlanibhaḥ sthūlastrirekhālāñchitaḥ śubhaḥ
kūrmastathonnataḥ pṛṣṭhe vartulāvartako 'sitaḥ
hayagrīvoṅkuśāvārarekho nīlaḥ savindukaḥ
śrīdharo vanamālāṅkaḥ pañjarekhastu vartulaḥ
sudarśanastvekacakro lakṣmīnārāyaṇo dvayāt
janārdanaś catuś cakro vāsudevaś ca pañcabhiḥ
ṣaṭvakraś caiva pradyumnaḥ saṅkarṣaṇañca saptabhiḥ
puruṣottamoṣṭacakro navavyūho navāṅkitaḥ
daśāvatāro daśabhirdaśaikenāniruddhakaḥ
dvādaśātmā dvādaśabhirata ūrdhvamanantakaḥ
śālagrāmādipūjākathanaṃ
bhagavānuvāca
śālagrāmādicakrāṅkapūjāḥ siddhyai vadāmi te
trividhā syāddhareḥ pūjā kāmyākāmyobhayātmikā
mīnādīnāntu pañcānāṃ kāmyātho vobhayātmikā
cakrādīnāṃ trayāṇāntu śālagrāmārcanaṃ śṛṇu
uttamā niṣphalā pūjā kaniṣṭhā saphalārcanā
praṇavaṃ hṛdi vinyasya ṣaḍaṅgaṅkaradehayoḥ
kṛtamudrātrayaś cakrād vahiḥ pūve guruṃ yajet
āpye gaṇaṃ vāyave ca dhātāraṃ nairṛte yajet
vidhātārañca kartāraṃ hartāraṃ dakṣasaumyayoḥ
viśvaksenaṃ yajedīśe āgneye kṣetrapālakam
ṛgādivedān prāgādau ādhārānantakaṃ bhuvaṃ
pīṭhaṃ padmaṃ cārkacandravahnyākhyaṃ maṇḍalatrayaṃ
āsanaṃ dvādaśārṇena tatra sthāpya śilāṃ yajet
pūrvādāvatha vedādyair gāyatrībhyāṃ jitādinā
śālagrāmasya prathamā pūjārtho niṣphalocyate
pūrvavat ṣoḍaśārañca sapadmaṃ maṇḍalaṃ likhet
pūrve saumye dhanurvāṇān vedādyair āsanaṃ dadet
śilāṃ nyased dvādaśārṇaistṛtīyaṃ pūjanaṃ śṛṇu
aṣṭārṇenāsanaṃ datvā tenaiva ca śilāṃ nyaset
pūjayeddaśadhā tena gāyatrībhyāṃ jitaṃ tathā
bhagavānuvāca
oṃrūpaḥ keśavaḥ padmaśaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ
nārāyaṇaḥ śaṅkhapadmagadācakrī pradakṣiṇaṃ
bhokṣadaḥ śrīgadī padmī śaṅkhī viṣṇuś ca cakradhṛk
śaṅkhacakragadāpadmī vāmanaḥ pātu māṃ sadā
gaditaḥ śrīdharaḥ padmī cakraśārṅgī ca śaṅkhyapi
hṛṣīkeśo gadācakrī padmī cakraśaṅkhī ca pātu naḥ
varadaḥ padmanābhastu śaṅkhābjārigadādharaḥ
dāmodaraḥ padmaśaṅkhagadācakrī namāmi taṃ
saṅkarṣaṇo gadī śaṅkhī padmī cakrī ca pātu vaḥ
gadī cakrī śaṅkhagadī pradyumnaḥ padmabhṛt prabhuḥ
aniruddhaś cakragadī śaṅkhī padmī ca pātu naḥ
sureśoryabjaśaṅkhāḍhyaḥ śrīgadī puruṣottamaḥ
adhokṣajaḥ padmagadī śaṅkhī cakrī ca pātu vaḥ
devo nṛsiṃhaś cakrābjagadāśaṅkhī namāmi tam
acyutaḥ śrīgadī padmī cakrī śaṅkhī ca pātu vaḥ
bālarūpī śaṅkhagadī upendraś cakrapadmyapi
janārdanaḥ padmacakrī śaṅkhadhārī gadādharaḥ
śaṅkhī padmī ca cakrī ca hariḥ kaumodakīdharaḥ
kṛṣṇaḥ śaṅkhī gadī padmī cakrī me bhuktimuktidaḥ
ādimūttirvāsudevastasmāt saṅkarṣaṇobhavat
dvādaśākṣarakaṃ stotraṃ caturviṃśatimūrtimat
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi nirmalaḥ sarvamāpnuyāt
matsyādilakṣaṇavarṇanaṃ
bhagavānuvāca
daśāvatāraṃ matsyādilakṣaṇaṃ pravadāmi te
matsyākārastu matsyaḥ syāt kūrmaḥ kārmākṛlirbhavet
narāṅgo vātha kartavyo bhūvarāho gadādibhṛt
dakṣiṇe vāmake śaṅkhaṃ lakṣmīrvā padmameva vā
śrīvāmakūrparasthā tu kṣmānantau caraṇānugau
varāhasthāpanādrājyaṃ bhavābdhitaraṇaṃ bhavet
narasiṃho vivṛttāsyo vāmorukṣatadānavaḥ
chatrī daṇḍī vāmanaḥ syādathavā syāccaturbhujaḥ
rāmaścāpeṣuhastaḥ syāt kaḍgī paraśunānvitaḥ
rāmaścāpī śarī khaḍgī śaṅkhī vā dvibhujaḥ smṛtaḥ
gadālāṅgaladhārī ca rāmo vātha caturbhujaḥ
vāmordhve lāṅgalaṃ dadyādadhaḥ śaṅkhaṃ suśobhanaṃ
muṣalaṃ dakṣiṇordhve tu cakrañcādhaḥ suśobhanaṃ
śāntātmā lambakarṇaś ca gaurāṅgaścāmbarāvṛtaḥ
athavāśvasthitaḥ khaḍgī śaṅkhacakraśarānvitaḥ
lakṣaṇaṃ vāsudevādinavakasya vadāmi te
lāṅgalī muṣalī rāmo gadāpadmadharaḥ smṛtaḥ
pradyumno dakṣiṇe vajraṃ śaṅkhaṃ vāme dhanuḥ kare
gadānābhyāvṛtaḥ pītyā pradyumno vā dhanuḥśarī
caturbhujo niruddhaḥ syāttathā nārāyaṇo vibhuḥ
caturmukhaś caturbāhurvṛhajjaṭharamaṇḍalaḥ
lambakūrco jaṭāyukto vrahmā haṃsāgravāhanaḥ
dakṣiṇe cākṣasūtrañca sruvo vāme tu kuṇḍikā
ājyasthālī sarasvatī sāvitrī vāmadakṣiṇe
viṣṇuraṣṭabhujastārkṣe kare khaḍgastu dakṣiṇe
gadāśaraś ca varado vāme kārmukakheṭake
acaturbāhurvarāhastu śeṣaḥ pāṇitale dhṛtaḥ
dhārayan bāhunā pṛthvīṃ vāmnena kamalādharaḥ
pādalagnā dharā kāryā padā lakṣmīrvyavasthitā
trailokyamohanastārkṣye aṣṭabāhustu dakṣiṇe
cakraṃ khaḍgaṃ ca muṣalaṃ aṅkuśaṃ vāmake kare
śaṅkhaśārṅgagadāpāśān padmavīṇāsamanvite
lakṣmīḥ sarasvatī kārye viśvarūpo 'tha dakṣiṇe
mudgaraṃ ca tathā pāśaṃ śaktiśūlaṃ śaraṃ kare
vāme śaṅkhañca śārṅgañca gadāṃ pāśaṃ ca tomaraṃ
lāṅgalaṃ paraśuṃ daṇḍaṃ churikāṃ carmakṣepakaṃ
viṃśadbāhuś caturvaktro dakṣiṇasthotha vāmake
śriyā dhṛtaikacaraṇo vimalādyābhirīḍitaḥ
śūlarṣṭidhārī dakṣe ca gadācakradharo pade
rudrakeśavalakṣmāṅgo gaurīlakṣmīsamanvitaḥ
śaṅkhacakragadāvedapāṇiścāśvaśirā hariḥ
vāmapādo dhṛtaḥ śeṣe dakṣiṇaḥ kūrmapṛṣṭhagaḥ
dattātreyo dvibāhuḥ syādvāmotsaṅge śriyā saha
viśvaksenaś cakragadī halī śaṅkhī harergaṇaḥ
devīpratimālakṣaṇakathanaṃ
bhagavānuvāca
caṇḍī viṃśatibāhuḥ syādbibhratī dakṣiṇaiḥ karaḥ
śūlāsiśakticakrāṇi pāśaṃ kheṭāyudhābhayaṃ
ḍamaruṃ śaktikāṃ vāmair nāgapāśañca kheṭakaṃ
kuṭhāṅkuśacāpāṃś ca ghaṇṭādhvajagadāṃs tathā
ādarśamudgarān hastaiś caṇḍī vā daśabāhukā
śūlahasto vamadrakto raktasraṅmūrdhajekṣaṇaḥ
siṃhenāsvādyamānastu pāśabaddho gale bhṛśaṃ
yāmyāṅghyrākrāntasiṃhā ca savyāṅghrirnīcagāsure
caṇḍikeyaṃ trinetrā ca saśastrā ripumardanī
navapadmātmake sthāne pūjyā durgā svamūrtitaḥ
aṣṭādaśabhujaikā tu dakṣe muṇḍaṃ ca kheṭakaṃ
ādarśatarjanīcāpaṃ dhvajaṃ ḍamarukaṃ tathā
pāśaṃ vāme bibhratī ca śaktimudgaraśūlakaṃ
vajrakhaḍgāṅkuśaśarān cakrandevī śalākayā
etair evāyudhair yuktā śeṣāḥ ṣoḍaśabahukāḥ
ḍamaruṃ tarjanīṃ tyaktvā rudracaṇḍādayo nava
rudracaṇḍā pracaṇḍā ca caṇḍogrā caṇḍanāyikā
caṇḍā caṇdavatī caiva caṇḍarūpāticaṇḍikā
ugracaṇḍā ca madhyasthā rocanābhāruṇāsitā
nīlā śuklā dhūmrikā ca pītā śvetā ca siṃhagāḥ
mahiṣotha pumān śastrī tatkacagrahamuṣṭikāḥ
ālīḍhā nava durgāḥ syuḥ sthāpyāḥ putrādivṛddhaye
tathā gaurī ca caṇḍikādyā kuṇḍyakṣararadāgnidhṛk
skandhamūrdhakarā vāme dvitīye dhṛtadarpaṇā
lakṣmīryāmyakarāmbhojā vāme śrīphalasaṃyutā
pustākṣamālikāhastā vīṇāhastā sarasvatī
kumbhābjahastā śvetābhā makaropari jāhnavī
kūrmagā yamunā kumbhakarā śyāmā ca pūjyate
savīṇastumburuḥ śuklaḥ śūlī mātragrato vṛṣe
gaurī caturmukhī brāhmī akṣamālāsurānvitā
kuṇḍakṣapātriṇī vāme haṃsagā śāṅkarī sitā
śaracāpau dakṣiṇe 'syā vāme cakraṃ dhanurvṛṣe
kaumārī śikhigā raktā śaktihastā dvibāhukā
cakraśaṅkhadharā savye vāme lakṣmīrgadābjadhṛk
daṇḍaśaṅkhāsi gadayā vārāho mahiṣasthitā
cāmuṇḍā koṭarāghnī syānnirmāṃsā tu trilocanā
nirmāṃsā asthisārā vā ūrdhvakeśī kṛśodarī
dvīpacarmadharā vāme kapālaṃ paṭṭiśaṅkare
śūlaṃ kartrī dakṣaṇe 'syāḥ śavārūḍhāsthitabhūṣaṇā
vināyako narākāro vṛhatkukṣirgajānanaḥ
vistārāddairghyatacaiva śuṇḍaṃ ṣaṭtriṃśadaṅgulaṃ
kalā dvādaśa nāḍī tu grīvā sārdhakalocchritā
ṣaṭtriṃśadaṅgulaṃ kaṇṭhaṃ guhyamadhyardhamaṅgulaṃ
nābhirūrū dvādaśañca jaṅghe pāde tu dakṣiṇe
svadantaṃ paraśuṃ vāme laḍḍukañcotpalaṃ śaye
sumukhī ca viḍālākṣī pārśve skando mayūragaḥ
svāmī śākho viśākhaś ca dvibhujo bālarūpadhṛk
dakṣe śaktiḥ kukkuṭotha ekavaktrotha ṣaṇmukhaḥ
ṣaḍbhujo vā dvādaśabhirgrāmeraṇye dvibāhukaḥ
śaktīṣupāśanistriṃśatotradostarjanīyutaḥ
śaktyā dākṣiṇahasteṣu ṣaṭsu vāme kare tathā
śikhipicchandhanuḥ kheṭaṃ patākābhayakukkuṭe
kapālakartarīśūlapāśabhṛdyāmyasaumyayoḥ
gajacarmabhṛdūrdhvāsyapādā syāt rudracarcikā
saiva cāṣṭabhujā devī śiroḍamarukānvitā
tena sā rudracāmuṇḍā nāṭeśvaryatha nṛtyatī
iyameva mahālakṣmīrupaviṣṭā caturmukhī
nṛvājimahiṣebhāṃś ca khādantī ca kare sthitān
daśabāhustrinetrā ca śastrāsiḍamarutrikaṃ
bibhratī dakṣiṇe haste vāme ghaṇṭāṃ ca kheṭakaṃ
khaṭvāṅgaṃ ca triśūlañca siddhacāmuṇḍakāhvayā
etadrūpā bhavedanyā pāśāṅkuśayutāruṇā
etāḥ śmaśānajā raudrā ambāṣṭakamidaṃ smṛtaṃ
kṣamā śivāvṛtā vṛddhā dvibhujā vivṛtānanā
danturā kṣemakarī syādbhūmau jānukarā sthitā
yakṣiṇyastabdhadīrghākṣāḥ śākinyo vakradṛṣṭayaḥ
piṅgākṣāḥ syurmahāramyā rūpiṇyopsarasaḥ sadā
sākṣamālī triśūlī ca nandīśo dvārapālakaḥ
mahākālosimuṇḍī syācchūlakhaṭakavāṃs tathā
kṛśo bhaṅgī ca nṛtyan vai kuṣmāṇḍasthūlakharvavān
gajagokarṇavaktrādyā vīrabhadrādayo gaṇāḥ
ghaṇṭākarṇoṣṭadaśadoḥ pāparogaṃ vidārayan
vajrāsidaṇḍacakreṣumuṣalāṅkuśamudgarān
dakṣiṇe tarjanīṃ kheṭaṃ śaktiṃ muṇḍañca pāśakaṃ
cāpaṃ ghaṇṭāṃ kuṭhārañca dvābhyāñcaiva triśūlakaṃ
ghaṇṭāmālākulo devo visphoṭakavimardanaḥ
sūryādipratimālakṣaṇaṃ
bhagavānuvāca
masībhājanalekhanyau bibhratkuṇḍī tu dakṣiṇe
vāme tu piṅgalo dvāri daṇḍabhṛt sa ravergaṇaḥ
bālavyajanadhāriṇyau pārśve rājñī ca niṣprabhā
athavāśvārūḍhaḥ kārya ekastu bhāskaraḥ
mudgaraśūlacakrābjabhṛtognyādividiksthitāḥ
sūryāryamādirakṣontāś caturhastā dviṣaḍdale
varuṇaḥ sūryanāmā ca sahasrāṃśus tathāparaḥ
dhātā tapanasañjñaś ca savitātha gabhastikaḥ
raviś caivātha parjanyastvaṣṭā mitrotha viṣṇukaḥ
meṣādirāśisaṃsthāś ca mārgādikārttikāntakāḥ
kṛṣṇo rakto manāgraktaḥ pītaḥ pāṇḍarakaḥ sitaḥ
kapilaḥ pītavarṇaś ca śukābho dhavalas tathā
dhūmro nīlaḥ kramādvarṇāḥ śaktayaḥ keśarāgragāḥ
iḍā suṣumnā viśvārcirindusañjñā pramardinī
praharṣiṇī mahākālī kapilā ca prabodhanī
nīlāmbarā ghanāntasthā amṛtākhyā ca śaktayaḥ
varuṇādeś ca tadvarṇāḥ keśarāgreṣu vinyaset
kuṇḍikājapyāmālīnduḥ kujaḥ śaktyakṣamālikaḥ
budhaścāpākṣapāṇiḥ syājjīvaḥ kuṇḍyakṣamālikaḥ
śukraḥ kuṇḍyakṣamālī syāt kiṇkiṇīsūtravāñchaniḥ
ardhacandradharo rāhuḥ ketuḥ khaḍgī ca dīpabhṛt
anantastakṣakaḥ karkaḥ padmo mahābjaḥ śaṅkhakaḥ
kulikaḥ sūtriṇaḥ sarve phaṇavaktrā mahāprabhāḥ
indro vajrī gajārūḍhaśchāgagogniś ca śaktimān
yamo daṇḍī ca mahiṣe nairṛtaḥ khaḍgavān kare
makare varuṇaḥ pāśī vāyurdhvajadharo mṛge
gadī kuvero meṣastha īśānaś ca jaṭī vṛṣe
dvibāhavo lokapālā viśvakarmākṣasūtrabhṛt
hanūmān vajrahastaḥ syāt padbhyāṃ sampīḍitāśrayaḥ
vīṇāhastāḥ kinnarāḥ syurmālāvidyādharāś ca khe
durbalāṅgāḥ piśācāḥ syurvetālā vikṛtānanāḥ
kṣetrapālāḥ śūlavantaḥ pretā mahodarāḥ kṛśāḥ
devīpratimālakṣaṇaṃ
bhagavānuvāca
yoginyaṣṭāṣṭakaṃ vakṣye aindrādīśāntataḥ kramāt
akṣobhyā rūkṣakarṇo ca rākṣasī kṛpaṇākṣayā
piṅgākṣī ca kṣayā kṣemā ilā līlālayā tathā
lolā laktā balākeśī lālasā vimalā punaḥ
hutāśā ca viśālākṣī huṅkārā vaḍavāmukhī
mahākrūrā krodhanā tu bhayaṅkarī mahānanā
sarvajñā taralā tārā ṛgvedā tu hayānanā
sārākhyā rudraśaṅgrāhī sambarā tālajaṅghikā
raktākṣī suprasiddhā tu vidyujjihvā karaṅkiṇī
meghanādā pracaṇḍogrā kālakarṇī varapradā
candrā candrāvalī caiva prapañcā pralayāntikā
śiśuvaktrā piśācī ca piśitāśā ca lolupā
dhamanī tāpanī caiva rāgiṇī vikṛtānanā
vāyuvegā vṛhatkukṣirvikṛtā viśvarūpikā
viḍālī revatī caiva pūtanā vijayāntikā
aṣṭahastāś caturhastā icchāstrāḥ sarvasiddhidāḥ
bhairavaścārkahastaḥ syāt kūrparāsyo jaṭendubhṛt
khaḍgāṅkuśakuṭhāreṣuviśvabhayabhṛdekataḥ
cāpatriśūlakhaṭvāṅgapāśakārdhavarodyataḥ
gajacarmadharo dvābhyāṃ kṛttivāsohibhūṣataḥ
pretāśano mātṛmadhye pūjyaḥ pañcānanothavā
avilomāgniparyantaṃ dīrghāṣṭakaikabheditaṃ
tatṣaḍaṅgāni jātyantair anvitaṃ ca kramād yajet
mandirāgnidalārūḍhaṃ suvarṇarasakānvitaṃ
nādavindvandusaṃyuktaṃ mātṛnāthāṅgadīpitaṃ
vīrabhadro vṛṣārūḍho mātragre sa caturmukhaḥ
gaurīṃ tu dvibhujā tryakṣā śūlinī darpaṇānvitā
śūlaṃ galantikā kuṇḍī varadā ca caturbhujā
abjasthā lalitā skandagaṇādarśaśalākayā
caṇḍikā saśahastā syāt khaḍgaśūlāriśaktidhṛk
dakṣe vāme nāgapāśaṃ carmāgkuśakuṭhārakaṃ
dhanuḥ siṃhe ca mahiṣaḥ śūlena prahatogrataḥ
liṅgalakṣaṇaṃ
bhagavānuvāca
liṅgādilakṣaṇaṃ vakṣye kamalodbhava tacchṛṇu
brahmaviṣṇuśivāṃśeṣu vardhamānoyamucyate
caturasresya varṇārdhaṃ guhyakoṇeṣu lāñchayet
aṣṭāgraṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ bhāgaṃ sidhyatyeva na saṃśayaḥ
ṣoḍaśāsraṃ tataḥ kuryāddvātriṃśāsraṃ tataḥ punaḥ
catuḥṣaṣṭyasrakaṃ kṛtvā vartulaṃ sādhayettataḥ
vistāramatha liṅgasya aṣṭadhā saṃvibhājayet
triṣu bhāgeṣu sadṛśamāyāmaṃ yasya cistaraḥ
sarveṣāmeva liṅgānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ śṛṇu sāmprataṃ
ṣoḍaśāṅgulaliṅgasya ṣaḍbhāgair bhājito yathā
yavāṣṭamuttare kāryaṃ śeṣāṇāṃ yavahānitaḥ
aṣṭadhā taddvayaṃ kṛtvā ūrdhvabhāgatryaṃ tyajet
ūrdhvañca pañcamādbhāgād bhrāmya rekhāṃ pralambayet
etat sādhāraṇaṃ proktaṃ liṅgānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ mayā
sarvasādhāraṇaṃ vakṣye piṇḍikāntānnibodha me
brahmabhāgapraveśañca jñātvā liṅgasya cocchrayaṃ
tathā sumucchrayaṃ jñātvā piṇḍikāṃ pravibhājayet
dvibhāgamucchritaṃ pīṭhaṃ vistāraṃ liṅgasammitam
tribhāgaṃ madhyataḥ khātaṃ kṛtvā pīṭhaṃ vibhājayet
mekhalāṣoḍaśāṃśena khātaṃ vā tatpramāṇajñaḥ
ucchrāyaṃ tasya pīṭhasya vikārāṅgaṃ tu kārayet
bhūmau praviṣṭamekaṃ tu bhāgaikena piṇḍikā
kaṇṭhaṃ bhāgaistribhiḥ kāryaṃ bhāgenaikena paṭṭikā
dyaṃgena cordhvapaṭṭantu ekāṃśāḥ śeṣapaṭṭikā
bhāgaṃ bhāgaṃ praviṣṭantu yāvat kaṇṭhaṃ tataḥ punaḥ
nirgamaṃ bhāgamekaṃ tu yāvadvai śeṣapaṭṭikā
piṇḍikāsahitaṃ liṅgametat sādhāraṇaṃ smṛtam
liṅgamānādikathanaṃ
bhagavānuvāca
vakṣyāmyanyaprakāreṇa liṅgamānādikaṃ śṛṇu
bhūtaye vastraliṅgantu liṅgantātkālikaṃ viduḥ
pakvāpakvaṃ mṛṇmayaṃ syādapakvāt pakvajaṃ varaṃ
tato dārumayaṃ puṇyaṃ dārujāt śailajaṃ varaṃ
śailādvaraṃ tu muktājaṃ tato lauhaṃ suvarṇajaṃ
rājataṃ kīrtitaṃ tāmraṃ paittalaṃ bhuktimuktidaṃ
mānādi neṣṭaṃ siddhādi sthāpitetha svayambhuvi
vāme ca svecchayā teṣāṃ pīṭhaprāsādakalpanā
aṅgulād gṛhaliṅgaṃ syādyāvat pañcaśāṅgulaṃ
dvāramānāt trisaṅkhyākaṃ navadhā garbhamānataḥ
evaṃ liṅgāni ṣaṭtriṃśat jñeyāni jyeṣṭhamānataḥ
madhyamānena ṣaṭtriṃśat ṣaṭtriṃśadadhamena ca
itthamaikyena liṅgānāṃ śatamaṣṭottaraṃ bhavet
ekāṅgulādipañcāntaṃ kanyasañcalamucyate
ṣadvādidaśaparyantañcalaṃ liṅgañca madhyamaṃ
ekādaśāṅgulādi syāt jyeṣṭhaṃ pañcadaśāntakam
ravibhirhemabhārotthaṃ liṅgaṃ śeṣaistripañcabhiḥ
ṣoḍaśāṃśe ca vedāṃśe yugaṃ luptvordhvadeśataḥ
dvātriṃśatṣoḍaśāṃśāṃś ca koṇayostu vilopayet
caturniveśanāt kaṇṭho viṃśatistriyugais tathā
pārśvābhyāṃ tu viluptābhyāṃ calaliṅgaṃ bhavedvaraṃ
dhāmno yugartunāgāṃśair dvāraṃ hīnāditaḥ kramāt
garbhārdhenādhamaṃ liṅgaṃ bhūtāṃśaiḥ syāt tribhirvaraṃ
evaṃ syurnava sūtrāṇi bhūtasūtraiś ca madhyamaṃ
dvyantaro vāmavāmañca liṅgānāṃ dīrghatā nava
ekaikaliṅgamadhyeṣu trīṇi trīṇi ca pādaśaḥ
liṅgāni ghaṭayeddhīmān ṣaṭsu cāṣṭottareṣu ca
bhāgeśañcāpyamīśañca devejyantulyasaṃjñitaṃ
catvāri liṅgarūpāṇi viṣkambheṇa tu lakṣayet
dīrghamāyānvitaṃ kṛtvā liṅgaṃ kuryāt trirūpakaṃ
caturaṣṭāṣṭavṛttañca tattvatrayaguṇātmakaṃ
liṅgānāmīpsitaṃ dairghyaṃ tena kṛtvāṅgulāni vai
dhvajādyāyaiḥ surair bhūtaiḥ śikhibhirvā haret kṛtiṃ
tānyaṅgulāni yaccheṣaṃ lakṣayecca śubhāśubhaṃ
dhvajādyā dhvajasiṃhebhavṛṣāḥ jyeṣṭhāḥ pare śubhāḥ
svareṣu ṣaḍjagāndhārapañcamāḥ śubhadāyakāḥ
bhūteṣu ca śubhā bhūḥ syādagniṣvāhavanīyakaḥ
uktāyāmasya cārdhāṃśe nāgāṃśair bhājite kramāt
rasabhūtāṃśaṣaṣṭhāṃśatryaṃśādhikaśarair bhavet
āḍhyānāḍhyasurejyārkatulyānāñcaturasratā
pañcamaṃ vardhamānākhyaṃ vyāsānnāhapravṛddhitaḥ
āḍhyādīnāṃ tridhā sthaulyādyavadhūtaṃ tadaṣṭadhā
pañcaviṃśatiliṅgāni nādye devārcite tathā
caturdaśasahasrāṇi caturdaśaśatāni ca
teṣāṃ koṇārdhakoṇasthaiścintyāt koṇāni sūtrakaiḥ
vistāraṃ madhyamaḥ kṛtvā sthāpyaṃ vā madhyatastrayaṃ
vibhāgādūrdhvamaṣṭāsro dvyaṣṭāsraḥ syācchivāṃśakaḥ
pādājjānvantako brahmā nābhyanto viṣṇurityataḥ
chatrābhaṃ kukkuṭābhaṃ vā bālendupratimākṛtiḥ
catvāri tatra sūtrāṇi bhāgabhāgānupātanāt
puṇḍarīkantu bhāgena viśālākhyaṃ vilopanāt
triśātanāttu śrīvatsaṃ śatrukṛdvedalopanāt
śiraḥ sarvasame śreṣṭhaṃ kukkuṭābhaṃ surāhvaye
anādyasya śiraḥ proktamardhacandraṃ śiraḥ śṛṇu
aṃśāt prānte yugāṃśaiś ca tvekāhānyāmṛtākṣakaṃ
pūrṇabālendukumudaṃ dvitrivedakṣayāt kramāt
arkāṃśaṃ pūrvavat tyaktvā ṣaṭ sthānāni vivartayat
śironnatiḥ prakartavyā lalāṭaṃ nāsikā tataḥ
vadanaṃ civukaṃ grīvā yugabhāgair bhujākṣibhiḥ
karābhyāṃ mukulīkṛtya pratimāyāḥ pramāṇataḥ
mukhaṃ prati samaḥ kāryo vistārādaṣṭamāṃśataḥ
caturmukhaṃ mayā proktaṃ trimukhañcocyate śṛṇu
karṇapādādhikāstasya lalāṭādīni nirdiśet
vistarādaṣṭamāṃśena mukhānāṃ pratinirgamaḥ
ekavaktraṃ tathā kāryaṃ pūrvasyāṃ saumyalocanaṃ
lalāṭanāsikāvaktragrīvāyāñca vivartayet
bhujācca pañcamāṃśena bhujahīnaṃ vivartayet
vistārasya ṣaḍaṃśena mukhair nirgamanaṃ hitaṃ
sarveṣāṃ mukhaliṅgānāṃ trapuṣaṃ vātha kukkuṭaṃ
piṇḍikālakṣaṇakathanaṃ
bhagavānuvāca
ataḥ paraṃpravakṣyāmi pratimānāntu piṇḍikām
tṛtīyena tu vā tulyaṃ tattribhāgeṇa mekhalā
piṇḍikārdhena vā tulyaṃ dairghyamīśasya kīrtitam
īśaṃ vā tulyadīrghañca jñātvā sūtraṃ prakalpayet
ucchrāyaṃ pūrvavat kuryādbhāgaṣoḍaśasaṅkhyayā
adhaḥ ṣaṭkaṃ dvibhāgantu kaṇṭhaṃ kuryāttribhāgakam
śeṣāstvekaikaśaḥ kāryāḥ pratiṣṭhānirgamās tathā
paṭṭikā piṇḍikā ceyaṃ sāmānyapratimāsu ca
piṇḍikāpi yathāśobhaṃ kartavyā satataṃ hareḥ
sarveṣāmeva devānāṃ śiṣṇūktaṃ mānamucyate
devīnāmapi sarvāsāṃ lakṣmyuktaṃ mānamucyate
dikpālayāgakathanaṃ
bhagavānuvāca
pratiṣṭhāpañcakaṃ vakṣye pratimātmā tu pūruṣaḥ
prakṛtiḥ piṇḍikā lakṣmīḥ pratiṣṭhā yogakastayoḥ
garbhasūtraṃ tu niḥsārya prāsādasyāgrato guruḥ
aṣṭaṣoḍaśaviṃśāntaṃ maṇḍapañcādhamādikam
snānaṃ kalaśārthañca yāgadravyārthamardhataḥ
tribhāgeṇārdhabhāgena vediṃ kuryāttu śobhanām
kalaśair ghaṭikābhiś ca vitānādyaiś ca bhūṣayet
alaṅkṛto gururviṣṇuṃ dhyātvātmānaṃ prapūjayet
aṅgulīyaprabhṛtibhirmūrtipān valayādibhiḥ
kuṇḍe kuṇḍe sthāpayecca mūrtipāṃstatra pāragān
pūrvādau toraṇārthantu pippaloḍumbarau vaṭaṃ
plakṣaṃ suśobhanaṃ pūrvaṃ subhadrandakṣatoraṇaṃ
pañcahastaṃ tu saṃsthāpya syonāpṛthvīti pūjayet
toraṇastambhamūle tu kalaśānmaṅgalāṅkurān
pradadyādupariṣṭācca kuryāccakraṃ sudarśanaṃ
pañcahastapramāṇantu dhvajaṃ kuryāddvicakṣaṇaḥ
vaipulyaṃ cāsya kurvīta ṣoḍaśāṅgulasanmitaṃ
aruṇogninibhaś caiva kṛṣṇaḥ śuklotha pītakaḥ
raktavarṇas tathā śvetaḥ śvetavarṇādikakramāt
kumudaḥ kumudākṣaś ca puṇḍarīkotha vāmanaḥ
śaṅkukarṇaḥ sarvanetraḥ sumukhaḥ supratiṣṭhitaḥ
pūjyā koṭiguṇair yuktāḥ pūrvādyā dhvajadevatāḥ
jalāḍhakasupūrāstu pakvavimbopamā ghaṭāḥ
aṣṭāviṃśādhikaśataṃ kālamaṇḍanavarjitāḥ
sahiraṇyā vastrakaṇṭhāḥ sodakāstoraṇādvahiḥ
ghaṭāḥ sthāpyāś ca pūrvādau vedikāyāś ca koṇagān
kumbheṣvāvāhya śakrādīn pūrvādau pūjayet kramāt
rakṣāgneyīṃ diśaṃ devaiḥ pūjāṃ gṛha namostu te
nairṛtāgaccha khaḍgāḍhya balavāhanasaṃyuta
idamarghyamidaṃ pādyaṃ rakṣa tvaṃ nairṛtīṃ diśaṃ
makarārūḍha varuṇa pāśahasta mahābala
āgaccha paścimaṃ dvāraṃ rakṣa rakṣa namostu te
uruṃ hi rājā varuṇaṃ yajedarghyādibhirguruḥ
vāta ity ādibhiścārvedonnamo vāyavepi vā
somaṃ rājānamiti vā yajetsomāya vai namaḥ
āgaccheśāna sabala śūlahasta vṛṣasthita
yajñamaṇḍapasyaiśānīṃ diśaṃ rakṣa namostu te
īśānamasyeti yajedīśānāya namopi vā
salokordhvāṃ diśaṃ rakṣa yajñasyāja namostu te
anantāgaccha cakrāḍhya kūrmasthāhigaṇeśvara
kumbhādhivāsavidhiḥ
bhagavānuvāca
bhūmeḥ parigrahaṃ kuryāt kṣipedbrīhīṃś ca sarṣapān
nārasiṃhena rakṣoghnān prokṣoghnān prokṣayet pañcagavyataḥ
bhūmiṃ ghaṭe tu sampūjya saratne sāṅgakaṃ hariṃ
astramantreṇa karakaṃ tatra cāṣṭaśataṃ yajet
acchinnadhārayā siñcan brīhīn saṃskṛtya dhārayet
savastre kalaśe bhūyaḥ pūjayedacyutaṃ śriyaṃ
kuśopari tūlikāñca śayyāyāṃ digvidikṣu ca
vidyādhipān yajedviṣṇuṃ madhughātaṃ trivikramaṃ
vāmanaṃ dikṣu vāyvādau śrīdharañca hṛṣīkapaṃ
padmanābhaṃ dāmodaramaiśānyāṃ snānamaṇḍape
abhyarcya paścādaiśānyāṃ catuṣkumbhe savedike
snānamaṇḍaṣake sarvadravyāṇyānīya nikṣipet
snānakumbheṣu kumbhāṃstāṃś caturdikṣvadhivāsayet
kalaśāḥ sthāpanīyāstu abhiṣekārthamādarāt
vaṭodumbarakāśvatthāṃś campakāśokaśrīdrumān
palāśārjunaplakṣāṃstu kadambavakulāmrakān
padmakaṃ rocanāṃ dūrvāṃ darbhapiñjalameva ca
jātīpuṣpaṃ kundapuṣpacandanaṃ raktacandanaṃ
siddhārthaṃ tagarañcaiva taṇḍulaṃ dakṣiṇe nyaset
nadyāḥ samudragāminyā viśeṣāt jāhnavīmṛdaṃ
gomayañca yavān śālīṃstilāṃś caivāpare nyaset
viṣṇuparṇīṃ śyāmalatāṃ bhṛṅgarājaṃ śatāvarīṃ
sahadevāṃ mahādevīṃ balāṃ vyaghrīṃ salakṣmaṇāṃ
jāhnavīvālukātoyaṃ vinyasedapare ghaṭe
varāhavṛṣanāgendraviṣāṇoddhṛtamṛttikāṃ
nāgakeśarapuṣpañca kāśmīramapare nyaset
nadīnadataḍāgānāṃ salilair aparaṃ nyaset
ekāśītipade cānyānmaṇḍape kalaśān nyaset
gandhodakādyaiḥ sampūrṇān śrīsūktenābhimantrayet
yavaṃ siddhārthakaṃ gandhaṃ kuśāgraṃ cākṣataṃ tathā
padmaṃ śyāmalatāṃ dūrvāṃ viṣṇuparṇīṃ kuśāṃs tathā
pādyārthaṃ dakṣiṇe bhāge madhuparkaṃ tu dakṣiṇe
kakkolakaṃ lavaṅgañca tathā jātīphalaṃ śubhaṃ
uttare hy ācamanāya agnau dūrvākṣatānvitaṃ
pātraṃ nīrājanārthaṃ ca tathodvartanamānile
gandhapuṣpānvitaṃ pātramaiśānyāṃ pātrake nyaset
murāmāṃsī cāmalakaṃ sahadevāṃ niśādikaṃ
ṣaṣṭidīpānnyasedaṣṭau nyasennīrājanāya ca
śaṅkhaṃ cakrañca śrīvatsaṃ kuliśaṃ paṅkajādikaṃ
hemādipātre kṛtvā tu nānāvarṇādipuṣpakaṃ
snānādividhiḥ
bhagavānuvāca
aiśānyāṃ janayet kuṇḍaṃ gururvahniñca vaiṣṇavaṃ
gāyatryaṣṭaśataṃ hutvā sampātavidhinā ghaṭān
prokṣayet kāruśālāyāṃ śilpibhirmūrtipair vrajet
viṣṇave śipiviṣṭeti ūrṇāsūtreṇa sarṣapaiḥ
paṭṭavastreṇa kartavyaṃ deśikasyāpi kautukaṃ
maṇḍape pratimāṃ sthāpya savastrāṃ pūjitān stuvan
namastercye sureśāni praṇīte viśvakarmaṇā
prabhāvitāśeṣajagaddhātri tubhyaṃ namo namaḥ
tvayi sampūjayāmīśe nārāyaṇamanāmayaṃ
evaṃ vijñāpya pratimāṃ nayettāṃ snānamaṇḍapaṃ
agnirjyotīti dṛṣṭiñca dadyādvai bhadrapīṭhake
tataḥ śuklāni puṣpāṇi ghṛtaṃ siddhārthakaṃ tathā
dūrvāṃ kuśāgraṃ devasya dadyācchirasi deśikaḥ
ghṛtenābhyañjayet paścāt paṭhan ghṛtavatīṃ punaḥ
nadījaistīrthajaiḥ snānaṃ pāvamānīti ratnajaiḥ
śanno devīḥ snāpayecca gāyatryāpyuṣṇavāriṇā
yajñāyajñeti kāṣāyaiḥ pañcabhirgavyakaistataḥ
payaḥ pṛthivyāṃ mantreṇa yāḥ phalinī phalāmbubhiḥ
somaṃ rājānamityevaṃ viṣṇo rarāṭaṃ dakṣataḥ
haṃsaḥ śuciḥ paścimena kuryādudvartanaṃ hareḥ
mūrdhānandivamantreṇa dhātrīṃ māṃsīṃ ca ke dadet
yajñabhāgaṃ gṛhāṇemaṃ vāsudeva namostu te
madhuvātā madhuparkaṃ mayi gṛhṇāmi cācamet
kāṇḍānnirmañchanaṃ kuryādgandhaṃ gandhavatīti ca
unnayāmīti mālyañca idaṃ viṣṇuḥ pavitrakaṃ
mahāvratena sakalīpuṣpaṃ cauṣadhayaḥ kṣipet
dhūpaṃ dadyāddhūrasīti vibhrāṭsūktena cāñjanaṃ
yuñjantīti ca tilakaṃ dīrghāyuṣṭveti mālyakaṃ
cāmarantu vikarṇena bhūṣāṃ rathantareṇa ca
vedādyaiḥ saṃstutiṃ kuryāddhareḥ puruṣasūktataḥ
uttiṣṭheti samutthāpya śayyāyā maṇḍape nayet
ato deveti sūktena prātimāṃ piṇḍikāṃ tathā
śrīsūktena ca śayyāyāṃ viṣṇostu śakalīkṛtiḥ
mṛgarājaṃ vṛṣaṃ nāgaṃ vyajanaṃ kalaśaṃ tathā
vaijayantīṃ tathā bherīṃ dīpamityaṣṭamaṅgalaṃ
darśayedaśvasūktena pādadeśe tripāditi
ukhāṃ pidhānakaṃ pātramambikāṃ darvikāṃ dadet
muṣalolūkhalaṃ dadyācchilāṃ sammārjanīṃ tathā
tathā bhojanabhāṇḍāni gṛhopakāraṇāni ca
śirodeśe ca nidrākhyaṃ vastraratnayutaṃ ghaṭaṃ
khaṇḍakhādyaiḥ pūrayitvā snapanasya vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ
bhagavānuvāca
sarvajñaṃ sarvagaṃ dhyātvā ātmānaṃ puruṣottamaṃ
oṃkāreṇa samāyojya cicchaktimabhimāninīṃ
yojayenmarutāṃ pṛthvīṃ vahnivījena dīpayet
saṃharedvāyunā cāgniṃ vāyumākāśato nayet
tanmātrapātrakān kṛtvā saṃharettat kramād budhaḥ
ākāśaṃ manasāhatya manohaṅkaraṇe kuru
ahaṅkārañca mahati tañcāpyavyākṛte nayet
avyākṛtaṃ jñānarūpe vāsudevaḥ sa īritaḥ
sa tāmavyākṛtiṃ māyāmabhyaṣṭa sisṛkṣayā
saṅkarṣaṇaṃ saṃ śabdātmā sparśākhyamasṛjat prabhuḥ
kṣobhya māyāṃ sa pradyumnaṃ tejorūpaṃ sa cāsṛjat
aniruddhaṃ rasamātraṃ brahmāṇaṃ gandharūpakaṃ
tasmin hiraṇmayañcāṇḍaṃ so 'sṛjat pañcabhūtavat
tasmin saṅkrāmite jīve śaktirātmopasaṃhṛtā
prāṇo jīvena saṃyukto vṛttimāniti śabdyate
jīvovyāhṛtisañjñastu prāṇeṣvādhyātmikaḥ smṛtaḥ
prāṇair yuktā tato buddhiḥ sañjātā cāṣṭamūrtikī
arthāḥ prajajñire pañca saṅkalpādiyutāstataḥ
śabdaḥ sparśaś ca rūpañca raso gandha iti smṛtā
jñānaśaktiyutānyetair ārabdhānīndriyāṇi tu
tvakśrotraghrāṇacakṣūṃṣi jihvābuddhīndriyāṇi tu
pādau pāyuḥs tathā pāṇī vāgupasthaś ca pañcamaḥ
karmendriyāṇi caitāni pañcabhūtānyataḥ śṛṇu
ākāśavāyutejāṃsi salilaṃ pṛthivī tathā
sthūlamebhiḥ śarīrantu sarvādhāraṃ prajāyate
eteṣāṃ vācakā mantrā nyāsāyocyanta uttamāḥ
prāṇatattvaṃ bhakārantu jīvopādhigataṃ nyaset
ḍakāraṃ netrayugme tu rasanāyāṃ ṭhakārakaṃ
ṭakāraṃ nāsikāyāntu ñakāraṃ vāci vinyaset
jhakāraṃ karayor nyasya pāṇitattvaṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ
vinyaset pṛthivītattvaṃ ṅakāraṃ pādayugmake
khakāraṃ vāyutattvañca nāsikāyāṃ niveśayet
hṛtpuṇḍarīke vinyasya yakāraṃ sūryadaivataṃ
dvāsaptatisahasrāṇi hṛdayādabhiniḥsṛtāḥ
kalāṣoḍaśasaṃyuktaṃ makāraṃ tatra vinyaset
oṃ āṃ parameṣṭhyātmane āṃ namaḥ puruṣātmane
oṃ vāṃ manonivṛttyātmane nāñca viśvātmane namaḥ
oṃ vaṃ namaḥ sarvātmane ity uktāḥ pañca śaktayaḥ
sthāne tu prathamā yojyā dvitīyā āsane matā
tṛtīyā śayane tadvaccaturthī pānakarmaṇi
pratyarcāyāṃ pañcamī syātpañcopaniṣadaḥ smṛtāḥ
hūṅkāraṃ vinyasenmadhye dhyātvā mantramayaṃ hariṃ
yāṃ mūrtiṃ sthāpayettasmāt mūlamantraṃ nyasettataḥ
śiroghrāṇalalāṭeṣu mukhakaṇṭhahṛdi kramāt
nārāyaṇaṃ nyasedvaktre grīvāyāṃ mādhavaṃ nyaset
madhusūdanakaṃ pṛṣṭhe vāmanaṃ jaṭhare nyaset
kakṣyāntrivikramaṃ nyasya jaṅghāyāṃ śrīdharaṃ nyaset
hṛṣīkeśaṃ dakṣiṇāyāṃ padmanābhaṃ tu gulphake
dāmodaraṃ pādayoś ca hṛdayādiṣaḍaṅgakaṃ
yasyā mūrtestu yannāma tasyādyaṃ cākṣaraṃ ca yat
hṛdayādīni deveśa mūlañca daśamākṣaraṃ
cakrābjamaṇdale viṣṇuṃ yajedgandhādinā tathā
śubhañcakraṃ dvādaśāraṃ hy upariṣṭādvicintayet
pṛṣṭhadeśe tataḥ prājñaḥ prakṛtyādīnniveśayet
pūjayedārakāgreṣu sūryaṃ dvādaśadhā punaḥ
tanmadhye pauruṣīṃ śaktiṃ dhyātvābhyarcya ca diśikaḥ
pratimāyāṃ hariṃ nyasya tatra taṃ pūjayet surān
gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ samyak sāṅgaṃ sāvaraṇaṃ kramāt
dvādaśākṣaravījaistu keśavādīn samarcayet
dvādaśāre maṇḍale tu laukapālādikaṃ kramāt
pauruṣeṇa tu sūktena śriyāḥ sūktena piṇḍikāṃ
jananādikramāt paścājjanayedvaiṣṇavānalaṃ
hutvāgniṃ hutamiti kuṇḍegniṃ praṇayedbudhaḥ
dakṣiṇegniṃ hutamiti kuṇḍegniṃ praṇayedbudhaḥ
agnimagnīti pūrve tu kuṇḍegniṃ praṇayedbudhaḥ
palāśasamidhānāntu aṣṭottarasahasrakaṃ
kuṇḍe kuṇḍe homayecca vrīhīn vedādikais tathā
sājyāṃstilān vyāhṛtibhirmūlamantreṇa vai ghṛtaṃ
dvādaśārṇaiḥ spṛśet pādau nābhiṃ hṛn mastakaṃ tataḥ
spṛṣṭvā śironābhipādāṃś catasraḥ sthāpayennadīḥ
gaṅgā ca yamunā godā kramānnāmnā sarasvatī
dahettu viṣṇugāyatryā gāyatryā śrapayeccaruṃ
sāmādhipānāṃ tuṣṭyarthaṃ hemagāṃ gurave dadet
vāsudevapratiṣṭhādividhiḥ
bhagavānuvāca
piṇḍikāsthāpanārthantu garbhāgāraṃ tu saptadhā
devamanuṣapaiśācabhāgeṣu na kadācana
brahmabhāgaṃ parityajya kiñcidāśritya cāṇḍaja
devamānuṣabhāgābhyāṃ sthāpyā yatnāttu piṇḍikā
napuṃsakakaśilāyāntu ratnanyāsaṃ samācaret
vrīhīn ratnāṃstridhātūṃś ca lohādīṃś candanādikān
ratnanyāsavidhiṃ kṛtvā pratimāmālabhedguruḥ
homārthe khaṇḍilaṃ kuryāt sikatābhiḥ samantataḥ
sārdhahastapramāṇaṃ tu caturasraṃ suśobhanaṃ
aṣṭadikṣu yathānyāsaṃ kalaśānapi vinyaset
pūrvādyānaṣṭavarṇena agnimānīya saṃskṛtaṃ
aṣṭārṇenāṣṭaśatakaṃ ājyaṃ pūrṇāṃ pradāpayet
śāntyudakaṃ āmrapatraiḥ mūlena śatamantritaṃ
siñceddevasya tanmūrdhni śrīś ca te hy anayā ṛcā
tadviṣṇoriti mantreṇa prāsādābhimukhaṃ nayet
śivikāyāṃ hariṃ sthāpya bhrāmayīta purādikaṃ
gītavedādiśabdaiś ca prāsādadvāri dhārayet
strībhirviprair maṅgalāṣṭaghaṭaiḥ saṃsnāpayeddhariṃ
ato deveti vastrādyamaṣṭāṅgārghyaṃ nivedya ca
saṃsthyāpya piṇḍikāyāntu sthiraṃ kuryādvicakṣaṇaḥ
pūjayet sakalīkṛtya sāṅgaṃ sāvaraṇaṃ hariṃ
dhyāyet svaṃ tasya mūrtintu pṛthivī tasya pīṭhikā
jīvamāvāhayiṣyāmi pañcaviṃśatitattvagaṃ
aṅguṣṭhamātraḥ puruṣo dehopādhiṣu saṃsthitaḥ
jyotirjñānaṃ paraṃ brahma ekamevādvitīyakaṃ
sajīvīkaraṇaṃ kṛtvā praṇavena nibodhayet
sānnidhyakaraṇannāma hṛdayaṃ spṛśya vai japet
jñānavijñānarūpāya brahmatejonuyāyine
guṇātikrāntaveśāya puruṣāya mahātmane
akṣayāya purāṇāya viṣṇo sannihito bhava
ātmānaṃ sannidhīkṛtya brahmādiparivārakān
svanāmnā sthāpayedanyānāyudhān svamudrayā
yātrāvarṣādikaṃ dṛṣṭvā jñeyaḥ sannihito hariḥ
natvā stutvā stavādyaiś ca japtvā cāṣṭākṣarādikaṃ
agnimaṇḍapamāsādya garuḍaṃ sthāpya pūjayet
digīśān diśi devāṃś ca sthāpya sampūjya deśikaḥ
viśvaksenaṃ tu saṃsthāpya śaṅkhacakrādi pūjayet
ācāryadakṣiṇārdhantu ṛtvigbhyo dakṣiṇāṃ dadet
anyebhyo dakṣiṇāṃ dadyādbhojayed brāhmaṇāṃstataḥ
avāritān phalān dadyādyajamānāya vai guruḥ
viṣṇuṃ nayet pratiṣṭhātā cātmanā sakalaṃ kulaṃ
sarveṣāmeva devānāmeṣa sādhāraṇo vidhiḥ
mūlamantrāḥ pṛthakteṣāṃ śeṣaṃ kāryaṃ samānakaṃ
dvārapratiṣṭhādhvajārohāṇādividhiḥ
bhagavānuvāca
vakṣe cāvabhṛtasnānaṃ viṣṇor natveti homayet
ekāśītipade kumbhān sthāpya saṃsthāpayeddhariṃ
dvārapratiṣṭhāṃ vakṣyāmi dvārādho hema vai dadet
aṣṭabhiḥ kalaśaiḥ sthāpya śākhodumbarakau guruḥ
kuṇḍeṣu homayedvahniṃ samillājatilādibhiḥ
datvā śayyādikañcādho dadyādādhāraśaktikāṃ
ūrdhvodumbarake devīṃ lakṣmīṃ suragaṇārcitāṃ
nyasyābhyarcya yathānyāyaṃ śrīsūktena caturmukhaṃ
datvā tu śrīphalādīni ācāryādestu dakṣiṇāṃ
pratiṣṭhāsiddhadvārasya tvācāryaḥ sthāpayeddhariṃ
prāsādādasya pratiṣṭhantu hṛtpratiṣṭheti tāṃ śṛṇu
samāptau śukanāśāyā vedyāḥ prāgdarbhamastake
sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ kumbhamathavā śuklanirmitaṃ
aṣṭaratnauṣadhīdhātuvījalauhānvitaṃ śubhaṃ
savastraṃ pūritaṃ cādbhirmaṇḍale cādhivāsayet
sapallavaṃ nṛsiṃhena hutvā sampātasañcitaṃ
nārāyaṇākhyatattvena prāṇabhūtaṃ nyasettataḥ
vairājabhūtāntaṃ dhyāyet prāsādasya sureśvara
tataḥ puruṣavatsarvaṃ prāsādaṃ cintayed budhaḥ
gurvādau dakṣiṇāṃ dadyād brāhmaṇādeś ca bhojanaṃ
tataḥ paścādvedibandhaṃ tadūrdhvaṃ kaṇṭhabandhanaṃ
kaṇṭhopariṣṭāt kartavyaṃ vimalāmalasārakaṃ
tadūrdhvaṃ vṛkalaṃ kuryāccakrañcādyaṃ sudarśanaṃ
mūttiṃ śrīvāsudevasya grahaguptāṃ nivedayet
kalaśaṃ vātha kurvīta tadūrdhvaṃ cakramuttamaṃ
vedyāś ca paritaḥ sthāpyā aṣṭau vighneśvarāstvaja
catvāro vā caturdikṣu sthāpanīyā garutmataḥ
dhvajārohaṃ ca vakṣyāmi yena bhūtādi naśyati
prāsādavimbadravyāṇāṃ yāvantaḥ paramāṇavaḥ
tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi tatkartā viṣṇulokabhāk
kumbhāṇḍavedivimbānāṃ bhramaṇādvāyunānagha
kaṇṭhasyāveṣṭanāj jñeyaṃ phalaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ dhvajāt
patākānāṃ prakṛtiṃ viddhi daṇḍaṃ puruṣarūpiṇaṃ
dhāraṇāddharaṇīṃ viddhi ākāśaṃ śuṣirātmakaṃ
tejastat pāvakaṃ viddhi vāyuṃ sparśagataṃ tathā
pāṣāṇādiṣveva jalaṃ pārthivaṃ pṛthivīguṇaṃ
pratiśabdodbhavaṃ śabdaṃ sparśaṃ syāt karkaśādikaṃ
śuklādikaṃ bhavedrūpaṃ rasamannādidarśanaṃ
dhūpādigandhaṃ gandhantu vāg bheryādiṣu saṃsthitā
śukanāśāśritā nāsā bāhū tadrathakau smṛtau
śirastvaṇḍaṃ nigaditaṃ kalaśaṃ mūrdhajaṃ smṛtaṃ
kaṇṭhaṃ kaṇṭhamiti jñeyaṃ skandhaṃ vedī nigadyete
pāyūpasthe praṇāle tu tvak sudhā parikīrtitā
tacchaktiṃ piṇḍikāṃ viddhi prakṛtiṃ ca tadākṛtiṃ
niś calatvañca garbhosyā adhiṣṭhātā tu keśavaḥ
evameva hariḥ sākṣātprāsādatvena saṃsthitaḥ
jaṅghā tvasya śivo jñeyaḥ skandhe dhātā vyavasthitaḥ
prāsādasya pratiṣṭhāntu dhvajarūpeṇa me śṛṇu
dhvajaṃ kṛtvā surair daityā jitāḥ śastrādicihnitaṃ
aṇḍordhvaṃ kalaśaṃ nyasya tadūrdhvaṃ vinyaseddhvajaṃ
vimbārdhamānaṃ daṇḍasya tribhāgenātha kārayet
aṣṭāraṃ dvādaśāraṃ vā madhye mūrtimatānvitaṃ
nārasiṃhena tārkṣyeṇa dhvajadaṇḍastu nirbraṇaḥ
prāsādasya tu vistāro mānaṃ daṇḍasya kīrtitaṃ
śikharārdhena vā kuryāt tṛtīyārdhena vā punaḥ
dvārasya dairghyād dviguṇaṃ daṇḍaṃ vā parikalpayet
dhvajayaṣṭirdevagṛhe aiśānyāṃ vāyavethavā
kṣaumādyaiś ca dhvajaṃ kuryādvicitraṃ vaikavarṇakaṃ
ghaṇṭācāmarakiṅkiṇyā bhūṣitaṃ pāpanāśanaṃ
daṇḍāgrāddharaṇīṃ yāvaddhastaikaṃ vistareṇa tu
mahādhvajaḥ sarvadaḥ syātturyāṃśāddhīnatorcitaḥ
dhvaje cārdhena vijñeyā patākā mānavarjitā
vistareṇa dhvajaḥ kāryo viṃśadaṅgulasannibhaḥ
adhivāsavidhānena cakraṃ daṇḍaṃ dhvajaṃ tathā
devavat sakalaṃ kṛtvā maṇḍapasnapanādikaṃ
adhivāsayecca vidhinā śayyāyāṃ sthāpya deśikaḥ
tataḥ sahasraśīrṣeti sūktaṃ cakre nyased budhaḥ
manorūpeṇa tasyaiva sajīvakaraṇaṃ smṛtaṃ
areṣu mūrtayo nyasyāḥ keśavādyāḥ surottama
nṛsiṃhaṃ viśvarūpaṃ vā abjamadhye niveśayet
sakalaṃ vinyaseddaṇḍe sūtrātmānaṃ sajīvakaṃ
tacchaktiṃ vyāpinīṃ dhyāyed dhvajarūpāṃ balābalāṃ
maṇḍape sthāpya cābhyarcya homaṃ kuṇḍeṣu kārayet
oṃ kṣoṃ nṛsiṃhāya namaḥ pūjayet sthāpayeddhariṃ
tato dhvajaṃ gṛhītvā tu yajamānaḥ sabāndhavaḥ
śirasyādhāya tat pātraṃ nārāyanamanusmaran
pradakṣiṇaṃ tu kurvīta turyamaṅgalaniḥsvanaiḥ
tato niveśayet daṇḍaṃ mantreṇāṣṭākṣareṇa tu
muñcāmi tveti sūktena dhvajaṃ muñcedvicakṣaṇaḥ
pātraṃ dhvajaṃ kuñjarādi dadyādācāryake dvijaḥ
eṣa sādhāraṇaḥ prokto dhvajasyārohaṇe vidhiḥ
svargatvā dhvajadānāttu rājā balī bhavet
lakṣmīpratiṣṭhāvidhiḥ
bhagavānuvāca
samudāyena devādeḥ pratiṣṭhāṃ pravadāmi te
lakṣmyāḥ pratiṣṭhā prathamaṃ tathā devīgaṇasya ca
pūrvavat sakalaṃ kuryānmaṇḍapasnapanādikaṃ
bhadrapīṭhe śriyaṃ nyasya sthāpayedaṣṭa vai ghaṭān
hiraṇyavarṇā hariṇī netre conmīlayecchriyāḥ
aśvapūrveti pūrveṇa tāṃ kumbhenābhiṣecayet
gandhadvāreti vāyavyāṃ manasaḥ kāmamākṛtim
īśānakalaśenaiva śiraḥ sauvarṇakardamāt
ekāśītighaṭaiḥ snānaṃ mantreṇāpaḥ sṛjan kṣitim
ārdrāṃ puṣkariṇīṃ gandhair ārdrāmityādipuṣpakaiḥ
tanmayāvaha mantreṇa ya ānanda ṛcākhilaṃ
śāyantīyena śayyāyāṃ śrīsūktena ca sannidhim
śrīsūktena maṇḍapetha kuṇḍeṣvabjāni homayet
karavīrāṇi vā hutvā sahasraṃ śatameva vā
gṛhopakaraṇāntādi śrīsūktenaiva cārpayet
tataḥ prāsādasaṃskāraṃ sarvaṃ kṛtvā tu pūrvavat
mantreṇa piṇḍikāṃ kṛtvā pratiṣṭhānaṃ tataḥ śriyaḥ
śrīsūktena ca sānnidhyaṃ pūrvavat pratyṛcaṃ japet
evaṃ devyo 'khilāḥ sthāpyāvāhya svargādi bhāvayet
sudarśanacakrādipratiṣṭhākathanaṃ
bhagavānuvāca
pratiṣṭhā viṣṇuvat kāryā svasvamantreṇa tāṃ śṛṇu
sudarśana mahācakra śānta duṣṭabhayaṅkara
āviśa sarvamantrarūpāṇi sarvamantrajātayaś ca hana hana chinda saṅkṣipa saṅkṣipa sara sara dāraya dāraya sphuṭa sphuṭa sphoṭaya sphoṭaya jvālāmālāsaṅghātamaya sarvato 'nantajvālāvajrāśanicakreṇa sarvapātālān utsādaya utsādaya sarvato 'natajvālāvajraśarapañjareṇa sarvapātālān parivāraya parivāraya sarvapātālāsuravāsināṃ hṛdayānyākarṣaya ākarṣaya śīghraṃ daha daha paca paca matha matha śoṣaya śoṣaya nikṛntaya nikṛntaya tāvadyāvanme vaśamāgatāḥ pātālebhyaḥ phaṭ asurebhyaḥ phaṭ mantrarūpebhyaḥ phaṭ mantrajātibhyaḥ phaṭ saṃśayānmāṃ bhagavannarasiṃharūpa viṣṇo sarvāpadbhyaḥ sarvamantrarūpebhyo rakṣa rakṣa hrūṃ phaṭ namo 'stu te
śrīpuṣṭisaṃyuktaṃ kuryād balena saha bhadrayā
prāsāde sthāpayedviṣṇuṃ gṛhe vā maṇḍape 'pi vā
vāmanaṃ caiva vaikuṇṭhaṃ hayāsyamaniruddhakaṃ
sthāpayejjalaśayyāsthaṃ matsyādīṃścāvatārakān
saṅkarṣaṇaṃ viśvarūpaṃ liṅgaṃ vai rudramūrtikaṃ
ardhanārīśvaraṃ tadvaddhariśaṅkaramātṛkāḥ
bhairavaṃ ca tathā sūryaṃ grahāṃstadvināyakam
gaurīmindrādikāṃ lepyāṃ citrajāṃ ca balābalāṃ
pustakānāṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ ca vakṣye likhanatadvidhiṃ
yajamāno guruṃ vidyāṃ hariṃ lipikṛtaṃ naraṃ
prāṅmukhaḥ padminīṃ dhyāyet likhitvā ślokapañcakaṃ
brāhmaṇān bhojayecchakyā śaktyā dadyācca dakṣiṇāṃ
guruṃ vidyāṃ hariṃ prārcya purāṇādi likhennaraḥ
pūrvavanmaṇḍalādye ca aiśānyāṃ bhadrapīṭhake
darpaṇe pustakaṃ dṛṣṭvā secayet pūrvavad ghaṭaiḥ
netronmīlanakaṃ kṛtvā śayyāyāṃ tu nyasennaraḥ
kṛtvā sajīvīkaraṇaṃ prārcya hutvā caruṃ tataḥ
samprāśya dakṣiṇābhistu gurvādīn bhojayeddvijān
vastrādiveṣṭitaṃ pāṭhādādāvante samarcayet
jagacchāntiñcāvadhārya pustakaṃ vācayennaraḥ
trīṇyāhuratidānāni gāvaḥ pṛthvīṃ sarasvatī
vidyādānaphalaṃ datvā masyantaṃ patrasañcayaṃ
yāvattu patrasaṅkhyānamakṣarāṇāṃ tathānagha
tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi viṣṇuloke mahīyate
pañcarātraṃ purāṇāni bhāratāni dadannaraḥ
kūpādipratiṣṭhākathanaṃ
bhagavānuvāca
kūpavāpītaḍāgānāṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ vacmi tāṃ śṛṇu
agnīṣomamayaṃ viśvaṃ viṣṇurāpastu kāraṇaṃ
haimaṃ raupyaṃ ratnajaṃ vā varuṇaṃ kārayennaraḥ
dvibhujaṃ haṃsapṛṣṭhasthaṃ dakṣiṇenābhayapradaṃ
vāmena nāgapāśaṃ taṃ nadīnāgādisaṃyutaṃ
yāgamaṇḍapamadhye syādvedikā kuṇḍamaṇḍitā
toraṇaṃ vāruṇaṃ kumbhaṃ nyasecca karakānvitaṃ
agnyādhānaṃ cāpyakuṇḍe kṛtvā pūrṇāṃ pradāpayet
varuṇaṃ snānapīṭhe tu ye te śateti saṃspṛśet
ghṛtenābhyañjayet paścānmūlamantreṇa deśikaḥ
śanno devīti prakṣālya śuddhavatyā śivodakaiḥ
audbhijjaṃ cottare sthāpya aiśānyāṃ tīrthasambhavaṃ
alābhe tu nadītoyaṃ yāsāṃ rājeti mantrayet
samudrajyeṣṭhetyabhiṣiñcayedvaruṇaṃ pūrvakumbhataḥ
āpo hi ṣṭhā pañcagavyāddhiraṇyavarṇeti svarṇajāt
āpo asmeti varṣoptyair vyāhṛtyā kūpasambhavaiḥ
varuṇañca taḍāgoptyair varuṇādbhistu vaśyataḥ
āpo devīti girijair ekāśīvighaṭaistataḥ
yadvāraṇyena puṣpādi pradadyādvaruṇāya tu
cāmaraṃ darpaṇaṃ chatraṃ vyajanaṃ vaijayantikāṃ
mūlenottiṣṭhetyutthāpya tāṃ rātrimadhivāsayet
varuṇañceti sānnidhyaṃ yadvāraṇyena pūjayet
sajīvīkaraṇaṃ mūlāt punargandhādinā yajet
maṇḍape pūrvavat prārcya kuṇḍeṣu samidādikaṃ
vyāhṛtyā vātha gāyatryā mūlenāmantrayettathā
sūryāya prajāpataye dyauḥ svāhā cāntarikṣakaḥ
viṣṇuś ca varuṇo dhātā rāyaspoṣo mahendrakaḥ
kuvera īśo 'nanto 'tha brahmā rājā jaleśvaraḥ
daśādikṣu baliṃ dadyāt gandhapuṣpādinārcayet
kṛtvāṣṭau sthaṇḍilān ramyān saikatān deśikottamaḥ
varuṇasyeti mantreṇa sājyamaṣṭaśataṃ tataḥ
caruṃ yavamayaṃ hutvā śāntitoyaṃ samācaret
dhyāyettu varuṇaṃ yuktaṃ gauryā nadanadīgaṇaiḥ
utthāpya nāgapṛṣṭhādyair bhrāmayettaiḥ samaṅgalaiḥ
snātvā dhyāyecca varuṇaṃ sṛṣṭiṃ brahmāṇḍasañjñikāṃ
caturasramathāṣṭāsraṃ vartulaṃ vā pravartitaṃ
ārādhya devatāliṅgaṃ daśahastaṃ tu kūpake
yūpaṃ yajñīyavṛkṣotthaṃ mūle haimaṃ phalaṃ nyaset
vāpyāṃ pañcadaśakaraṃ puṣkariṇyāṃ tu viṃśatikaṃ
taḍāge pañcaviṃśākhyaṃ jalamadhye niveśayet
yāgamaṇḍapāṅgeṇa vā yūpabrasketi mantrataḥ
dakṣiṇāṃ gurave dadyādbhūgohemāmbupātrakaṃ
dvijebhyo dakṣiṇā deyā āgatān bhojayettathā
āpo hi ṣṭheti tisṛbhiḥ śāntitoyaṃ dvijaiḥ kṛtaṃ
tīrthatoyaṃ kṣipet puṇyaṃ gokulañcārpayedvijān
aśvamedhasahasrāṇāṃ sahasraṃ yaḥ samācaret
ekāhaṃ sthāpayettoyaṃ tatpuṇyamayutāyutaṃ
bhagavānuvāca
sabhādisthānaṃ vakṣye tathaiva teṣāṃ pravartanaṃ
bhūmau parīkṣitāyāñca vāstuyāgaṃ samācaret
svecchayā tu sabhāṃ kṛtvā svecchayā sthāpayet surān
catuṣpathe grāmādau ca na śūnye kārayet sabhāṃ
yathā rājñāṃ tathānyeṣāṃ pūrvādyāś ca dhvajādayaḥ
koṇabhujān varjayitvā catuḥśālaṃ tu vartayet
triśālaṃ vā dviśālaṃ vā ekaśālamathāpi vā
āyādhike bhavet pīḍā tasmāt kuryāt samaṃ dvayaṃ
kararāśiṃ samastantu kuryādvasuguṇaṃ guruḥ
saptārciṣā hṛte bhāge gargavidyāvicakṣaṇaḥ
aṣṭadhā bhājite tasmin yaccheṣaṃ sa vyayo gataḥ
athavā kararāśiṃ tu hanyāt saptārciṣā budhaḥ
dhvajo dhūmras tathā siṃhaḥ śvā vṛṣastu kharo gajaḥ
triśālakatrayaṃ śastaṃ udakpūrvavivarjitaṃ
yāmyāṃ paragṛhopetaṃ dviśālaṃ labhyate sadā
yāmye śālaikaśālaṃ tu pratyakśālamathāpi vā
ekaśāladvayaṃ śastaṃ śeṣāstvanye bhayāvahāḥ
catuḥśālaṃ sadā śastaṃ sarvadoṣavivarjitaṃ
devagṛhaṃ devatāyāḥ pratiṣṭhāvidhinā sadā
saṃsthāpya manujānāñca samudāyoktakarmaṇā
prātaḥ sarvauṣadhīsnānaṃ kṛtvā śuciratandritaḥ
satoraṇaṃ svasti vācya dvijān goṣṭhahastakaḥ
gṛhī gṛhaṃ praviśecca daivajñān prārcya saṃviśet
gṛhe puṣṭikaraṃ mantraṃ paṭheccemaṃ samāhitaḥ
oṃ nande nandaya vāśiṣṭhe vasubhiḥ prajayā saha
jaye bhārgavadāyade prajānāṃ vijayāvahe
pūrṇe 'ṅgirasadāyāde pūrṇakāmaṃ kurudhva māṃ
bhadre kāśyapadāyāde kuru bhadrāṃ matiṃ mama
iṣṭake tvaṃ prayaccheṣṭaṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ kārayāmyahaṃ
sādhāraṇapratiṣṭhāvidhānaṃ
bhagavānuvāca
samudāyapratiṣṭhāñca vakṣye sā vāsudevavat
ādityā vasavo rudrāḥ sādhyā viśve 'śvinau tathā
ṛṣayaś ca tathā sarve vakṣye teṣāṃ viśeṣakaṃ
yasya devasya yannāma tasyādyaṃ gṛhya cākṣaraṃ
mātrābhirbhedayitvā tu dīrghāṇyaṅgāni bhedayet
sarveṣāṃ mūlamantreṇa pūjanaṃ sthāpanaṃ tathā
niyamavratakṛcchrāṇāṃ maṭhasaṅkramaveśmanāṃ
māsopavāsaṃ dvādaśyāṃ ity ādisthāpanaṃ vade
śilāṃ pūrṇaghaṭaṃ kāṃsyaṃ sambhāraṃ sthāpayettataḥ
brahmakūrcaṃ samāhṛtya śraped yavamayaṃ caruṃ
kṣīreṇa kapilāyāstu tadviṣṇoriti sādhakaḥ
praṇavenābhighāryaiva darvyā saṅghaṭṭayettataḥ
dyauḥ svāhā brahmaṇe svāhā pṛthivī mahārājakaḥ
evaṃ hutvā carorbhāgān dadyāddigbalimādarāt
samidho 'ṣṭaśataṃ hutvā pālāśāṃścājyahomakaṃ
kuryāt puruṣasūktena irāvatī tilāṣṭakaṃ
hutvā tu brahmaviṣṇvīśadevānāmanuyāyināṃ
grahāṇāmāhutīrhutvā lokeśānāmatho punaḥ
parvatānāṃ nadīnāñca samudrāṇāṃ tathāahutīḥ
hutvā ca vyāhṛtīrdaddyāt sruvapūrṇāhutitrayaṃ
pañcagavyaṃ caruṃ prāśya datvācāryāya dakṣiṇāṃ
tilapātraṃ hemayuktaṃ savastraṃ gāmalaṅkṛtāṃ
prīyatāṃ bhagavān viṣṇurityutsṛjedvrataṃ budhaḥ
māsopavāsāderanyāṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ vacmi pūrṇataḥ
yajñenātoṣya deveśaṃ śrapayedvaiṣṇavaṃ caruṃ
tilataṇḍulanīvāraiḥ śyāmākair athavā yavaiḥ
viṣṇvādīnāṃ māsapānāṃ tadante homayet punaḥ
oṃ viṣṇave svāhā oṃ viṣṇave nibhūyapāya svāhā oṃ viṣṇave śipiviṣṭāya svāhā oṃ narasiṃhāya svāhā oṃ puruṣottamāya svāhā
dvādaśāśvatthasamidho homayedghṛtasamplutāḥ
viṣṇo rarāṭamantreṇa tato dvādaśa cāhutīḥ
idaṃ viṣṇurirāvatī carordvādaśa āhutīḥ
śeṣahomaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā dadyāt pūrṇāhutitrayaṃ
yuñjatetyanuvākantu japtvā prāśīta vai caruṃ
tato māsādhipānāntu viprān dvādaśa bhojayet
gāvaḥ prītiṃ samāyāntu pracarantu praharṣitāḥ
daśahastaṃ prapāarāmamaṭhasaṅkramaṇādiṣu
pūrvoktena vidhānena praviśecca gṛhaṃ gṛhī
dvijebhyo dakṣiṇā deyā yathāśaktyā vicakṣaṇaiḥ
prapādānādvāruṇena saṅkrameṇa vaseddivi
iṣṭakāsetukārī ca goloke mārgakṛdgavāṃ
niyamavratakṛdviṣṇuḥ kṛcchrakṛtsarvapāpahā
gṛhaṃ datvā vasetsvarge yāvadābhūtasamplavaṃ
samudāyapratiṣṭheṣṭā śivādīnāṃ gṛhātmanāṃ
jīrṇoddhāravidhānaṃ
bhagavānuvāca
jīrṇāddhāravidhiṃ vakṣye bhūṣitāṃ snapayedguruḥ
vyaṅgāṃ bhagnāṃ ca śailāḍhyāṃ nyasedanyāṃ ca pūrvavat
saṃhāravidhinā tatra tattvān saṃhṛtya deśikaḥ
dāravīṃ dārayedvahnau śailajāṃ prakṣipejjale
dhātujāṃ ratnajāṃ vāpi agādhe vā jale 'mbudhau
yānamāropya jīrṇāṅgaṃ chādya vastrādinā nayet
vāditraiḥ prakṣipettoye gurave dakṣiṇāṃ dadet
yatpramāṇā ca yaddravyā tanmānāṃ sthāpayeddine
kūpavāpītaḍāgāderjīrṇoddhāre mahāphalaṃ
bhagavānuvāca
tasminnabde caikarātraṃ trirātrañcāṣṭarātrakaṃ
kārakasyānukūle vā yātrāndevasya kārayet
maṅgalāṅkuraropaistu gītanṛtyādivādyakaiḥ
śarāvaghaṭikāpālīstvaṅkurārohaṇe hitāḥ
yavāñchālīṃstilān mudgān godhūmān sitasarṣapān
kulatthamāṣaniṣpāvān kṣālayitvā tu vāpayet
pūrvādau ca baliṃ dadyāt bhraman dīpaiḥ puraṃ niśi
pade pade 'śvamedhasya phalaṃ teṣāṃ na saṃśayaḥ
āgatya devatāgāraṃ devaṃ vijñāpayed guruḥ
tīrthayātrā tu yā deva śvaḥ kartavyā surottama
prarohaghaṭikābhyāntu vedikāṃ bhūṣitāṃ vrajet
kāmyārthāṃ lekhyacitreṣu sthāpya tatrādhivāsayet
vaiṣṇavaiḥ saha kurvīta ghṛtābhyaṅgantu mūlataḥ
ghṛtadhārābhiṣekaṃ vā sakalāṃ śarvarīṃ budhaḥ
darpaṇaṃ darśya nīrājaṃ gītavādyaiś ca maṅgalaṃ
vyajanaṃ pūjanaṃ dīpaṃ gandhapuṣpādibhiryajet
haridrāmudgakāśmīraśuklacūrṇādi mūrdhni
pratimāyāś ca bhaktānāṃ sarvatīrthaphalaṃ dhṛte
nayedgurur nadīrnādaiśchatrādyai rāṣṭrapālikāḥ
vāhanādavatāryainaṃ tasyāṃ vedyānniveśayet
āpo hiṣṭhopaniṣadaiḥ pūjayedarghyamukhyakaiḥ
punardevaṃ samādāya toye kṛtvāghamarṣaṇaṃ
pūjayitvā tadahnā ca prāsādaṃ tu nayettataḥ
snānavidhānaṃ
prāsādasyāgrataḥ kumbhānmaṇḍape maṇḍale nyaset
sahasraṃ vā śataṃ vāpi homayet pūrṇayā saha
snānadravyāṇyathāhṛtya kalaśāṃścāpi vinyaset
adhivāsya sūtrakaṇṭhān dhārayenmaṇḍale ghaṭān
śālicūrṇādināpūrya pūrvādinavakeṣu ca
puṇḍarīkākṣamantreṇa darbhāṃstāṃstu visarjayet
yavavrīhitilāṃś caiva nīvarān śyāmakān kramāt
palāśāśvatthanyagrodhavilvodumbaraśīrṣāṃ
jambūśamīkapitthānāṃ tvakkaṣāyair ghaṭāṣṭakaṃ
gośṛṅganaśvagaṅgāgajendradaśaneṣu ca
tīrthakṣetrakhaleṣvaṣṭau mṛttikāḥ syurghaṭāṣṭake
nāraṅgamatha jambīraṃ kharjūraṃ mṛdvikāṃ kramāt
nārikelaṃ nyaset pūgaṃ dāḍimaṃ panasaṃ phalaṃ
nairṛte navake madhye kṣīrapūrṇaṃ ghaṭaṃ nyaset
kuṅkumaṃ nāgapuṣpañca campakaṃ mālatīṃ kramāt
sahadevīṃ kumārīṃ ca siṃhīṃ vyāghrīṃ tathāmṛtāṃ
viṣṇuparṇīṃ śataśivāṃ vacāṃ divyauṣadhīrnyaset
patramelāṃ tvacaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ bālakaṃ candanadvayaṃ
latāṃ kastūrikāṃ caiva kṛṣṇāgurumanukramāt
siddhadravyāṇi pūrvādau śāntitoyamathaikataḥ
ghanasāraṃ tathā śīrṣaṃ pūrvādau ratnameva ca
gandhādyaiḥ pūjayedvahnau hutvā pūrṇāhutiṃ caret
devaiś ca munibhirbhūpair devaṃ saṃsthāpya ceśvarāḥ
aṣṭottarasahasreṇa ghaṭānāṃ sarvabhāg bhavet
yajñāvabhṛthasnānena pūrṇasaṃsnāpanaṃ kṛtam
gaurīlakṣmīvivāhādi cotsavaṃ snānapūrvakam
vṛkṣādipratiṣṭhākathanaṃ
bhagavānuvāca
pratiṣṭhāṃ pādapānāñca vakṣye 'haṃ bhuktimuktidāṃ
sarvauṣadhyudakair liptān piṣṭātakavibhūṣitān
vṛkṣānmālyair alaṅkṛtya vāsobhirabhiveṣṭayet
sūcyā sauvarṇayā kāryaṃ sarveṣāṃ karṇavedhanam
vṛkṣamadhyādutsṛjedgāṃ tato 'bhiṣekamantrataḥ
ṛgyajuḥsāmamantraiś ca vāruṇair maṅgalai ravaiḥ
tarūṇāṃ yajamānasya kuryuś ca yajamānakaḥ
bhūṣito dakṣiṇāṃ dadyādgobhūbhūṣaṇavastrakaṃ
kṣīreṇa bhojanaṃ dadyādyāvaddinacatuṣṭayaṃ
ācārye dviguṇaṃ dadyāt pūrvavan maṇḍapādikam
pāpanāśaḥ parā siddhirvṛkṣārāmapratiṣṭhayā
skandāyeśo yathā prāha pratiṣṭhādyaṃ tathā śṛṇu
sūryeśagaṇaśaktyādeḥ parivārasya vai hareḥ
gaṇeśapūjāvidhiḥ
aiśvara uvāca
gaṇapūjāṃ pravakṣyāmi nirvighnāmakhilārthadāṃ
gaṇāya svāhā hṛdayamekadaṃṣṭrāya vai śiraḥ
padmakarṇikavījāṃś ca jvālinīṃ nandayārcayet
sūryeśā kāmarūpā ca udayā kāmavartinī
satyāṃ ca vighnanāśā ca āsanaṃ gandhamṛttikā
yaṃ śoṣā raṃ ca dahanaṃ plavo laṃ vaṃ tathāmṛtam
gaṇapatirgaṇādhipo gaṇeśo gaṇanāyakaḥ
gaṇakrīḍo vakratuṇḍa ekadaṃṣṭro mahodaraḥ
dhūmravarṇā mahendrādyāḥ pūjyā gaṇapateḥ smṛtāḥ
snānaviśeṣādikathanaṃ
īśvara uvāca
vakṣyāmi skanda nityādyaṃ snānaṃ pūjāṃ pratiṣṭhayā
khātvāsinā samuddhṛtya mṛdamaṣṭāṅgulāṃ tataḥ
śirasā payasastīre nidhāyāstreṇa śodhayet
tṛṇāni śikhayoddhṛtya varmaṇā vibhajettridhā
ekayā nābhipādāntaṃ prakṣālya punaranyayā
niruddhākṣāṇi pāṇibhyāṃ prāṇān saṃyamya vāriṇi
nimajyāsīta hṛdyastraṃ smaran kālānalaprabhaṃ
sārasvatāditīrthānāṃ ekamaṅkuśamudrayā
hṛdākṛṣya tathā snāpya punaḥ saṃhāramudrayā
śeṣaṃ mṛdbhāgamādāya praviśya nābhivāriṇi
vāmapāṇitale kuryādbhāgatrayamudaṅmukhaḥ
aṅgair dakṣiṇamekādyaṃ pūrvamastreṇa saptadhā
śivena daśadhā saumyaṃ japedbhāgatrayaṃ kramāt
sarvadikṣu kṣipet pūrvaṃ hūṃ phaḍantaśarātmanā
sarvāṅgamaṅgajaptena mūrdhādicaraṇāvadhi
dakṣiṇena samālabhya paṭhannaṅgacatuṣṭayam
vauṣaḍantaṣaḍaṅgena ke kuryādabhiṣecanaṃ
kumbhamātreṇa rakṣārthaṃ pūrvādau nikṣipejjalaṃ
snātvā rajopacāreṇa sugandhāmalakādibhiḥ
snātvā cottīrya tattīrthaṃ saṃhāriṇyopasaṃharet
śirastaḥ pādaparyantaṃ hrūṃ phaḍantaśarātmanā
tena kṛtvā malasnānaṃ vidhisnānaṃ samācaret
īśatatpuruṣāghoraguhyakājātasañcaraiḥ
sandhyātraye niśīthe ca varṣāpūrvāvasānayoḥ
suptvā bhuktvā payaḥ pītvā kṛtvā cāvaśyakādikam
strīpunnapuṃsakaṃ śūdraṃ viḍālaśaśamūṣikam
snānamāgneyakaṃ spṛṣṭvā śucā vuddhūlakaṃ caret
sūryāṃśuvarṣasamparkaiḥ prāṅmukhenordhvabāhunā
māhendraṃ snānamaiśena kāryaṃ saptapadāvadhi
pāvanaṃ navamantreṇa snānantadvarmaṇāthavā
manasā mūlamantreṇa prāṇāyāmapuraḥsaram
vaiṣṇavādau ca tanmantrair evaṃ snānādi kārayet
saṃvīkṣya triḥ pivedambu brahmatīrthena śaṅkaraiḥ
svadhāntair ātmatattvādyaistataḥ khāni spṛśeddhṛdā
śakalīkaraṇaṃ kṛtvā prāṇāyāmena saṃsthitaḥ
triḥ samāvartayen mantrī manasā śivasaṃhitāṃ
ācamya nyasya sandhyāñca brāhmīṃ prātaḥ smarennaraḥ
haṃsapadmāsanāṃ raktāṃ caturvaktrāṃ caturbhujāṃ
praskandamālinīṃ dakṣe vāme daṇḍakamaṇḍaluṃ
tārkṣyapadmāsanāṃ dhyāyenmadhyāhne vaiṣṇavīṃ sitāṃ
śaṅkhacakradharāṃ vāme dakṣiṇe sagadābhayaṃ
raudrīṃ dhyāyed vṛṣābjasthāṃ trinetrāṃ śaśibhūṣitāṃ
triśūlākṣadharāṃ dakṣe vāme sābhayaśaktikāṃ
sākṣiṇīṃ karmaṇāṃ sandhyāṃ ātmānaṃ tatprabhānugaṃ
caturthī jñāninaḥ sandhyā niśīthādau vibhāvyate
paitryaṃ mūle pradeśinyāḥ kaniṣṭhāyāḥ prajāpateḥ
brāhmyamaṅguṣṭhamūlasthaṃ tīrthaṃ daivaṃ karāgrataḥ
ṛṣīṇāṃ tu samagreṣu aṅgulīparvasandhiṣu
tataḥ śivātmakair mantraiḥ kṛtvā tīrthaṃ śivātmakaṃ
vāmapāṇipatattoyayojanaṃ savyapāṇinā
uttamāṅge kramānmantrair mārjanaṃ samudāhṛtaṃ
nītvā tadupanāsāgraṃ dakṣapāṇipuṭasthitaṃ
bodharūpaṃ sitaṃ toyaṃ vāmamākṛṣya stambhayet
tatpāpaṃ kajjalābhāsampiṅgayāricya muṣṭinā
kṣipedvajraśilāyāntu tadbhavedaghamarṣaṇaṃ
svāhāntaśivamantreṇa kuśapuṣpākṣatānvitaṃ
śivāyārghyāñjalindatvā gāyatrīṃ śaktito japet
tarpayeddhauṃ śivāyeti svāhānyān svāhayā yutān
hrāṃ hṛdyāya hrīṃ śirase hrūṃ śikhāyai hraiṃ kavacāya
astrāyāṣṭau devagaṇān hṛdādityebhya eva ca
bhṛgubhyo hāmaṅgirobhya ṛṣīn kaṇṭhopavītyatha
kṛtave bhāradvajāya viśvāmitrāya vai namaḥ
pracetase manuṣyāṃś ca sanakāya vaṣaṭ tathā
hāṃ sanandāya vaṣaṭ sanātanāya vai vaṣaṭ
sanatkumārāya vaṣaṭ kapilāya tathā vaṣaṭ
dakṣaskandhopavītī ca kuśamūlāgratastilaiḥ
kavyabālānalāyātha somāya ca yamāya ca
aryamṇe cāgnisomāya varhiṣadbhyaḥ svadhāyutān
ājyapāya ca somāya viśeṣasuravat pitṝn
oṃ hāṃ īśānāya pitre svadhā dadyāt pitāmahe
śāntaprapitāmahāya tathāpretapitṝṃs tathā
hāṃ mātāmahebhyaḥ svadhā hāṃ pramātāmahebhyaś ca
diśāṃ dikpatisiddhānāṃ mātṝṇāṃ graharakṣasāṃ
sūryapūjāvidhiḥ
īśvara uvāca
vakṣye sūryārcanaṃ skanda karāṅganyāsapūrvakaṃ
pūrayedraktavarṇena lalāṭākṛṣṭavindunā
taṃ saṃpūjya raveraṅgaiḥ kṛtvā rakṣāvaguṇṭhanaṃ
oṃ aṃ hṛdvījādi sarvatra pūjanaṃ daṇḍipiṅgalau
dvāri dakṣe vāmapārśve īśāne aṃ gaṇāya ca
agnau guruṃ pīṭhamadhye prabhūtaṃ cāsanaṃ yajet
agnyādau vimalaṃ sāramārādhyaṃ paramaṃ sukhaṃ
padmamadhye rāṃ ca dīptāṃ rīṃ sūkṣmāṃ raṃ jayāṃ kramāt
rūṃ bhadrāṃ reṃ vibhūtīś ca vimalāṃ raimamoghayā
roṃ rauṃ vidyutā śaktiṃ pūrvādyāḥ sarvatomukhāḥ
raṃ madhye arkāsanaṃ syāt sūryamūrtiṃ ṣaḍakṣaraṃ
oṃ haṃ khaṃ kholkayeti yajedāvāhya bhāskaraṃ
lalāṭākṛṣṭamañjalyāṃ dhyātvā raktaṃ nyasedraviṃ
hrāṃ hrīṃ saḥ sūryāya namo mudrayāvāhanādikaṃ
padmamudrāṃ bilvamudrāṃ pradarśyāgnau hṛdīritaṃ
oṃ āṃ hṛdayāya namaḥ arkāya śirase tathā
bhūrbhuvaḥ svaḥ sureśāya śikhāyai nairṛte yajet
huṃ kavacāya vāyavye hāṃ netrāyeti madhyataḥ
vaḥ astrāyeti pūrvādau tato mudrāḥ pradarśayet
dhenumudrā hṛdādīnāṃ goviṣāṇā ca netrayoḥ
astrasya trāsanī yojyā grahaṇāṃ ca namaskriyā
soṃ somaṃ buṃ budhaṃ vṛñca jīvaṃ bhaṃ bhārgavaṃ yajet
dale pūrvādike 'gnyādau aṃ bhaumaṃ śaṃ śanaiś caraṃ
mūlaṃ japtvārghyapātrāmbu datvā sūryāya saṃstutiḥ
natvā parāṅmukhañcārkaṃ kṣamasveti tato vadet
śarāṇunā phaḍantena samāhatyāṇusaṃhṛtiṃ
hṛtpadme śivasūryetisaṃhāriṇyopasaṃskṛtiṃ
śivapūjākathanaṃ
īśvara uvāca
śivapūjāṃ pravakṣyāmi ācamya praṇavārghyavān
dvāramastrāmbunā prokṣya homādidvārapānyajet
gaṇaṃ sarasvatīṃ lakṣmīmūrdhvodumbarake yajet
mahākālaṃ ca yamunāṃ divyadṛṣṭinipātitaḥ
utsārya divyān vighnāṃś ca puṣpākṣepāntarikṣagān
dakṣapārṣṇitribhirghātaibhūmiṣṭhānyāgamandiraṃ
dehalīṃ laṅghayedvāmaśākhāmāśritya vai viśet
nirīkṣaṇādibhiḥ śastraiḥ śuddhānādāya gaḍḍukān
labdhānujñaḥ śivānmaunī gaṅgādikamanuvrajet
pavitrāṅgaḥ prajaptena vastrapūtena vāriṇā
pūrayedambudhau tāṃstān gayatryā hṛdayena vā
sannidhīkṛtya pūjārthaṃ bhūtaśuddhādi kārayet
saṃhāramudrayādāya mūrdhni mantreṇa dhārayet
hṛdambuje nijātmānaṃ dvādaśāntapade 'thavā
śodhayet pañcabhūtāni sañcintya śuṣirantanau
caraṇāṅguṣṭhayoryugmān śuṣirāntarvahiḥ smaret
śaktiṃ hṛdvyāpinīṃ paścāddhūṅkāre pāvakaprabhe
granthīnnirbhidya hūṅkāraṃ mūrdhni vinyasya jīvanaṃ
sampuṭaṃ hṛdayenātha pūrakāhitacetanaṃ
pārthivaṃ maṇḍalaṃ pītaṃ kaṭhinaṃ vajralāñchitaṃ
hrīmityanena vījena pratiṣṭhārūpatāṃ gataṃ
saṃyuktaṃ rāmamantreṇa puruṣāntamakāraṇaṃ
āgneyaṃ maṇḍalaṃ tryastraṃ raktaṃ svastikalāñchitaṃ
ṣaḍasraṃ maṇḍalaṃ vāyorvindubhiḥ ṣaḍbhiraṅkitaṃ
kṛṣṇaṃ hremiti vījena jātaṃ śāntikalāmayaṃ
nabhovindumayaṃ vṛttaṃ vinduśaktivibhūṣitaṃ
vyomākāraṃ suvṛttañca śuddhasphaṭikanirmalaṃ
hauṅkāreṇa phaḍantena śāntyatītakalāmayaṃ
āpyāyayettataḥ sarvaṃ mūlenāmṛtavarṣiṇā
ādhārākhyāmanantañca dharmajñānādipaṅkajaṃ
hṛdāsanamidaṃ dhyātvā mūrtimāvāhayettataḥ
sṛṣṭyā śivamayaṃ tasyāmātmānaṃ dvādaśāntataḥ
atha tāṃ śaktimantreṇa vauṣaḍantena sarvataḥ
divyāmṛtena samplāvya kurvīta sakalīkṛtaṃ
hṛdayādikarānteṣu kaniṣṭhādyaṅgulīṣu ca
hṛdādimantravinyāsaḥ sakalīkaraṇaṃ mataṃ
astreṇa rakṣya prākāraṃ tanmantreṇātha tadvahiḥ
śaktijālamadhaścordhvaṃ mahāmudrāṃ pradarśayet
āpadamastakaṃ yāvad bhāvapuṣpaiḥ śivaṃ hṛdi
padme yajet pūrakeṇa ākṛṣṭāmṛtasadghṛtaiḥ
śivamantrair nābhikuṇḍe tarpayeta śivānalaṃ
ekaṃ svarṇādipātrāṇāṃ pātramastrāmbuśodhitaṃ
vinduprasūtapīyūṣarūpatoyākṣatādinā
hṛdāpūrya ṣaḍaṅgena pūjayitvābhimantrayet
racayitvārghyamaṣṭāṅgaṃ secayeddhenumudrayā
abhiṣiñcedathātmānaṃ mūrdhni tattoyavindunā
tatrasthaṃ yāgasambhāraṃ prokṣayedastravāriṇā
abhimantrya hṛdā piṇḍaistanutrāṇena veṣṭayet
darśayitvāmṛtāṃ mudrāṃ puṣpaṃ datvā nijāsane
āvaśyake jape dhīraḥ sadā vācaṃyamo bhavet
nādāntoccāraṇānmantraṃ śodhayitvā susaṃskṛtaṃ
brahmapañcakamāvartya mālyamādāya liṅgataḥ
aiśānyāndiśi caṇḍāya hṛdayena nivedayet
prakṣālya piṇdikāliṅge astratoye tato hṛdā
arghyapātrāmbunā siñcediti liṅgaviśodhanaṃ
ādhāraśaktimaṅkuranibhāṃ kūrmaśilāsthitāṃ
yajed brahmaśilārūḍhaṃ śivasyānantamāsanaṃ
vicitrakeśaprakhyānamanyonyaṃ pṛṣṭadarśinaḥ
kṛtatretādirūpeṇa śivasyāsanapādukāṃ
dharmaṃ jñānañca vairāgyamaiśvaryañcāgnidiṅmukhān
kūrpārakuṅkumasvarṇakajjalābhān yajet kramāt
varadābhayahastāś ca śaktayo dhṛtacāmarāḥ
vāmā jyeṣṭhā ca raudrī ca kālī kalavikāriṇī
hāṃ sarvabhūtadamanī keśarāgre manonmanī
nyaset siṃhāsane devaṃ śuklaṃ pañcamukhaṃ vibhuṃ
daśabāhuṃ ca khaṇḍenduṃ dadhānandakṣiṇaiḥ karaiḥ
śaktyṛṣṭiśūlakhaṭvāṅgavaradaṃ vāmakaiḥ karaiḥ
ḍamaruṃ vījapurañca nīlābjaṃ sūtrakotpalaṃ
dvātriṃśallakṣaṇopetāṃ śaivīṃ mūrtintu madhyataḥ
hāṃ haṃ hāṃ śivamūrtaye svaprakāśaṃ śivaṃ smaran
brahmādikāraṇatyāgānmantraṃ nītvā śivāspadaṃ
ṣaḍaṅgena samākīrṇaṃ vindurūpaṃ paraṃ śivaṃ
puṣpāñjaligataṃ dhyātvā lakṣmīmūrtau niveśayet
oṃ hāṃ hauṃ śivāya nama āvāhanyā hṛddā tataḥ
āvāhya sthāpya sthāpanyā sannidhāyāntikaṃ śivaṃ
nirodhayenniṣṭhurayā kālakāntyā phaḍantataḥ
vighnānutsārya viṣṭhyātha liṅgamudrāṃ namaskṛtiṃ
hṛdāvaguṇṭhayet paścādāvāhaḥ sammukhī tataḥ
niveśanaṃ sthāpanaṃ syātsannidhānaṃ tavāsmi bhoḥ
ākarmakāṇḍaparyantaṃ sannedheyoparikṣayaḥ
sakalīkaraṇaṃ kṛtvā mantraiḥ ṣaḍbhirathaikatāṃ
aṅgānāmaṅginā sārdhaṃ vidadhyādamṛtīkṛtaṃ
cicchaktihṛdayaṃ śambhoḥ śiva aiśvaryamaṣṭadhā
śikhāvaśitvaṃ cābhedyaṃ tejaḥ kavacamaiśvaraṃ
pratāpo duḥsahaścāstramantarāyāpahārakaṃ
namaḥ svadhā ca svāhā ca vauṣaṭ ceti yathākramaṃ
pādyaṃ pādāmbujadvandve vaktreṣvācamanīyakaṃ
arghyaṃ śirasi devasya dūrvāpuṣpākṣatāni ca
evaṃ saṃskṛtya saṃskārair daśabhiḥ parameśvaraṃ
arghyodavindupuṣpādyair gaḍḍūkaiḥ snāpayecchanaiḥ
īśādimantritardravyair arcya teṣāṃ viparyayaḥ
virūkṣya yavacūrṇena yatheṣṭaṃ śītalair jalaiḥ
svaśaktyā gandhatoyena saṃsnāpya śucivāsasā
na śūnyamastakaṃ liṅgaṃ puṣpaiḥ kuryāttato dadet
candanādyaiḥ samālabhya puṣpaiḥ prārcya śivāṇunā
dhūpabhājanamastreṇa prokṣyābhyarcya śivāṇunā
astreṇa pūjitāṃ ghaṇṭāṃ cādāya guggulaṃ dadet
dadyādācamanaṃ paścāt svadhāntaṃ hṛdayāṇunā
ārātrikaṃ samuttārya tathaivācāmayet punaḥ
praṇamyādāya devājñāṃ bhogāṅgāni prapūjayet
hṛdagnau candrabhaṃ caiśe śivaṃ cāmīkaraprabhaṃ
śikhāṃ raktāñca nairṛtye kṛṣṇaṃ varma ca vāyave
daṃṣṭrākarālamapyastraṃ pūrvādau vajrasannibhaṃ
mūle hauṃ śivāya namaḥ oṃ hāṃ hūṃ hīṃ hoṃ śiraś ca
hṛṃ śikhāyai haiṃ varma haścāstraṃ parivārayutāya ca
śivāya dadyāt pādyañca ācāmañcārghyameva ca
gandhaṃ puṣpaṃ dhūpadīpaṃ naivedyācamanīyakaṃ
karodvartanatāmbūlaṃ mukhavāsañca darpaṇaṃ
mūlamaṣṭaśataṃ japtvā hṛdayenābhimantritaṃ
carmaṇāveṣṭitaṃ khaḍgaṃ rakṣitaṃ kuśapuṣpakaiḥ
akṣatair mudrāyā yuktaṃ śivamudbhavasañjñayā
guhyātiguhyaguptyarthaṃ gṛhāṇāsmatkṛtaṃ japaṃ
bhogī ślokaṃ paṭhitvādyaṃ dakṣahastena śambhave
tanme śivapadasthasya hūṃ kṣaḥ kṣepaya śaṅkara
śivo dātā śivo bhoktā śivaḥ sarvamidaṃ jagat
śivāṅgānāṃ daśāṃśañca datvārghyaṃ stutimācaret
pradakṣiṇīkṛtya nameccāṣṭāṅgañcāṣṭamūrtaye
agnisthāpanādividhiḥ
īśvara uvāca
arghapātrakaro yāyādagnyāgāraṃ susaṃvṛtaḥ
yāgopakaraṇaṃ sarvaṃ divyadṛṣṭyā ca kalpayet
udaṅmukhaḥ kuṇḍamīkṣet praokṣaṇaṃ tāḍanaṃ kuśaiḥ
vidadhyādastramantreṇa varmaṇābhyukṣaṇaṃ mataṃ
khaḍgena khātamuddhāraṃ pūraṇaṃ samatāmapi
kurvīta varmaṇā sekaṃ kuṭṭanantu śarātmanā
sammārjanaṃ samālepaṃ kalārūpaprakalpanaṃ
trisūtrīparidhānaṃ ca varmaṇābhyarcanaṃ sadā
rekhātrayamudak kuryādekāṃ pūrvānanāmadhaḥ
kuśena ca śivāstreṇa yadvā tāsāṃ viparyayaḥ
vajrīkaraṇamantreṇa hṛdā darbhaiś catuṣpathaṃ
akṣapātrantatanutreṇa vinyasedviṣṭaraṃ hṛdā
hṛdā vāgīśvarīṃ tatra īśāmāvāhya pūjayet
vahniṃ sadāśrayānītaṃ śuddhapātroparisthitaṃ
kravyādāṃśaṃ parityajya vīkṣaṇādiviśodhitaṃ
audaryaṃ caindavaṃ bhautaṃ ekīkṛtyānalatrayaṃ
saṃhitāmantritaṃ vahniṃ dhenumudrāmṛtīkṛtaṃ
rakṣitaṃ hetimantreṇa kavacenāvaguṇṭhitaṃ
pūjitantriḥ paribhrāmya kuṇḍasyordhvaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ
śivavījamiti dhyātvā vāgīśāgarbhagocare
vāgīśvareṇa devena kṣipyamānaṃ vibhāvayet
bhūmiṣṭhajānukko mantrī hṛdātmasammukhaṃ kṣipet
sambhṛtiṃ paridhānasya śaucamācamanaṃ hṛdā
garbhāgneḥ pūjanaṃ kṛtvā tadrakṣārthaṃ śarāṇunā
badhnīyādgarbhajaṃ devyāḥ kakaṅkaṇaṃ pāṇipallave
garbhādhānāya sampūjya sadyojātena pāvakaṃ
puṃsavanāya vāmena tṛtīye yāsi pūjayet
āhutitritayaṃ dadyācchirasāmbukaṇānvitaṃ
sīmantonnayanaṃ ṣaṣṭhe māsi sampūjya rūpiṇā
juhuyādāhutīstisraḥ śikhayā śikhayaiva tu
vaktrāṅgakalpanāṃ kuryādvaktrodghāṭananiṣkṛtī
jātakarmanṛkarmabhyāṃ daśame māsi pūrvavat
vahniṃ sandhukṣya darbhādyaiḥ snānaṃ garbhamalāpahaṃ
suvarṇabandhanaṃ devyā kṛtaṃ dhyātvā hṛdārcayet
sadyaḥsūtakanāśāya prokṣayedastravāriṇā
astreṇottarapūrvāgrānmekhalāsu vahiḥ kuśān
āsthāpya sthāpayetteṣu hṛdā paridhivistaraṃ
samidhiḥ pañca hotavyāḥ prānte mūle ghṛtaplutāḥ
brahmāṇaṃ śaṅkaraṃ viṣṇumanantañca hṛdārcayet
indrādīśānaparyantāntānviṣṭarasthānanukramāt
nivārya vighnasaṅghātaṃ vālakaṃ pālayiṣyatha
śaivīmājñābhimānteṣāṃ śrāvayettadanantaraṃ
gṛhītvā sruksruvāvūrdhvavadanādhomukhaiḥ kramāt
pratāpyāgnau tridhā darbhamūlamadhyāgrakaiḥ spṛśet
kuśaspṛṣṭapradeśe tu ātmavidyāśivātmakaṃ
kramāttattvatrayaṃ nyasya hāṃ hīṃ hūṃ saṃ ravaiḥ kramāt
sruvi śaktiṃ sruve śambhuṃ vinyasya hṛdayāṇunā
trisūtrīveṣṭitagrīvo pūjitau kusumādibhiḥ
kuśānāmupariṣṭāttau sthāpayitvā svadakṣiṇe
gavyamājyaṃ samādāya vīkṣaṇādiviśodhitaṃ
svakāṃ brahmamayīṃ mūrtiṃ sañcintyādāya tadghṛtaṃ
punarviṣṇumayīṃ dhyātvā ghṛtamīśānagocare
dhṛtvādāya kuśāgreṇa svāhāntaṃ śirasāṇunā
bhāvayannijamātmānaṃ nābhau dhṛtvāplavettataḥ
prādeśamātradarbhābhyāmaṅguṣṭānāmikāgrakaiḥ
dhṛtābhyāṃ sammukhaṃ vahnerastreṇāplavamācaret
kṣiptvā ghṛte kṛtagranthikuśaṃ prādeśasammitaṃ
pakṣadvayamiḍādīnāṃ trayaṃ cājye vibhāvayet
krāmādbhāgatrayādājyaṃ sruveṇādāya homayet
svetyagnau hā ghṛte bhāgaṃ śeṣamājyaṃ kṣipet kramāt
oṃ hāṃ agnaye svāhā oṃ hāṃ somāya svāhā oṃ hāṃ agnīṣomābhyāṃ svāhā
udghāṭanāya netrāṇāṃ agnernetratraye mukhe
sruveṇa ghṛtapūrṇena caturthīmāhutiṃ yajet
oṃ hāṃ agnaye sviṣṭakṛte svāhā
avaguṇṭhya tanutreṇa rakṣedājyaṃ śarāṇunā
hṛdājyavinduvikṣepāt kuryādabhyukṣya śodhanaṃ
vaktrābhighārasandhānāṃ vaktraikīkaraṇaṃ tathā
oṃ hāṃ sadyojātāya svāhā oṃ hāṃ vāmadevāya svāhā oṃ hāṃ
aghorāya svāhā oṃ tatpuruṣāya svāhā oṃ hāṃ īśānāya svāhā
ityekaikaghṛtāhutyā kuryādvaktrābhighārakaṃ
auṃ hāṃ sadyojātavāmadevābhyāṃ svāhā oṃ hāṃ vāmadevāghorābhyāṃ svāhā oṃ hāṃ aghoratatpuruṣābhyāṃ svāhā oṃ hāṃ tatpuruṣeśānābhyāṃ svāhā
agrito gatayā vāyuṃ nirṛtādiśivāntayā
vaktrāṇāmekatāṃ kuryāt sruveṇa ghṛtaghārayā
oṃ hāṃ sadyojātavāmadevāghoratatpuruṣeśānebhyaḥ svāhā
itīṣṭavaktre vaktrāṇāmantarbhāvastadākṛtiḥ
kuryāt sarvātmanā nāma śivāgnistvaṃ hutāśana
hṛdārcitau visṛṣṭāgnau pitarau vidhipūraṇīṃ
mūlena vauṣaḍantena dadyāt pūrṇāṃ yathāvidhi
tato hṛdambuje sāṅgaṃ sasenaṃ bhāsuraṃ paraṃ
yajet pūrvavadāvāhya prārthyājñāntarpayecchivaṃ
yāgāgniśivayoḥ kṛtvā nāḍīsandhānamātmanā
śaktyā mūlāṇunā homaṃ kuryādaṅgair daśāṃśataḥ
ghṛtasya kārṣiko homaḥ kṣīrasya madhunas tathā
śaktimātrāhutirdadhnaḥ prasṛtiḥ pāyasyatu
yathāvat sarvabhakṣāṇāṃ lājānāṃ muṣṭisammitaṃ
khaṇḍatrayantu mūlānāṃ kalānāṃ svapramāṇataḥ
grāsārdhamātramannānāṃ sūkṣmāṇi pañca homayet
ikṣorāparvikaṃ mānaṃ latānāmaṅguladvayaṃ
puṣpaṃ patraṃ svamānena samidhāṃ tu daśāṅgulaṃ
candracandanakāśmīrakastūrīyakṣakardamān
kandānāmaṣṭamaṃ bhāgaṃ juhuyādvidhivat paraṃ
ghṛtena sruci pūrṇāyāṃ nidhāyādhomukhaṃ sruvaṃ
srugagre puṣpamāropya paścādvāmena pāṇinā
brahmādikāraṇātyāgādviniḥsṛtya suṣumṇayā
mūlamantramavispaṣṭaṃ vauṣaḍantaṃ samuccaret
ācāmaṃ candanaṃ datvā tāmbūlaprabhṛtīnapi
bhaktyā tadbhūtimāvandya vidadhyātpraṇatiṃ parāṃ
bhāsurān paridhīstāṃś ca pūrakeṇa hṛdāṇunā
sarvapākāgramādāya kṛtvā maṇḍalakadvayaṃ
oṃ hāṃ rudrebhyaḥ svāhā pūrve mātṛbhyo dakṣiṇe tathā
vāruṇe hāṃ gaṇebhyaś ca svāhā tebhyastvayaṃ baliḥ
uttare hāñca yakṣebhya īśāne hāṃ grahebhya
hāṃ rāśibhyaḥ svāhā vahnau viśvebhyo nairṛte yathā
vāruṇyāṃ kṣetrapālāya antarbalirudāhṛtaḥ
dvitīye maṇḍale vāhye indyāyāgniyamāya ca
nairṛtāya jaleśāya vāyave dhanarakṣiṇe
īśānāya ca pūrvādau hīśāne brahmaṇe namaḥ
nairṛte viṣṇave svāhā vāyasādervahirbaliḥ
caṇdapūjākathanaṃ
īśvara uvāca
tataḥ śivāntikaṅgatvā pūjāhomādikaṃ mama
nārācamudrayāstreṇa phaḍantenātmasañcayaṃ
saṃhṛtya divyayā liṅgaṃ mūrtimantreṇa yojayet
oṃ caṇḍeśānāya namo madhyataś caṇḍamūrtaye
oṃ dhūlicaṇḍeśvarāya hūṃ phaṭ svāhā tamāhṇayet
caṇḍahṛdayāya hūṃ phaṭ oṃ caṇḍaśirase tathā
oṃ caṇḍaśikhāyai hūṃ phaṭ caṇḍāyuḥ kavacāya ca
caṇḍastrāya tathā hūṃ phaṭ caṇḍaṃ rudrāgnijaṃ smaret
śūlaṭaṅkadharaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ sākṣasūtrakaṇḍaluṃ
yathāśakti japaṃ kuryādaṅgānāntu daśāṃśataḥ
gobhūhiraṇyavastrādimaṇihemādibhūṣaṇaṃ
vihāya śesanirmālyaṃ caṇḍeśāya nivedayet
lehyacoṣyādyanuvaraṃ tāmbūlaṃ sragvilepanaṃ
nirmālyaṃ bhojanaṃ tubhyaṃ pradattantu śivājñayā
sarvametat kriyākāṇḍaṃ mayā caṇḍa tavājñayā
nyūnādhikaṃ kṛtaṃ mohāt paripūrṇaṃ sadāstu me
saṃhāramūrtimantreṇa śanaiḥ saṃhāramudrayā
nirmālyāpanayasthānaṃ limpedgomayavāriṇā
prokṣyārghyādi visṛjyātha ācānto 'nyatsamācaret
kapilādipūjāvidhanaṃ
īśvara uvāca
gṛhāṇa varade grāsamīpsitārthañca dehi me
vanditāsi vasiṣṭhena viśvāmitreṇa dhīmatā
kapile hara me pāpaṃ yanmayā duṣkṛtaṃ kṛtaṃ
gāvo mamāgrato nityaṃ gāvaḥ pṛṣṭhata eva ca
gāvo me hṛdaye cāpi gavāṃ madhye vasāmyahaṃ
dattaṃ gṛhṇantu me grāsaṃ japtvā syāṃ nirmalaḥ śivaḥ
yajet snātvā tu madhyāhne aṣṭapuṣpikayā śivaṃ
pīṭhamūrtiśivāṅgānāṃ pūjā syādaṣṭapuṣpikā
japtaiḥ sadarbhaśaṅkhasthaiḥ siñcettaṃ vārivindubhiḥ
viśodhya vidhinā cullīṃ tadvahniṃ pūrakāhutiṃ
vahnivījaṃ samādāya kādisthānagatikramāt
oṃ hāṃ agnaye namo vai hāṃ somāya vai namaḥ
sūryāya vṛhaspataye prajānāṃ pataye namaḥ
hāmagnaye khiṣṭikṛte pūrvādāvarcayedimān
svāhāntāmāhutiṃ datvā kṣamayitvā visarjayet
vāmabāhāvadharmāya kāñjikādikabhāṇḍake
vighnarājo gṛhadvāre peṣaṇyāṃ subhage namaḥ
sammārjanyāṃ devatokte kāmāya śayanīyake
ācāryaḥ sādhakaḥputra samayī maunamāsthitaḥ
vaṭāśvatthārkavātāvisarjabhallātakāṃstyajet
apośānaṃ purādāya prāṇādyaiḥ praṇavānvitaiḥ
svāhāntenāhutīḥ pañca datvādīpyodarānalaṃ
etebhya upavāyubhyaḥ svāhāpoṣānavāriṇā
prāṇāya svāhāpānāya samānāya tatas tathā
amṛtāpiścānamasīti śarīre 'nnādivāyavaḥ
īśvara uvāca
pavitrārohaṇaṃ vakṣye kriyārcādiṣu pūraṇaṃ
āṣāḍhādicaturdaśyāmatha śrāvaṇabhādrayoḥ
sitāsitāsu kartavyaṃ caturdaśyaṣṭamīṣu tat
kuryādvā kārttikīṃ yāvattithau pratipādike
vahnibrahmāmbikebhāsyanāgaskandārkaśūlināṃ
sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ tāmraṃ kṛtādiṣu yathākramaṃ
kalau kārpāsajaṃ cāpi paṭṭapadmādisūtrakaṃ
sarveśaḥ sarvadevāḥ syuḥ krameṇa navatantuṣu
aṣṭottaraśatānyardhaṃ tadardhaṃ cottamādikaṃ
ekāśītyāthavā sūtraistriṃśatāppaṣṭayuktayā
pañcāśatā vā kartavyaṃ tulyagranthyantarālakaṃ
dvādaśāṅgulamānāni vyāsādaṣṭāṅgulāni ca
liṅgavistāramānāni caturaṅgulakāni vā
gaṅgāvatārakaṃ kāryaṃ sujātena sudhautakaṃ
prakṛtiḥ pauruṣī vīrā caturthī tvaparājitā
jayānyā vijayā ṣaṣṭhī ajitā ca sadāśivā
syādekaikaṃ tathā dvāradikpālakalaśādiṣu
hastādinavahastāntaṃ liṅgānāṃ syātpavitrakaṃ
aṣṭāviṃśatito yuddhaṃ daśabhirdaśabhiḥ kramāt
dvyaṅgulābhyantarāstatra kramādekāṅgulāntarāḥ
granthayo mānamapyeṣāṃ liṅgavistārasasmitaṃ
saptamyāṃ vā trayodaśyāṃ kṛtanityakriyaḥ śuciḥ
bhūṣayet puṣpavastrādyaiḥ sāyāhne yāgamandiraṃ
kṛtvā naimittikīṃ sandhyāṃ viśeṣeṇa ca tarpaṇaṃ
hāṃ śāntikalādvārāya tathā vidyākalātmane
nivṛttikalādvārāya pratiṣṭhākhyakalātmane
nandine mahākālāya bhṛṅgiṇe 'tha gaṇāya ca
vṛṣabhāya ca skandāya devyai caṇḍāya ca kramāt
nityaṃ ca dvārapālādīn praviśya dvārapaścime
iṣṭvā vāstuṃ bhūtaśuddhiṃ viśeṣārghyakaraḥ śivaḥ
prokṣaṇādyaṃ vidhāyātha yajñasambhārakṛnnaraḥ
mantrayeddarbhadūrvādyaiḥ puṣpādyaiś ca hṛdādibhiḥ
śivo 'hamādiḥ sarvajño mama yajñapradhānatā
nairṛtīṃ diśamāsādya prakṣipedudagānanaḥ
catuṣpathāntasaṃskārair vīkṣaṇādyaiḥ susaṃskṛtaiḥ
tānīśadiśi vardhanyāmāsanāyopakalpayet
nairṛte vāstugīrvāṇā dvāre lakṣmīṃ prapūjayet
praṇavena vṛṣārūḍhaṃ siṃhasthāṃ vardhanīntataḥ
dikṣu śakrādidikpālān viṣṇubrahmaśivādikān
vardhanīṃ samyagādāya ghaṭapṛṣṭānugāminīṃ
śivājñāṃ śrāvayenmantrī pūrvādīśānagocaraṃ
samantād bhrāmayedenāṃ rakṣārthaṃ śastrarūpiṇīṃ
pūrvaṃ kalaśamāropya śastrārthantasya vāmataḥ
taddaśāṃśena vardhanyāṃ rakṣāṃ vijñāpayedapi
gaṇeśaṃ vāyave 'bhyarcya haraṃ pañcāmṛtādibhiḥ
snāpayet pūrvavat prārcya kuṇḍe ca śivapāvakaṃ
vidhivacca caruṃ kṛtvā sampātāhutiśodhitaṃ
datvā bhāgau śivāgnibhyāṃ saṃrakṣedbhāgamātmani
śareṇa carmaṇā deyaṃ pūrvato dantadhāvanaṃ
tasmādghoraśikhābhyāṃ vā dakṣiṇe paścime mṛdaṃ
sādyojātena ca hṛdā cottare vāmanīkṛtaṃ
jalaṃ vāmena śirasā īśe gandhānvitaṃ jalaṃ
pañcagavyaṃ palāśādipuṭakaṃ vai samantataḥ
aiśānyāṃ kusumaṃ dadyādāgneyyāṃ diśi rocanāṃ
aguruṃ nirṛtāśāyāṃ vāyavyāṃ ca catuḥsamaṃ
homadravyāṇi sarvāṇi sadyojātaiḥ kuśaiḥ saha
daṇḍākṣasūtrakaupīnabhikṣāpātrāṇi rūpiṇe
kajjalaṃ kuṅkumantailaṃ śalākāṃ keśaśodhanīṃ
tāmbūlaṃ darpaṇaṃ dadyāduttare rocanāmapi
āsanaṃ pāduke pātraṃ yogapaṭṭātapatrakaṃ
aiśānyāmīśamantreṇa dadyādīśānatuṣṭaye
pūrvasyāñcarukaṃ sājyaṃ dadyādgandhādikaṃ nave
pūrvitrāṇi samādāya prokṣitānyarghyavāriṇā
saṃhitāmantrapūtāni nītvā pāvakasannidhiṃ
kṛṣṇājinādināacchādya smaran saṃvatsarātmakaṃ
sākṣiṇaṃ sarvakṛtyānāṃ goptāraṃ śivamavyayaṃ
śodhayecca pavitrāṇi vārāṇāmekaviṃśatiṃ
gṛhādi veṣṭayetsūtrair gandhādyaṃ ravaye dadet
pūjitāya samācamya kṛtanyāsaḥ kṛtārghyakaḥ
atha sarvauṣadhīliptaṃ dhūpitaṃ puṣpadūrvayā
prabhavamantrayāmi tvāṃ tvadicchāvāptikārikāṃ
niyamañca kariṣyāmi parameśa tavājñayā
japaṃ stotraṃ pramāṇañca kṛtvā śambhuṃ kṣamāpayet
hutvā carostṛtīyāṃśaṃ taddaddīta śivāgnaye
digvāsibhyo digīśebhyo bhūtamātṛgaṇebhya
diṅnāgādyaiś ca pūrvādau kṣetrāya cāgnaye baliḥ
pūrṇāṃ vyāhṛtihomañca kṛtvā rundhīta pāvakaṃ
omagnīṣomābhyāṃ svāhāgnaye sviṣṭakṛte tathā
vahnikuṇḍārcitaṃ devaṃ maṇḍalābhyarcite śive
nāḍīsandhānarūpeṇa vidhinā yojayettataḥ
vaṃśādipātre vinyasya astrañca hṛdayantataḥ
ṣaḍaṅgaṃ brahmamūlair vā hṛddharmāstrañca yojayet
vidhāya sūtraiḥ saṃveṣṭya pūjayitvāṅgasambhavaiḥ
rakṣārthaṃ jagadīśāya bhaktinamraḥ samarpayet
guroḥ pādāntikaṃ gatvā bhaktyā dadyāt pavitrakaṃ
ācānto mantrasambaddhaḥ kṛtasaṅgītajāgaraḥ
kevalambhasmaśayyāyāṃ sopavāsaḥ samāhitaḥ
pavitrārohaṇavidhiḥ
īśvara uvāca
atha prātaḥ samutthāya kṛtasnānaḥ samāhitaḥ
aiśānyāṃ bhājane śuddhe sthāpayet kṛtamaṇḍale
naimittikīṃ savistarāṃ kuryāt pūjāṃ viśeṣataḥ
mantrāṇāṃ tarpaṇaṃ prāyaścittahomaṃ śarātmanā
aṣṭottaraśataṃ kṛtvā dadyāt pūrṇāhutiṃ śanaiḥ
oṃ kālātmanā tvayā deva yaddiṣṭaṃ māmake vidhau
kṛtaṃ kliṣṭaṃ samutsṛṣṭaṃ kṛtaṃ guptañca yat kṛtaṃ
tadastu kliṣṭamakliṣṭaṃ kṛtaṃ kliṣṭamasaṃskṛtaṃ
oṃ pūrayamakhavrataṃ niyameśvarāya svāhā
mūlaṃ layāntamuccārya pavitreṇārcayecchivaṃ
vidyātattve ca vidyānte viṣṇukāraṇapālite
śivānte śivatattve ca rudrakāraṇapālite
sarvakāraṇapāleṣu śivamuccārya suvrataḥ
mūlaṃ layāntamuccārya dadyādgaṅgāvatārakaṃ
ātmavidyāśivaiḥ proktaṃ mumukṣūṇāṃ pavitrakaṃ
vinirdiṣṭaṃ bubhukṣūṇāṃ śivatattvātmabhiḥ kramāt
svāhāntaṃ vā namo 'ntaṃ vā mantrameṣāmudīrayet
oṃ hāṃ ātmatattvādhipataye śivāya svāhā
oṃ hāṃ vidyātattvādhipataye śivāya svāhā
oṃ hauṃ śivatattvādhipataye śivāya svāhā
oṃ hauṃ sarvatattvādhipataye śivāya svāhā
natvā gaṅgāvatārantu prārthayettaṃ kṛtāñjaliḥ
tvaṅgatiḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ saṃsthitistvañcarācare
antaścāreṇa bhūtānāṃ draṣṭā tvaṃ parameśvara
karmaṇā manasā vācā tvatto nānyā gatirmama
mantrahīnaṃ kriyāhīnaṃ dravyahīnañca yat kṛtaṃ
japahomārcanair hīnaṃ kṛtaṃ nityaṃ mayā tava
akṛtaṃ vākyahīnaṃ ca tat pūraya maheśvaraṃ
supūtastvaṃ pareśāna pavitraṃ pāpanāśanaṃ
ekībhavatu tat sarvaṃ tavājñāsūtragumphitaṃ
natvā tu guruṇādiṣṭaṃ gṛhṇīyānniyamannaraḥ
praṇamya kṣamayitveśaṃ gatvā kuṇḍāntikaṃ vratī
pāvakasthe śive 'pyevaṃ pavitrāṇāṃ catuṣṭayaṃ
samāropya samabhyarcya puṣpadhūpākṣatādibhiḥ
praviśyāntaḥ śivaṃ stutvā sapraṇāmaṃ kṣamāpayet
prāyaścittakṛtaṃ homaṃ kṛtvā hutvā ca pāyasaṃ
śanaiḥ pūrṇāhutiṃ datvā vahnisthaṃ visṛjecchivaṃ
homaṃ vyāhṛtibhiḥ kṛtvā rundhyānniṣṭhurayānalaṃ
agnyādibhyastato dadyādāhutīnāṃ catuṣṭayaṃ
oṃ hāṃ bhūḥ svāhā oṃ hāṃ bhuvaḥ svāhā oṃ hāṃ svaḥ svāhā oṃ hāṃ bhūrbhuvaḥ svaḥ svāhā
homaṃ vyāhṛtibhiḥ kṛtvā datvāahuticatuṣṭayaṃ
oṃ hāṃ agnaye svāhā oṃ hāṃ somāya svāhā oṃ hāṃ agnīṣomābhyāṃ svāhā oṃ hāṃ agnaye sviṣṭakṛte svāhā
samagraṃ saphalaṃ tasya kriyākāṇḍādi vārṣikaṃ
dānenānena deveśa prīyatāṃ me sadā śivaḥ
bhaktyā snānādikaṃ prātaḥ kṛtvā śambhoḥ samāharet
pavitrāṇyaṣṭapuṣpaistaṃ pūjayitvā visarjayet
nityaṃ naimittikaṃ kṛtvā vistareṇa yathā purā
pavitrāṇi samāropya praṇamyāgnau śivaṃ yajet
prāyaścittaṃ tato 'streṇa hutvā pūrṇāhutiṃ yajet
bhuktikāmaḥ śivāyātha kuryāt karmasamarpaṇaṃ
vahnisthaṃ nāḍīyogena śivaṃ saṃyojayechive
hṛdi nyasyāgnisaṅghātaṃ pāvakaṃ ca visarjayet
samācamya praviśyāntaḥ kumbhānugatasaṃvarān
visṛjya lokapālādīnādāyeśāt pavitrakaṃ
sati caṇḍeśvare pūjāṃ kṛtvā datvā pavitrakaṃ
athavā sthaṇḍile caṇḍaṃ vidhinā pūrvavadyajet
yat kiñcidvārṣikaṃ karma kṛtaṃ nyūnādhikaṃ mayā
tadastu paripūrṇaṃ me caṇḍa nātha tavājñayā
tyaktanirmālyakaḥ śuddhaḥ snāpayitvā śivaṃ yajet
damanakārohaṇavidhiḥ
īśvara uvāca
harakopāt purā jāto bhairavo damitāḥ surāḥ
tenātha śapto viṭapo bhaveti tripurāriṇā
paripūrṇaphalaṃ teṣāṃ nānyathā te bhaviṣyati
saptamyāṃ vā trayodaśyāṃ damanaṃ saṃhitātmabhiḥ
śivakāryaṃ samuddiśya netavyo 'si śivājñayā
gṛhe 'pyāmantraṇaṃ kuryāt sāyāhne cādhivāsanaṃ
devasya paścime mūlaṃ dadyāttasya mṛdā yutaṃ
vāmena śirasā vātha nālaṃ dhātrīṃ tathottare
dakṣiṇe bhagnapatrañca prācyāṃ puṣpañca dhāraṇaṃ
puṭikāsthaṃ phalaṃ mūlamathaiśānyāṃ yajecchivaṃ
pañcāṅgamañjalau kṛtvā āmantrya śirasi nyaset
kartavyastapaso lābhaḥ pūrṇaṃ sarvaṃ tavājñayā
mūlena śeṣaṃ pātrasthaṃ pidhāyātha pavitrakaṃ
prātaḥ snātvā jagannāthaṃ gandhapuṣpādibhiryajet
nityaṃ naimittikaṃ kṛtvā damanaiḥ pūjayettataḥ
śeṣamañjalimādāya ātmavidyāśivātmabhiḥ
mūlādyair īśvarāntaiś ca caturthāñjalinā tataḥ
oṃ hauṃ makheśvarāya makhaṃ pūraya śūlapāṇaye namaḥ
bhagavannatiriktaṃ vā hīnaṃ vā yanmayā kṛtaṃ
samayadīkṣāvidhānaṃ
īśvara uvāca
vākṣyāmi bhogamokṣārthaṃ dīkṣāṃ pāpakṣayaṅkarīṃ
malamāyādipāśānāṃ viśleṣaḥ kriyate yayā
jñānañca janyate śiṣye sā dīkṣā bhuktimuktidā
vijñātakalanāmaiko dvitīyaḥ pralayākalaḥ
tṛtīyaḥ sakalaḥ śāstre 'nugrāhyastrividho mataḥ
nirādhārātha sādhārā dīkṣāpi dvividhā matā
nirādhārā dvayosteṣāṃ sādhārā sakalasya tu
tīvraśaktinipātena nirādhāreti sā smṛtā
ācāryamūrtimāsthāya māyātīvrādibhedayā
śaktyā yāṃ kurute śambhuḥ sā sādhikaraṇocyate
iyaṃ caturvidhā proktā savījā vījavarjitā
sādhikārānadhikārā yathā tadabhidhīyate
samayācārasaṃyuktā savījā jāyate nṛṇāṃ
nirvījā tvasamarthānāṃ samayācāravarjitā
sādhikārā bhaveddīkṣā sādhakācāryayorataḥ
nirvījā dīkṣitānāntu yadāsa mama putrayoḥ
nityamātrādhikāratvaddīkṣā niradhikārikā
ekā kriyāvatī tatra kuṇḍamaṇḍalapūrvikā
manovyāpāramātreṇa yā sā jñānavatī matā
itthaṃ labdhādhikāreṇa dīkṣāacāryeṇa sādhyate
skandadīkṣāṃ guruḥ kuryāt kṛtvā nityakriyāṃ tataḥ
praṇavārgyakarāmbhojakṛtadvārādhipārcaṇaḥ
vighnānutsārya dehalyāṃ nyasyāstraṃ svāsane sthitaḥ
tilataṇḍulasiddhārthakuśadūrvākṣatodakaṃ
sayavakṣīranīrañca viśeṣārghyamidantataḥ
tadambunā dravyaśuddhiṃ tilakaṃ svāsanātmanoḥ
lājacandanasiddhārthabhasmadūrvākṣataṃ kuśān
vikirān śuddhalājāṃstān sadhūpānastramantritān
śastrāmbuprokṣitānetān kavacenāvaguṇṭhitān
nānāgrahaṇākārān vighnaughavinivārakān
darbhāṇāntālamānena kṛtvā ṣaṭtriṃśatā dalaiḥ
saptajaptaṃ śivāstreṇa veṇīṃ bodhāsimuttamaṃ
śivamātmani vinyasya sṛṣṭyādhāramabhīpsitaṃ
uṣṇīṣaṃ śirasi nyasya alaṃ kuryātsvadehakaṃ
gandhamaṇḍanakaṃ svīye vidadhyāddakṣiṇe kare
śivādabhinnamātmānaṃ kartāraṃ bhāvayedyathā
maṇḍale karmaṇāṃ sākṣī kalaśe yajñarakṣakaḥ
homādhikaraṇaṃ vahnau śiṣye pāśavimocakaḥ
svātmanyanugṛhīteti ṣaḍādhāro ya īśvaraḥ
jñānakhaḍgakaraḥ sthitvā nairṛtyābhimukho naraḥ
sārghyāmbupañcagavyābhyāṃ prokṣayedyāgamaṇḍapaṃ
catuṣpathāntasaṃskāraiḥ saṃskuryādīkṣaṇādibhiḥ
tānīśadiśi vardhanyāmāsanāyopakalpayet
nairṛte vāstugīrvāṇān dvāre lakṣmīṃ prapūjayet
āpye ratnaiḥ pūrayantīṃ hṛdā maṇḍaparūpiṇīṃ
paścimasyāntu siṃhasthāṃ vardhanīṃ khaḍgarūpiṇīṃ
dikṣu śakrādidikpālānviṣṇvantān praṇavāsanān
vāhanāyudhasaṃyuktān hṛdābhyarcya svanāmabhiḥ
prathamantāṃ samādāya kumbhasyāgrābhigāminīṃ
avicchinnapayodharāṃ bhrāmayitvā pradakṣiṇaṃ
śivājñāṃ lokapālānāṃ śrāvayenmūlamuccaran
saṃrakṣata yathāyogaṃ kumbhaṃ dhṛtvātha tāṃ dhāret
tataḥ sthirāsane kumbhe sāṅgaṃ sampūjya śaṅkaraṃ
oṃ haḥ astrāsanāya hūṃ phaṭ oṃ oṃ astramūrtaye namaḥ oṃ hūṃ phaṭ pāśupatāstrāya namaḥ oṃ oṃ hṛdayāya hūṃ phaṭ namaḥ oṃ śrīṃ śirase hūṃ phaṭ namaḥ oṃ yaṃ śikhāyai hūṃ phaṭ namaḥ oṃ gūṃ kavacāya hūṃ phaṭ namaḥ oṃ phaṭ astrāya hūṃ phaṭ namaḥ
caturvaktraṃ sadaṃṣṭrañca smaredastraṃ saśaktikaṃ
samudgaratriśūlāsiṃ sūryakoṭisamaprabhaṃ
agguṣṭhena spṛśet kumbhaṃ hṛdā muṣṭyāstravardhanīṃ
bhuktaye muktaye tvādau muṣṭinā vardhanīṃ spṛśet
taddaśāṃśena vardhanyāṃ rakṣāṃ vijñāpayettataḥ
rakṣaṇīyaṃ jagannātha sarvādhvaradhara tvayā
sthaṇḍile śivamabhyarcya sārghyakuṇḍaṃ vrajennaraḥ
kuṇḍavahnisrugājyādi prāgvat saṃskṛtya bhāvayet
sṛṣṭinyāsena vinyasya śodhyādhvānaṃ yathāvidhi
kuṇḍamānaṃ mukhaṃ dhyātvā hṛdāhutibhirīpsitaṃ
hiraṇyā vanakā raktā kṛṣṇā tadanu suprabhā
atiriktā bahurūpā rudrendrāgnyāpyadiṅmukhā
kṣīrādimadhurair homaṃ kuryācchāntikapauṣṭike
abhicāre tu piṇyākasaktukañcukakāñcikaiḥ
lavaṇair ājikātakrakaṭutailaiś ca kaṇṭakaiḥ
bandhūkakiṃśukādīni vaśyākarṣāya homayet
bilvaṃ rājyāya lakṣmārthaṃ pāṭalāṃś campakānapi
dūrvā vyādhivināśāya sarvasattvavaśīkṛte
priyaṅgupāṭalīpuṣpaṃ cūtapatraṃ jvarāntakaṃ
mṛtyuñjayo mṛtyujit syād vṛddhiḥ syāttilahomataḥ
āhutyaṣṭaśatair mūlamaṅgāni tu daśāṃśataḥ
santarpayeta mūlena dadyāt pūrṇāṃ yathā purā
tathā śiṣyapraveśāya pratiśiṣyaṃ śataṃ japet
mūlādyaṣṭāstramantrāṇāṃ svāhāntaistarpaṇaṃ sakṛt
śikhāsampuṭitair vījair hrūṃ phaḍantaiś ca dīpanaṃ
oṃ hauṃ śivāya svāhetyādimantraiś ca tarpaṇaṃ
oṃ hrūṃ hrauṃ hrīṃ śivāya hrūṃ phaḍityādidīpanaṃ
tataḥ śivāmbhasā sthālīṃ kṣālitāṃ varmaguṇṭhitāṃ
candanādisamālabdhāṃ badhnīyāt kaṭakaṃ gale
nyastāyāṃ mūrtibhūtāyāṃ bhāvapuṣpaiḥ śivaṃ yajet
vastrabaddhamukhāyāṃ vā sthālyāṃ puṣpair vahirbhavaiḥ
cullyāṃ paścimavaktrāyāṃ nyastāyāṃ mānuṣātmanā
nyastāhaṅkāravījāyāṃ śuddhāyāṃ vīkṣaṇādibhiḥ
dharmādharmaśarīrāyāṃ japtāyāṃ mānuṣātmanā
sthālīmāropayedastrajaptāṃ gavyāmbumārjitāṃ
gavyaṃ payo 'strasaṃśuddhaṃ prāsādaśatamantritaṃ
tuṇḍalān śyāmakādīnāṃ nikṣipettatra tadyathā
ekaśiṣyavidhānāya teṣāṃ prasṛtipañcakaṃ
prasṛtiṃ prasṛtiṃ paścādvardhayed dvyādiṣu kramāt
kuryāccānalamantreṇa pidhānaṃ kavacāṇunā
śivāgnau mūlamantreṇa pūrvāsyaś carukaṃ pacet
sukhinne tatra taccullyāṃ śruvamāpūrya sarpiṣā
svāhāntaiḥ saṃhitāmantrair datvā taptābhighāraṇaṃ
saṃsthāpya maṇḍale sthālīṃ saddarbhe 'strāṇunā kṛte
praṇavena pidhāyāsyāṃ taddehalepanaṃ hṛdā
suśītalo bhavatyevam prāpya śītābhighāraṇaṃ
vidadhyātsaṃhitāmantraiḥ śiṣyaṃ prati sakṛt sakṛt
dharmādyāsanake hutvā kuṇḍamaṇḍalapaścime
sampātañca srucā hutvā śuddhiṃ saṃhitayā caret
dhenumudrāmṛtībhūtaṃ sthaṇḍileśāntikaṃ nayet
sājyabhāgaṃ svaśiṣyāṇāṃ bhāgo devāya vahnaye
sājyaṃ mantraśataṃ hutvā dadyāt pūrṇāṃ yathāvidhi
maṇḍalaṃ kuṇḍataḥ pūrve madhye vā śambhukumbhayoḥ
rudramātṛgaṇādīnāṃ nirvartyāntarbaliṃ hṛdā
mamāṃśo yojanāsthānamadhiṣṭhāhamadhvare
śivo 'hamityahaṅkārī niṣkramed yāgamaṇḍapāt
nyastapūrvāgrasandharbhe śastrāṇukṛtamaṇḍale
praṇavāsanake śiṣyaṃ śuklavastrottarīyakaṃ
ūrdhvaṃ kāyaṃ samāropya pūrvāsyaṃ pravilokayet
caraṇādiśikhāṃ yāvanmuktau bhuktau vilomataḥ
cakṣuṣā saprasādena śaivaṃ dhāma vivṛṇvatā
bhasmasnānāya vighnānāṃ śāntaye pāpabhittaye
sṛṣṭisaṃhārayogena tāḍayedastrabhasmanā
punarastrāmbunā prokṣya sakalīkaraṇāya taṃ
nābherūrdhvaṃ kuśāgreṇa mārjanīyāstramuccaran
dvaividhyāya ca pāśānāṃ ālabheta śarāṇunā
taccharīre śivaṃ sāṅgaṃ sāsanaṃ vinyasettataḥ
puṣpādipūjitasyāsya netre netreṇa vā hṛdā
pradakṣiṇakramādenaṃ praveśya śivadakṣiṇaṃ
saṃhāramudrayātmānaṃ mūrtyā tasya hṛdambuje
śivahastaṃ pradātavyaṃ rudreśapadadāyakaṃ
śivasevāgrahopāyaṃ dattahastaṃ śivāṇunā
śive prakṣepayet puṣpamapanīyārcakantāraṃ
tatpātrasthānamantrāḍhyaṃ śivadevagaṇānugaṃ
viprādīnāṃ kramānnāma kuryādvā svecchayā guruḥ
śiṣyadehaviniṣkrāntāṃ suṣumṇāmiva cintayet
tammūlamātmajaṅghāyāmagrañceti śikhidhvaje
śiṣyasya hṛdayaṃ gatvā recakena śivāṇunā
purakeṇa samāgatya svakīyaṃ hṛdyāntaraṃ
śivāgninā punaḥ kṛtvā nāḍīsandhānamīdṛśaṃ
hṛdā tatsannidhānārthañjuhuyādāhutitrayaṃ
itthaṃ samayadīkṣāyāṃ bhavedyogyo bhavārcane
saṃskāradīkṣākathanaṃ
īśvara uvāca
vakṣye saṃskāradīkṣāyāṃ vidhānaṃ śṛṇu ṣaṇmukha
kusumenāstraliptena tāḍayettaṃ hṛdā śiśuṃ
saṃhāriṇyā tadākṛṣya pūrakeṇa hṛdi nyaset
tato vāgīśvarīyaunau mudrayodbhavasañjñayā
oṃ hāṃ hāṃ hāṃ ātmane namaḥ
snigdhaḥ pradakṣiṇāvartaḥ sugandhiḥ śasyate 'nalaḥ
viparītasphuliṅgī ca bhūmisparśaḥ praśasyate
ityevamādibhiścihnair hutvā śiṣyasya kalmaṣaṃ
pāpabhakṣaṇahomena dahedvā taṃ bhavātmanā
dvijatvāpādanārthāya tathā rudrāṃśabhāvane
āhāravījasaṃśuddhau garbhādhānāya saṃsthitau
śatāni pañca mūlena vauṣaḍādidaśāṃśataḥ
śithilībhūtabandhasya śaktāvutkarṣaṇaṃ ca yat
māyātmanorvivekena jñānaṃ sīmantavardhanaṃ
śivāditattvaśuddhestu svīkāro jananaṃ mataṃ
saṃhāramudrayātmānaṃ sphuradvahnikaṇopamaṃ
kuryāt samavaśībhāvaṃ tadā ca śivayorhṛdi
brahmādikāraṇātyāgakramādrecakayogataḥ
nītvā śivāntamātmānamādāyodbhavamudrayā
śiṣyasya hṛdayāmbhojakarṇikāyāṃ vinikṣipet
pūjāṃ śivasya vahneś ca guruḥ kuryāttadocitāṃ
praṇatiñcātmane śiṣyaṃ samayān śrāvayettathā
