śivāgnigurupūjā ca kartavyā jīvitāvadhi
bālabāliśavṛddhastrībhogabhugvyādhitātmanāṃ
bhūtāṅgāni jaṭābhasmadaṇḍakaupīnasaṃyamān
īśānādyair hṛdādyair vā parijapya yathākramāt
svāhāntasaṃhitamantraiḥ pātreṣvāropya pūrvavat
sampāditadrutaṃ hutvā sthaṇḍileśāya darśayet
rakṣaṇāya ghaṭādhastādāropya kṣaṇamātrakaṃ
śivādājñāṃ samādāya dadīta yatine guruḥ
evaṃ samayadīkṣāyāṃ viśiṣṭāyāṃ viśeṣataḥ
vahnihomāgamajñānayogyaḥ sañjāyate śiśruḥ
nirvāṇadīkṣākathanaṃ
īśvara uvāca
atha nirvāṇadīkṣāyāṃ kuryānmūlādidīpanaṃ
pāśabandhanaśaktyarthaṃ tāḍanādikṛtena vā
vījagarbhaśikhārdhantu hūṃ phaḍantadhruvādinā
oṃ hrūṃ hrauṃ hauṃ hrūṃ phaḍiti mūlamantrasya dīpanaṃ
oṃ hrūṃ hauṃ hauṃ hrūṃ phaḍiti hṛdaya evaṃ śiromukhe
śāntike pauṣṭike cāsya vaṣaḍantādināṇunā
havanaṃ saṃvaraiḥ kuryāt sarvatrāpyāyanādiṣu
śiṣyaṃ sampūjya tat sūtraṃ suṣumṇeti vibhāvitaṃ
mūlena tacchikhābandhaṃ pādāṅguṣṭhāntamānayet
saṃhāreṇa mumukṣostu badhnīyācchiṣyakāyake
puṃsastu dakṣiṇe bhāge vāme nāryā niyojayet
nāḍīntvādāya mūlena sūtre nyasya hṛdārcayet
oṃ hāṃ varṇādhvane namo hāṃ bhavanādhvane namaḥ
oṃ hāṃ kālādhvane namaḥ śodhyādhvānaṃ hi sūtrake
nyasyāstravāriṇā śiṣyaṃ prokṣyāstramantritena ca
puṣpeṇa hṛdi santāḍya śiṣyadehe praviśya ca
caitanyaṃ haṃsavījasthaṃ viśliṣyedāyudhātmanā
oṃ hauṃ hūṃ phaṭ
āchidya śaktisūtreṇa hāṃ haṃ svāheti cāṇunā
saṃhāramudrayā sūtre nāḍībhūte niyojayet
oṃ hāṃ haṃ hāṃ ātmane namaḥ
vyāpakaṃ bhāvayedenaṃ tanutrāṇāvaguṇṭhayet
vidyādehañca vinyasya śāntyatītāvalokanaṃ
oṃ hāṃ hauṃ śāntyatītakalāpāśāya nama ity anenāvalokayet
he tattve mantramapyekaṃ padaṃ varṇāś ca ṣoḍaśa
tathāṣṭau bhuvanānyasyāṃ vījanāḍīkathadvayaṃ
viṣayañca guṇañcaikaṃ kāraṇaṃ ca sadā śivaṃ
sitāyāṃ śāntyatītāyāmantarbhāvya prapīḍayet
oṃ hauṃ śāntyatītakalāpāśāya hūṃ phaṭ
guṇau mantrau tathābjasthamekaṃ kāraṇamīśvaraṃ
ekañca viṣayaṃ śāntau kṛṣṇāyāmacyutaṃ smaret
tāḍayitvā samādāya mukhasūtre niyojayet
vidyāyāṃ sapta tattvāni pādānāmekaviṃśatiṃ
ṣaḍ varṇān sañcaraṃ caikaṃ lokānāṃ pañcaviṃśatiṃ
guṇānāntrayamekañca viṣayaṃ rudrakāraṇaṃ
antarbhāvyātiriktāyāṃ jīvanāḍīkathadvayaṃ
astramādāya dadhyācca padaṃ dvyadhikaviṃśatiṃ
lokānāñca kalānāñca ṣaṣṭiṃ guṇacatuṣṭayaṃ
mantrāṇāṃ trayamekañca viṣayaṃ kāraṇaṃ hariṃ
antarbhāvya pratiṣṭhāyāṃ śuklayāntāḍanādikaṃ
vidhāya nābhisūtrasthāṃ sannidhāyāhutīryajet
hrīṃ bhuvanānāṃ śataṃ sāgraṃ padānāmaṣṭaviṃśatiṃ
vījanāḍīsamīrāṇāṃ dvayorindriyayorapi
varṇantattvañca viṣayamekaikaṃ guṇapañcakaṃ
hetuṃ brahmāṇḍamantrasthaṃ śambarāṇāṃ catuṣṭayaṃ
nivṛttau pītavarṇāyāmantarbhāvya pratāḍayet
juhuyādāhutīstisraḥ sannidhāya pāvake
savījāyāntu dīkṣāyāṃ samayācārayāgataḥ
iṣṭāpūrtādidharmārthaṃ vyatiriktaṃ prabandhakaṃ
oṃ hauṃ śāntyatītakalāpāśāya svāhetyāditarpaṇaṃ
oṃ hāṃ haṃ hāṃ śāntyatītakalāpāśāya hūmphaḍityādidīpanaṃ
tat sūtraṃ vyāptibodhāya kalāsthāneṣu pañcasu
saṅgṛhya kuṅkumājyena tatra sāṅgaṃ śivaṃ yajet
hūmphaḍantaiḥ kalāmantrair bhittvā pāśānanukramāt
oṃ hūṃ hāṃ hauṃ hāṃ hūṃ phaṭ śāntyatītakalāṃ gṛhṇāmi badhnāmi cetyādimantraiḥ kalānāṃ grahaṇabandhanādiprayogaḥ
pāśādīnāñca svīkāro grahaṇaṃ bandhanaṃ punaḥ
puruṣaṃ prati niḥśeṣavyāpārapratipattaye
upaveśyātha tat sūtraṃ śiṣyaskandhe niveśayet
vistṛtāghapramoṣāya śataṃ mūlena homayet
śarāvasampuṭe puṃsaḥ striyāś ca praṇitodare
hṛdastrasampuṭaṃ sūtraṃ vidhāyābhyarcayeddhṛdā
sūtraṃ śivena sāṅgena kṛtvā sampātaśodhitaṃ
nidadhyāt kalaśasyādho rakṣāṃ vijñāpayediti
śiṣyaṃ puṣpaṃ kare datvā sampūjya kalaśādikaṃ
maṇḍalatritayaṃ kṛtvā mumukṣvanuttarānanān
bhuktaye pūrvavaktrāṃś ca śiṣyāṃstatra niveśayet
pāṇinā kuśayuktena arcitānantarāntaraṃ
aṣṭagrāsapramāṇaṃ vā daśanasparśavarjitaṃ
hṛdā sambhojanaṃ datvā pūtair ācāmayejjalaiḥ
dantakāṣṭhaṃ hṛdā kṛtvā prakṣipecchobhane śubhaṃ
nyūnādidoṣamoṣāya mūlenāṣṭottaraṃ śataṃ
vidhāya sthiṇḍileśāya sarvakarmasamarpaṇaṃ
pūjāvisarjanañcāsya caṇḍeśasya ca pūjanaṃ
kalaśaṃ lokapalāṃś ca pūjayitvā visṛjya ca
visṛjedgaṇamagniñca rakṣitaṃ yadi vāhyataḥ
vāhyato lokapālānāṃ datvā saṅkṣepato baliṃ
bhasmanā śuddhatoyair vā snātvā yā gālayaṃ viśet
gṛhasthān darbhaśayyāyāṃ pūrvaśīrṣān surakṣitān
hṛdā sadbhasmaśayyāyāṃ yatīn dakṣiṇamastakān
śikhābaddhasikhānastrasaptamāṇavakānvitān
vijñāya snāpayecchiṣyāṃstato yāyāt punarvahiḥ
oṃ hili hili triśūlapāṇaye svāhā
pañcagavyañcaruṃ prāśya gṛhītvā dantadhāvanaṃ
samācamya śivaṃ dhyātvā śayyāmāsthāya pāvanīṃ
dīkṣāgataṅkriyākāṇḍaṃ saṃsmaran saṃviśedguruḥ
iti saṅkṣepataḥ prokto vidhirdīkṣādhivāsane
nirvāṇadīkṣāvidhānaṃ
īśvara uvāca
dadhyārdramāṃsamadyādeḥ praśastābhyavahāritā
gajāśvarohaṇaṃ svapne śubhaṃ śuklāṃśukādikaṃ
tailābhyaṅgādikaṃ hīnaṃ homo ghoreṇa śāntaye
nityakarmadvayaṃ kṛtvā praviśya makhamaṇḍapaṃ
tataḥ saṃśodhya cātmānaṃ śivahastaṃ tathātmani
maṇḍale sthaṇḍile vāpi prakurvīta śivarcanaṃ
tarpaṇaṃ pūjanaṃ vahneḥ pūrṇāntaṃ mantratarpaṇaṃ
duḥkhapradoṣamoṣāya śastreṇāṣṭādhikaṃ śataṃ
hutvā hūṃ sampuṭenaiva vidadhyāt mantradīpanaṃ
kṛtvā śiṣyapraveśāya labdhānujño vahirvrajet
kuryātsamayavattatra maṇḍalāropaṇādikaṃ
sampātahomaṃ tannāḍīrūpadarbhakarānugaṃ
tatsannidhānāya tistro hutvā mūlāṇunāahutīḥ
tacchikhāyāṃ nibadhnīyāt pādāṅguṣṭhāvalambitaṃ
jñeyāni bhuvanānyasyāṃ śatamaṣṭādhikaṃ tataḥ
vibhūtiravyayaḥ śāstā pinākī tridaśādhipaḥ
agnī rudro hutāśo ca piṅgalaḥ khādako haraḥ
yāmyamṛtyuharo dhātā vidhātā kāryarañjakaḥ
nairṛto māraṇo hantā krūradṛṣṭirbhayānakaḥ
ūrdhvāṃśako virūpākṣo dhūmralohitadaṃṣṭravān
balaścātibalaś caiva pāśahasto mahābalaḥ
śvetaś ca jayabhadraś ca dīrghabāhurjalāntakaḥ
vaḍavāsyaś ca bhīmaś ca daśaite vāruṇāḥ smṛtāḥ
śīghro laghurvāyuvegaḥ sūkṣmastīkṣṇaḥ kṣapāntakaḥ
pañcāntakaḥ pañcaśikhaḥ kapardī meghavāhanaḥ
jaṭāmukuṭadhārī ca nānāratnadharas tathā
nidhīśo rūpavān dhanyo saumyadehaḥ prasādakṛt
prakāśo 'pyatha lakṣmīvān kāmarūpo daśottare
vidyādharo jñānadharaḥ sarvajño vedapāragaḥ
mātṛvṛttaś ca piṅgākṣo bhūtapālo balipriyaḥ
anantaḥ pālako dhīraḥ pātālādhipatis tathā
vṛṣo vṛṣadharo vīryo grasanaḥ sarvatomukhaḥ
lohitaś caiva vijñeyā daśa rudrāḥ phaṇisthitāḥ
saṃhāraś ca vihāraś ca lābho lipsurvicakṣaṇaḥ
kuṣmāṇḍaś caiva satyaś ca brahmā viṣṇuś ca saptamaḥ
rudraścāṣṭāvime rudrāḥ kaṭāhābhyantare sthitāḥ
eteṣāmeva nāmāni bhuvanānāmapi smaret
saṃstuta pūrvasthita oṃ sākṣin oṃ rudrāntaka oṃ pataṅga oṃ śabda oṃ sūkṣma oṃ śiva sarvasarvada sarvasānnidhyakara brahmaviṣṇurudrakara oṃ namaḥ śivāya oṃ namo namaḥ
aṣṭāviṃśati pādāni vyomavyāpi mano guha
sadyohṛdastranetrāṇi mantravarṇāṣṭako mataḥ
vījākāro makāraś ca nāḍyāviḍāpiṅgalāhvaye
prāṇāpānāvubhau vāyū ghrāṇopasthau tathendriye
pārthivaṃ maṇḍalaṃ pītaṃ vajrāṅgaṃ caturasrakaṃ
vistāro yojanānāntu koṭirasya śatāhatā
prathamā sarvadevānāṃ manvādyā devayonayaḥ
mṛgapakṣī ca paśavaś caturdhā tu sarīsṛpāḥ
sthāvaraṃ pañcamaṃ sarvaṃ yoniḥ ṣaṣṭhī amānuṣī
paiśācaṃ rākṣasaṃ yākṣaṃ gāndharvaṃ caindrameva ca
saumyaṃ prāṇeśvaraṃ brāhmamaṣṭamaṃ parikīrtitaṃ
aṣṭānāṃ pārthivantattvamadhikārāspadaṃ mataṃ
oṃ hāṃ hrūṃ hāṃ nivṛttikalāpāśāya hūṃ phaṭ tata oṃ hāṃ hāṃ nivṛttikalāpāśāya svāhetyanenāṅkuśamudrayā pūrakeṇākṛṣya oṃ hrūṃ hrāṃ hrūṃ nivṛttikalāpāśāya hūṃ phaḍityanena saṃhāramudrayā kumbhakenādhaḥ
sthānādādāya oṃ oṃ hrāṃ hāṃ nivṛttikalāpāśāya nama ity anenodbhavamudrayā recakena kumbhe saṃsthāpya oṃ hāṃ nivṛttikalāpāśāya nama ity anenārghyaṃ datvā sampūjya vimukhenaiva svāhāntenai sannidhānāyāhutitrayaṃ santarpaṇāhutitrayaṃ ca datvā oṃ hāṃ brahmaṇe nama iti brahmāṇamāvāhya sampūjya ca svāhāntena santarpya
bhāvyaṃ tvayānukūlena vidhiṃ vijñāpayediti
āvāhayettato devīṃ rakṣāṃ vāgīśvarīṃ hṛdā
icchājñānakriyārūpāṃ ṣaḍvidhāṃ hy ekakāraṇaṃ
pūjayettarpayeddevīṃ prakāreṇāmunā tataḥ
vāgīśvarīṃ viniḥśeṣayonivikṣobhakāraṇaṃ
hṛtsampuṭārthavījādihūṃ phaḍantaśarāṇunā
tataḥ śiṣyasya caitanyaṃ hṛdi vahnikaṇopamaṃ
nivṛttisthaṃ yutaṃ pāśair jyeṣṭhayā vibhajedyathā
oṃ hāṃ hūṃ haḥ hūṃ phaṭ
oṃ hāṃ svāhetyanenātha pūrakeṇāṅkuśamudrayā
tadākṛṣya svamantreṇa gṛhītvāatmani yojayet
oṃ hāṃ hrūṃ hāṃ ātmane namaḥ
brahmādikāraṇatyāgakramānnītvā śivāspadaṃ
kṣipedvāgīśvarīyonau vāmayodbhavamudrayā
oṃ hāṃ hāṃ hāṃ ātmane namaḥ
nātra puṃsavanaṃ stryādiśarīrasyāpi sambhavāt
tathaiva bhāvayedeṣāmadhikāraṃ śivāṇunā
bhogaṃ kavacamantreṇa śastreṇa viṣayātmanā
śivena śrotasāṃ śuddhiṃ hṛdā tattvaviśodhanaṃ
pañca pañcāhutīḥ kuryāt garbhādhānādiṣu kramāt
māyayā malakarmādipāśabandhanivṛttaye
niṣkṛtyaiva hṛdā paścād yajeta śatamāhutīḥ
malaśaktinirodhena pāśānāñca viyojanaṃ
svāhāntāyudhamantreṇa pañcapañcāhutīryajet
māyādyantasya pāśasya saptavārāstrajaptayā
oṃ hūṃ nivṛttikalāpāśāya hūṃ phaṭ
bandhakatvañca nirvartya hastābhyāñca śarāṇunā
kuryāt pañcāhutīrdatvā pāśāṅkuśanivṛttaye
oṃ haḥ astrāya hūṃ phaṭ
prāyaścittaṃ tataḥ kuryādastrāhutibhiraṣṭabhiḥ
athāvāhya vidhātāraṃ pūjayettarpayettathā
tata oṃ hāṃ śabdasparśaśuddhabrahman gṛhāṇa svāhetyāhutitrayeṇādhikāramasya samarpayet
bandhāya na punaḥ stheyaṃ śivājñāṃ śrāvayediti
tato visṛjya dhātāraṃ nāḍyā dakṣiṇayā śanaiḥ
saṃhāramudrayātmānaṃ kumbhakena nijātmanā
visṛjya pitarau dadyādvauṣaḍantaśivāṇunā
pūraṇāya vidhiḥ pūrṇā nivṛttiriti śodhitā
pratiṣṭhākalāśodhanoktiḥ
īśvara uvāca
hrasvadīrghaprayogeṇa nādanādāntasaṅginā
oṃ hāṃ hrūṃ hāṃ
aptejo vāyurākāśaṃ tanmātrendriyabuddhayaḥ
guṇatrayamahaṅkāraś caturviṃśaḥ pumāniti
pratiṣṭhāyāṃ niviṣṭhāni tattvānyetāni bhāvayet
pañcaviṃśatisaṅkhyāni khādiyāntākṣarāṇi ca
pañcāśadadhikā ṣaṣṭirbhuvanaistulyasañjñitāḥ
amareśaḥ prabhāvaś ca nemiṣaḥ puṣkaro 'pi ca
tathā pādiś ca daṇḍiś ca bhāvabhūtirathāṣṭamaḥ
nakulīśo hariś candraḥ śrīśailo daśamaḥ smṛtaḥ
anvīśo 'srātikeśaś ca mahākālo 'tha madhyamaḥ
kedāro bhairavaś caiva dvitīyāṣṭakamīritaṃ
vimalaścāṭṭahāsaś ca mahendro bhāma eva ca
gokarṇo bhadrakarṇaś ca svarṇākṣaḥ sthāṇureva ca
ajeśaś caiva sarvajño bhāsvaraḥ sūdanāntaraḥ
subāhurmattarūpī ca viśālo jaṭilas tathā
raudro 'tha piṅgalākṣaś ca kāladaṃṣṭrī bhavettataḥ
viduraś caiva ghoraś ca prājāpatyo hutāśanaḥ
kāmarūpī tathā kālaḥ karṇo 'pyatha bhayānakaḥ
mataṅgaḥ piṅgalaś caiva haro vai dhātṛsajñakaḥ
śaṅkukarṇo vidhānaś ca śrīkaṇṭhaś candraśekharaḥ
vyāpin oṃ arūpa oṃ pramatha oṃ tejaḥ oṃ jyotiḥ oṃ puruṣa oṃ agne oṃ adhūma oṃ abhasma oṃ anādi oṃ nānā oṃ dhūdhū oṃ bhūḥ oṃ bhuvaḥ oṃ svaḥ anidhana nidhanodbhava śiva śarva paramātman maheśvara mahādeva sadbhāveśvara mahātejaḥ yogādhipataye muñca prathama sarva sarvesarveti dvātriṃśat padāni
vījabhāve trayo mantrā vāmadevaḥ śivaḥ śikhā
gāndhārī ca suṣumṇā ca nāḍyau dvau mārutau tathā
samānodānanāmānau rasanāpāyurindriye
rasastu viṣayo rūpaśabdasparśarasā guṇāḥ
maṇḍalaṃ vartulaṃ tacca puṇḍarīkāṅkitaṃ sitaṃ
svapnāvasthāpratiṣṭhāyāṃ kāraṇaṃ garuḍadhvajaṃ
pratiṣṭhāntakṛtaṃ sarvaṃ sañcintya bhuvanādikaṃ
oṃ hāṃ khīṃ hāṃ pratiṣṭhākalāpāśāya oṃ phaṭ svāhāntenānainaiva pūrakeṇāṅkuśamudrayā samākarṣet tataḥ oṃ hāṃ hrūṃ hrāṃ hrūṃ pratiṣṭhā kalāpāśāya hrūṃ phaḍityanena saṃhāramudrayā kumbhakena hṛdayādadho nāḍī
sūtrādādāya oṃ hāṃ hrūṃ hrāṃ hāṃ pratiṣṭhākalāpāśāya nama ity anenodbhavamudrayā recakena kumbhe samāropayet oṃ hāṃ hrīṃ pratiṣṭhākalāpāśāya nama ity anenārcayitvā sampūjya svāhāntenāhutīnāṃ trayeṇa sannidhāya tataḥ oṃ hāṃ viṣṇave nama iti viṣṇumāvāhya sampūjya santarpya
viṣṇo tavādhikāre 'smin mumukṣuṃ dīkṣayāmyahaṃ
bhāvyaṃ tvayānukūlena viṣṇuṃ vijñāpayediti
tato vāgīśvarīṃ devīṃ vāgīśamapi pūrvavat
āvāhyābhyarcya santarpya śiṣyaṃ vakṣasi tāḍayet
oṃ hāṃ hāṃ haṃ phaṭ
śastreṇa pāśasaṃyuktaṃ jyeṣṭayāṅkuśamudrayā
oṃ hāṃ haṃ hoṃ hrūṃ phaṭ
svāhāntena hṛdākṛṣya tenaiva puṭitātmanā
oṃ hāṃ haṃ hoṃ ātmane namaḥ
pūrvavat pitṛsaṃyogaṃ bhāvayitvodbhavākhyayā
oṃ hāṃ haṃ hāṃ ātmane namaḥ
dehotpattau hṛdā hy evaṃ śirasā janmanā tathā
śikhayā vādhikārāya bhogāya kavacāṇunā
tattvaśuddhau hṛdā hy evaṃ garbhādhānāya pūrvavat
śirasā pāśaśaithilye niṣkṛtyaivaṃ śataṃ japet
evaṃ pāśaviyoge 'pi tataḥ śāstrajaptayā
chindyādastreṇa kartaryā kalāvījavatā yathā
oṃ hrīṃ pratiṣṭhākalāpāśāya haḥ phaṭ
visṛjya vartulīkṛtya pāśamantreṇa pūrvavat
ghṛtapūrṇe śrave datvā kalāstreṇaiva homayet
astreṇa juhuyāt pañca pāśāṅkuranivṛttaye
prāyaścittaniṣedhārthaṃ dadyādaṣṭāhutīstataḥ
oṃ haḥ astrāya hrūṃ phaṭ
hṛdāvāhya hṛṣīkeśaṃ kṛtvā pūjatarpaṇe
oṃ hāṃ rasaśulkaṃ gṛhāṇa svāhā
niḥśeṣadagdhapāśasya paśorasya hare tvayā
na stheyaṃ bandhakatvena śivājñāṃ śrāvayediti
dadyāt pūrṇāṃ vidhānena pratiṣṭhāpi viśodhitā
vidyāviśodhanavidhānaṃ
īśvara uvāca
sandhānamatha vidyāyāḥ prācīnakalayā saha
kurvīta pūrvavat kṛtvā tattvaṃ varṇaya tadyathā
oṃ hoṃ kṣīmiti sandhānaṃ
rāgś ca śuddhavidyā ca niyatiḥ kalayā saha
kālo mayā tathāvidyā tattvānāmiti saptakaṃ
ralavāḥ śaṣasāḥ varṇāḥ ṣaḍ vidyāyāṃ prakīrtitāḥ
padāni praṇavādīni ekaviṃśatisaṅkhyayā
oṃ namaḥ śivāya sarvaprabhave haṃ śivāya īśānamūrdhāya tatpuruṣavaktrāya aghorahṛdayāya vāmadevaguhyāya sadyojātamūrtaye oṃ namo namo guhyātiguhyāya goptre anidhāya sarvādhipāya jyotirūpāya prameśvārāya bhavena oṃ vyoma
oṃ rudrāṇāṃ bhuvanānāñca svarūpamatha kaśyape
vaṭuḥ praśāntanāmā ca paramākṣarasañjñakaḥ
adṛṣṭarūpanāmānau tathānyo rūpavardhanaḥ
kalyāṇa iti vijñeyāḥ pañcaviṃśatisaṅkhyayā
pūṣā ca hastijihvā ca vyānanāgau prabhañjanau
viṣayo rūpamevaikamindriye pādacakṣuṣī
śabdaḥ sparśaś ca rūpañca traya ete guṇāḥ smṛtāḥ
tāḍanaṃ chedanaṃ tatra praveśañcāpi yojanaṃ
ākṛṣya grahaṇaṃ kuryādvidyayā hṛtpradeśataḥ
ātmanyāropya saṅgṛhya kalāṃ kuṇḍe niveśayet
rudraṃ kāraṇamāvāhya vijñāpya ca śiśuṃ prati
pitrorāvahanaṃ kṛtvā hṛdaye tāḍayecchiśuṃ
ākṛṣyādāya pūrvoktavidhināatmani yojayet
vāmayā yojayet yonau gṛhītvā dvādaśāntataḥ
niḥśeṣamalakarmādipāśabandhanivṛttaye
niṣkṛtyaiva vidhānena yajeta śatamāhutīḥ
astreṇa pāśaśaithilyaṃ malaśaktiṃ tirohitāṃ
chedanaṃ mardanaṃ teṣāṃ vartulīkaraṇaṃ tathā
dāhaṃ tadakṣarābhāvaṃ prāyaścittamathoditaṃ
rudrāṇyāvāhanaṃ pūjā rūpagandhasamarpaṇaṃ
oṃ hrīṃ rūpagandhau śulkaṃ rudra gṛhāṇa svāhā
saṃśrāvya śāmbhavīmājñāṃ rudraṃ visṛjya kāraṇaṃ
vidhāyātmani caitanyaṃ pāśasūtre niveśayet
dadyāt pūrṇāṃ vidhānena samastavidhipūraṇīṃ
pūrvoktavidhinā kāryaṃ vidyāyāṃ tāḍanādikaṃ
svavījantu viśeṣaḥ syāditi vidyā viśodhitā
śāntiśodhanakathanaṃ
īśvara uvāca
sandadhyādadhunā vidyāṃ śāntyā sārdhaṃ yathāvidhi
śāntau tattvadvayaṃ līnaṃ bhāveśvarasadāśivau
hakāraś ca kṣakāraś ca dvau varṇau parikīrtitau
rudrāḥ samānanāmāno bhuvanaiḥ saha tadyathā
ghanau nirañjanākārau svaśivau dīptikāraṇau
tridaśeśvaranāmā ca tridaśaḥ kālasajjñakaḥ
sūkṣmāmbujeśvaraśceti rudrāḥ śāntau pratiṣṭhitāḥ
vyomavyāpine vyomavyāpyarūpāya sarvavyāpine śivāya anantāya anāthāya anāśritāya dhruvāya śāśvatāya yogapīṭhasaṃsthitāya nityayogine dhyānāhārāyeti dvādaśapādāni
alambuṣāyasānāḍyau vāyū kṛkarakarmakau
guṇau sparśaninādau dvāvekaḥ kāraṇamīśvaraḥ
vidadhyāttāḍanaṃ bhedaṃ praveśañca viyojanaṃ
ākṛṣya grahaṇaṃ kuryācchāntervadanasūtrataḥ
ātmanyāropya saṅgṛhya kalāṃ kuṇḍe niveśayet
īśaṃ tavādhikāre 'smin mumukṣuṃ dīkṣayāmyahaṃ
bhavyaṃ tvayānukūlena kuryāt vijñāpanāmiti
āvāhanādikaṃ pitroḥ śiṣyasya tāḍanādikaṃ
pūrvavat pitṛsaṃyogaṃ bhāvayitvodbhavākhyayā
śikhayā vādhikārāya bhogāya kavacāṇunā
layāya śastramantreṇa śrotaḥśuddhau śivena ca
tattvaśuddhau hṛdā hy evaṃ garbhādhānādi pūrvavat
varmaṇā pāśaśaithilyaṃ niṣkṛtyaivaṃ śataṃ japet
chindyādastreṇa kartaryā pāśānvījavatā yathā
oṃ hauṃ śāntikalāpāśāya haḥ hūṃ phaṭ
visṛjya vartulīkṛtya pāśamantreṇa pūrvavat
ghṛtapūrṇe śruve datvā kalāstreṇaiva homayet
astreṇa juhuyāt pañca pāśāṅkuśanivṛttaye
prāyaścittaniṣedhāya dadyādaṣṭāhutīratha
oṃ haḥ astrāya hūṃ phaṭ
hṛdeśvaraṃ samāvāhya kṛtvā pūjanatarpaṇe
oṃ hāṃ īśvara buddhyahaṅkārau śulkaṃ gṛhāṇa svāhā
niḥśeṣadagdhapāśasya paśorasyeśvara tvayā
na stheyaṃ bandhakatvena śivājñāṃ śrāvayediti
visṛjedīśvarandevaṃ raudrātmānaṃ niyojayet
dadyāt mūlena śiṣyasya śirasyamṛtavindukaṃ
dadyāt pūrṇāṃ vidhānajño niḥśeṣavidhipūraṇīṃ
asyāmapi vidhātavyaṃ pūrvavattāḍanādiakaṃ
svavījantu viśeṣaḥ syācchuddhiḥ śānterapīḍitā
nirvāṇadīkṣākathanaṃ
īśvara uvāca
sandhānaṃ śāntyatītāyāḥ śāntyā sārdhaṃ viśuddhayā
oṃ hīṃ kṣauṃ hauṃ hāṃ iti sandhānāni
vyomarūpamanāthañca syādanāśritanaṣṭamaṃ
oṅkārapadamīśāne mantro varṇāś ca ṣoḍaśa
akārādivisargāntā vījena dehakārakau
kuhūś ca śaṅkhinī nāḍyau devadattadhanañjayau
śabdo guṇo 'syāvasthā tu turyātītā tu pañcamī
hetuḥ sadāśivo deva iti tattvādisañcayaṃ
sañcintya śāntyatītākhyaṃ vidadhyāttāḍanādikaṃ
kalāpāśaṃ samātāḍya phaḍantena vibhidya ca
śikhāhṛtsampuṭībhūtaṃ svāhāntaṃ sṛṇimudrayā
pūrakeṇa samākṛṣya pāśaṃ mastakasūtrataḥ
asyāḥ pūjādikaṃ sarvaṃ nivṛtteriva sādhayet
sadāśivaṃ samāvāhya pūjayitvā pratarpya ca
sadā khyāte 'dhikāre 'smin mumukṣuṃ dīkṣayāmyahaṃ
bhāvyaṃ tvayānukūlena bhaktyā vijñāpayediti
pitrorāvāhanaṃ pūjāṃ kṛtvā tarpaṇasannidhī
hṛtsampuṭātmavījena śiṣyaṃ vakṣasi tāḍayet
oṃ hāṃ hūṃ haṃ phaṭ
śastreṇa pāśasaṃyuktaṃ jyeṣṭhayāṅkuśamudrayā
oṃ hāṃ hūṃ haṃ phaṭ
svāhāntena tadākṛṣya tenaiva puṭitātmanā
oṃ hāṃ haṃ hīṃ ātmane namaḥ
pūrvavat pitṛsaṃyogaṃ bhāvayitvodbhavākhyayā
garbhādhānādikaṃ sarvaṃ pūrvoktavidhinā caret
mūlena pāśaśaithilye niṣkṛtyaiva śataṃ japet
malaśaktitirodhāne pāśānāñca viyojane
pañcapañcāhutīrdadyādāyudhena yathā purā
pāśānāyudhamantreṇa sapravārābhijaptayā
chindyādastreṇa kartaryā kalāvījayujā yathā
oṃ hāṃ śāntyatītakalāpāśāya haḥ hūṃ phaṭ
visṛjya vartulīkṛtya pāśānastreṇa pūrvavat
ghṛtapūrṇe śruve datvā kalāstreṇaiva homayet
astreṇa juhuyāt pajca pāśāṅkuśanivṛttaye
prāyaścittaniṣedhārthaṃ dadyādaṣṭāhutīstataḥ
sadāśivaṃ hṛdāvāhya kṛtvā pūjanatarpaṇe
oṃ hāṃ sadāśiva manovindu śulkaṃ gṛhāṇa svāhā
niḥśeṣadagdhapāśasya paśorasya sadāśiva
bandhāya na tvayā stheyaṃ śivājñāṃ śrāvayediti
mūlena juhuyāt pūrṇāṃ visṛjettu sadāśivaṃ
dadyādāpyāyanāyāsya mastake 'rghyāmbuvindukaṃ
kheditau śiṣyadīkṣāyai yanmayā pitarau yuvāṃ
kāruṇyanānmokṣayitvā tadvraja tvaṃ sthānamātmanaḥ
śikhāmantritakartaryā bodhaśaktisvarūpiṇīṃ
śikhāṃ chidyācchivāstreṇa śiṣyasya caturaṅgulāṃ
oṃ klīṃ śikhāyai hūṃ phaṭ oṃ haḥ astrāya hūṃ phaṭ
sruci tāṃ ghṛtapūrṇāyāṃ goviḍgolakamadhyagāṃ
saṃvidhāyāstramantreṇa hūṃ phaḍantena homayet
oṃ hauṃ haḥ astrāya hūṃ phaṭ
prakṣālya sruksruvau śiṣyaṃ saṃsnāpyācamya ca svayaṃ
yojanikāsthānamātmānaṃ śastramantreṇa tāḍayet
viyojyākṛṣya sampūjya pūrvavad dvādaśāntataḥ
ātmīyahṛdayāmbhojakarṇikāyāṃ niveśayet
pūritaṃ śruvamājyena vihitādhomukhaśrucā
prasāritaśirogrīvo nādoccārānusārataḥ
samadṛṣṭiśivaścāntaḥ parabhāvasamanvitaḥ
kumbhamaṇḍalavahnibhyaḥ śiṣyādapi nijātmanaḥ
gṛhītvā ṣaḍvidhavidhānaṃ śrugagre prāṇanāḍikaṃ
hṛdayādikramoccāravisṛṣṭaṃ mantrasañjñakaṃ
pūrakaṃ kumbhakaṃ kṛtvā vyādāya vadanaṃ manāk
suṣumṇānugataṃ nādasvarūpantu tṛtīyakaṃ
saptame kāraṇe tyāgātpraśāntavikharaṃ layaḥ
tatkālavikharaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ śaktyatītañca saptamaṃ
pūrakaṃ kumbhakaṃ kṛtvā vyādāya vadanaṃ manāk
śanair udīrayan mūlaṃ kṛtvā śiṣyātmano layaṃ
hakāre taḍidākāre ṣaḍadhvajaprāṇarūpiṇi
ukāraṃ parato nābhervitastiṃ vyāpya saṃsthitaṃ
tataḥ paraṃ makārantu hṛdayāccaturaṅgulaṃ
oṅkāraṃ vācakaṃ viṣṇostato 'ṣṭāṅgulakaṇṭhakaṃ
caturaṅgulatālusthaṃ makāraṃ rudravācakaṃ
tadvallalāṭamadhyasthaṃ vindumīśvaravācakaṃ
nādaṃ sadāśivaṃ devaṃ brahmarandhrāvasānakaṃ
divyaṃ pipīlikāsparśaṃ tasminnevānubhūya ca
bhāvaśūnye mano 'tīte śive nityaguṇodaye
vilīya mānase tasmin śiṣyātmānaṃ vibhāvayet
vimuñcan sarpiṣo dhārāṃ jvālānte 'pi pare śive
yojanikāsthiratvāya vauṣaḍantaśivāṇunā
datvā pūrṇāṃ vidhānena guṇāpadānamacaret
oṃ hāṃ ātmane sarvajño bhava svāhā oṃ hāṃ ātmane paritṛpto bhava svāhā oṃ hrūṃ ātmane anādibodho bhava svāhā oṃ hauṃ ātmane svatantro bhava svāhā oṃ hauṃ ātman aluptaśaktirbhava svāhā oṃ haḥ ātmane anantaśaktirbhava svāhā
itthaṃ ṣaḍguṇamātmānaṃ gṛhītvā paramākṣarāt
tīvrāṇuśaktisampātajanitaśramaśāntaye
praṇamayyeśakumbhādīn śivāddakṣiṇamaṇḍale
saumyavaktraṃ vyavasthāpya śiṣyaṃ dakṣiṇamātmanaḥ
tvayaivānugṛhīto 'yaṃ mūrtimāsthāya māmakīṃ
iti vijñāpya deveśaṃ praṇamya ca guruḥ svayaṃ
śreyastavāstviti brūyādāśiṣaṃ śiṣyamādarāt
tataḥ paramayā bhaktyā datvā deve 'ṣṭapuṣpikāṃ
ekatattvadīkṣākathanaṃ
īśvara uvāca
athaikatāttvikī dīkṣā laghutvādupadiśyate
sūtrabandhādi kurvīta yathāyogaṃ nijātmanā
kālāgnyādiśivāntāni tattvāni parabhāvayet
samatattve samagrāṇi sūtre maṇigaṇāniva
āvāhya śivatattvādi garbhādhānādi pūrvavat
pradadīta tataḥ pūrṇāṃ tattvavātopagarbhitāṃ
yojanāyai śive cānyāṃ sthiratvāpādanāya ca
datvā pūrṇāṃ prakurvīta śivakumbhābhiṣecanaṃ
abhiṣekādikathanaṃ
īśvara uvāca
śivamabhyarcyābhiṣekaṃ kuryācchiṣyādike śriye
kumbhānīśādikāṣṭhāsu kramaśo nava vinyaset
teṣu kṣārodaṃ kṣīrodaṃ dadhyudaṃ ghṛtasāgaraṃ
ikṣukādambarīsvādumastūdānaṣṭasāgarān
niveśayed yathāsaṅkhyamaṣṭau vidyeśvarānatha
ekaṃ śikhaṇḍinaṃ rudraṃ śrīkaṇṭhantu dvitīyakaṃ
saptamaṃ sūkṣmanāmānamanantaṃ rudramaṣṭamaṃ
yāgālayān digīśasya racite snānamaṇḍape
kuryāt karadvayāyāmāṃ vedīmaṣṭāṅgulocchritāṃ
śrīparṇādyāsane tatra vinyasyānantamānasaṃ
śiṣyaṃ niveśya pūrvāsyaṃ sakalīkṛtya pūjayet
kṣārodānukrameṇātha hṛdā vidyeśaśambaraiḥ
kalasaiḥ snāpayecchiṣyaṃ svadhādhāraṇayānvitaṃ
pūrvoditāsane śiṣyaṃ punaḥ pūrvavadarcayet
uṣṇīṣaṃ yogapaṭṭañca mukuṭaṃ kartarīṃ ghaṭīṃ
akṣamālāṃ pustakādi śivakādyadhikārakaṃ
dīkṣāvyākhyāpratiṣṭhādyaṃ jñātvādyaprabhṛti tvayā
suparīkṣya vidhātavyamājñāṃ saṃśrāvayediti
abhivādya tataḥ śiṣyaṃ praṇipatya maheśvaraṃ
vighnajvālāpanodārthaṃ kuryādvijñāpanāṃ yathā
abhiṣekārthamādiṣṭastvayāhaṃ gurumūrtinā
saṃhitāpāragaḥ so 'yamabhiṣikto mayā śiva
dadyāt pūrṇāṃ tataḥ śiṣyaṃ sthāpayennijadakṣiṇe
śiṣyadakṣiṇapāṇisthā aṅguṣṭhādyaṅgulīḥ kramāt
kusumāni kare datvā praṇāmaṃ kārayedamuṃ
anugrāhyāstvayā śiṣyāḥ śāstreṇa suparīkṣitāḥ
bhūpavanmānavādīnāmabhiṣekādabhīpsitaṃ
āṃ śrāṃ śrauṃ paśuṃ hūṃ phaḍiti astrarājābhiṣekataḥ
īśvara uvāca
abhiṣiktaḥ śivaṃ viṣṇuṃ pūjayedbhāskarādikān
śaṅkhabheryādinirghoṣaiḥ snāpayet pañcagavyakaiḥ
varṣakoṭisahasreṣu yat pāpaṃ smupārjitaṃ
ghṛtābhyaṅgena devānāṃ bhasmībhavati pāvake
āḍhakena ghṛtādyaiś ca devān snāpya suro bhavet
atītānāgatajñānamantradhībhuktimuktidāḥ
gṛhītvā praśnasūkṣmārṇe hṛte dvābhyāṃ śubhāśubhaṃ
tribhirjīvo mūladhātuś caturbhirbrāhmaṇādidhīḥ
yañcādau bhūtatattvādi śeṣe caivaṃ japādikaṃ
aśubhaṃ madhyamaṃ madhyeṣvindrastriṣu nṛpaḥ śubhaḥ
saṅkhyāvṛnde jīvitābdaṃ yamo 'bdadaśahā dhruvaṃ
sūryebhāsyeśadurgāśrīviṣṇumantrair likhet kaje
kaṭhinyā japtayā spṛṣṭe gomūtrākṛtirekhayā
ārabhyaikaṃ trikaṃ yāvattricatuṣkāvasānakaṃ
marud vyoma marudvījaiś catuḥṣaṣṭipade tathā
akṣāṇāṃ patanāt sparśādviṣamādau śubhādikaṃ
ekatrikādimārabhya ante cāṣṭatrikaṃ tathā
dhvajādyāyāḥ samā hīnā viṣamāḥ śobhanādidāḥ
āipallavitaiḥ kādyaiḥ ṣoḍaśasvarapūrvagaiḥ
ādyaistaiḥ sasvaraiḥ kādyaistripurānāmamantrakāḥ
hrīṃ vījāḥ praṇavādyāḥspur namo 'ntā yatra pūjane
mantrā viṃśatisāhasrāḥ śataṃ ṣaṣṭhyadhikaṃ tataḥ
āṃ hrīṃ mantrāḥ sarasvatyāś caṇḍikāyāstathaiva ca
tathā gauryāś ca durgāyā āṃ śrīṃ mantrāḥ śriyas tathā
tathākṣauṃ krauṃ mantrāḥ sūryasya āṃ hauṃ mantrāḥ śivasya ca
āṃ gaṃ mantrā gaṇeśasya āṃ mantrāś ca tathā hareḥ
śatārdhaikādhikaiḥ kādyais tathā ṣoḍaśabhiḥ kharaiḥ
kādyaistaiḥ sasvaraisādyaiḥ kāntair mantrās tathākhilāḥ
ravīśadevīviṣṇūnāṃ svābdhidevendravartanāt
śatatrayaṃ ṣaṣṭyadhikaṃ pratyekaṃ maṇḍalaṃ kramāt
abhiṣikto japed dhyāyecchiṣyādīn dīkṣayedguruḥ
pratiṣṭhāvidhikathanaṃ
īśvara uvāca
pratiṣṭhāṃ sampravakṣyāmi kramāt saṅkṣepato guha
pīṭhaṃ śaktiṃ śivo liṅgaṃ tadyogaḥ sā śivāṇubhiḥ
pratiṣṭhāyāḥ pañca bhedāsteṣāṃ rūpaṃ vadāmi te
yatra brahmaśilāyogaḥ sā pratiṣṭhā viśeṣataḥ
sthāpanantu yathāyogaṃ pīṭha eva niveśanaṃ
utthāpanañca sā proktā liṅgoddhārapuraḥsarā
yasyāṃ tu liṅgamāropya saṃskāraḥ kriyate budhaiḥ
āthāpanaṃ taduddiṣṭaṃ dvidhā viṣṇvādikasya ca
āsu sarvāsu caitanyaṃ niyuñjīta paraṃ śivam
yadādhārādibhedena prāsādeṣvapi pañcadhā
parīkṣamatha medinyāḥ kuryātprāsādakāmyayā
pītā kṛṣṇā surāgandhā viprādīnāṃ mahī kramāt
pūrveśottarasarvatra pūrvā caiṣāṃ viśiṣyate
ākhāte hāstike yasyāḥ pūrṇe mṛdadhikā bhavet
uttamāntāṃ mahīṃ vidyāttoyādyair vā samukṣitāṃ
asthyaṅgārādibhirduṣṭāmatyantaṃ śodhayed guruḥ
nagaragrāmadurgārthaṃ gṛhaprāsādakāraṇaṃ
khananair gokulāvāsaiḥ karṣaṇair vā muhurmuhuḥ
maṇḍape dvārapūjādi mantratṛptyavasānakaṃ
samīkṛtyopaliptāyāṃ bhūmau saṃśodhayeddiśaḥ
svarṇadadhyakṣatai rekhāḥ prakurvīta pradakṣiṇaṃ
madhyādīśānakoṣṭasthe pūrṇakumbhe śivaṃ yajet
bāhye rakṣogaṇāniṣṭvā vidhinā digbalaṃ kṣipet
bhūmiṃ saṃsicya saṃsnāpya kuddālādyaṃ prapūjayet
nidhāya gītavādyādibrahmagoṣasamākulaṃ
pūjāṃ kumbhe samāhṛtya prāpte lagne 'gnikoṣṭhake
nairṛtyāṃ kṣepayenmṛtsnāṃ khāte kumbhajalaṃ kṣipet
siñcan sīmantacihnāni yāvadīśānagocaraṃ
karkarāntaṃ jalāntaṃ vā śalyadoṣajighāṃsayā
khānayed bhūḥ kumārīṃ ced vidhinā śalyamuddharet
akacaṭatapayaśahān mānavaścet praśnākṣarāṇi tu
agnerdhvajādipātitāḥ svasthāne śalyamākhyānti
kartuścāṅgavikāreṇa jānīyāttatpramāṇataḥ
paśvādīnāṃ praveśena kīrtanair virutair diśaḥ
mātṛkāmaṣṭavargāḍhyāṃ phalake bhuvi vā likhet
śalyajñānaṃ vargavaśāt pūrvādīśāntataḥ kramāt
yavarge śavakītādi śavarge lohamādiśet
prīkṣyātmabhiḥ karāpūrair aṣṭāṅgulamṛdantaraiḥ
pādonaṃ khātamāpūrya sajalair mudgarāhataiḥ
liptāṃ samaplavāṃ tatra kārayitvā bhuvaṃ guruḥ
sāmānyārghyakaro yāyānmaṇḍapaṃ vakṣyāmāṇakaṃ
toraṇadvāḥpatīniṣṭvā pratyagdvāreṇa saṃviśet
kuryāttatrātmaśuddhyādi kuṇḍamaṇḍapasaṃskṛtiṃ
kalasaṃ vardhanīsaktaṃ lokapālaśivārcanaṃ
yajamānānvito yāyācchilānāṃ snānamaṇḍapaṃ
śilāḥ prāsādaliṅgasya pādadharmādisañjñakāḥ
aṣṭāṅgulocchritāḥ śastāś caturasrāḥ karāyatāḥ
pāṣāṇānāṃ śilāḥ kāryā iṣṭakānāṃ tadardhataḥ
prāsāde 'śmaśilāḥ śaile iṣṭakā iṣṭakāmaye
aṅkitā navavaktrādyaiḥ paṅkajāḥ paṅkajāṅkitāḥ
nandā bhadrā jayā riktā pūrṇākhyā pañcamī matā
āsāṃ padmo mahāpadmaḥ śaṅkho 'tha makaras tathā
samudraśceti pañcāmī nidhikumbhāḥ kramādhaḥ
nandā bhadrā jayā pūrṇā ajitā cāparājitā
vijayā maṅgalākhyā ca dharaṇī navamī śilā
navānāntu yathāsaṅkhyaṃ nidhikumbhaḥ pūrṇastathottaraḥ
āsanaṃ prathamaṃ dattvā tāḍyollikhya śarāṇunā
sarvāsāmaviśeṣeṇa tanutreṇāvaguṇṭhanaṃ
mṛdbhirgomayayogāmūtrakaṣāyair gandhavāriṇā
astreṇa hūṃ phaḍantena malasnānaṃ samācaret
vidhinā pañcagavyena snānaṃ pañcāmṛtena ca
gandhatoyāntaraṃ kuryānnijanāmāṅkitāṇunā
phalaratnasuvarṇānāṃ gośṛṅgasalilaistataḥ
svarṇotthamāsanaṃ datvā nītvā yāgaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ
śayyāyāṃ kuśatalpe vā hṛdayena niveśayet
tanmātrādau dharānte ca śivavidyātmanāṃ sthitiḥ
tattvāni nijamantreṇa tattveśāṃś ca hṛdārcayet
sthāneṣu puṣpamālādicihniteṣu yathākramaṃ
oṃ hūṃ śivatattvāya namaḥ oṃ hūṃ śivatattvādhipataye rudrāya namaḥ oṃ hāṃ vidyātattvāya namaḥ oṃ hāṃ vidyātattvādhipāya viṣṇave namaḥ oṃ hāṃ ātmatattvāya namaḥ oṃ hāṃ ātmatattvādhipataye brahmaṇe namaḥ
kṣamāgniyajamānārkān jalavātendukhāni ca
pratitattvaṃ nyasedaṣṭau mūrtīḥ pratiśilāṃ śilāṃ
mahādevaṃ ca bhīmaṃ ca mūrtīśāṃś ca yathākramāt
oṃ dharāmūrtaye namaḥ oṃ dharādhipataye namaḥ
ityādimantrān lokapālān yathāsaṅkhyaṃ nijāṇubhiḥ
indrādīnāṃ tu vījāni vakṣyamāṇakrameṇa tu
lūṃ rūṃ śūṃ pūṃ vūṃ yūṃ mūṃ hūṃ kṣūmiti
ukto navaśilāpakṣaḥ śilā pañcapadā tathā
pratitattvaṃ nyasenmūrtīḥ sṛṣṭyā pañca dharādikāḥ
brahmā viṣṇus tathā rudra īśvaraś ca sadāśivaḥ
ete ca pañca mūrtīśā yaṣṭavyāstāsu pūrvavat
oṃ pṛthvīmūrtaye namaḥ oṃ pṛthvīmūrtyadhipataye brahmaṇe namaḥ ity ādi mantrāḥ
sampūjya kalaśān pañca krameṇa nijanāmabhiḥ
kuṇḍeṣu dhārikāṃ śaktiṃ vinyasyābhyarcya tarpayet
tattvatattvādhipān mūrtīrmūrtīśāṃś ca ghṛtādibhiḥ
tato brahmāṃśaśuddhyarthaṃ mūlāṅgaṃ brahmabhiḥ kramāt
kṛtvā śatādipūrṇāntaṃ prokṣyāḥ śāntijalaiḥ śilāḥ
pūjayecca kuśaiḥ spṛṣṭvā pratitattvamanukramāt
sāṃnidhyamatha sandhānaṃ kṛtvā śuddhaṃ punarnyaset
oṃ āṃ īṃ ātmatattvavidyātattvābhyāṃ namaḥ iti
saṃspṛśed darbhamūlādyair brahmāṅgāditrayaṃ kramāt
oṃ hāṃ uṃ vidyātattvaśivatattvābhyāṃ namaḥ
ghṛtena madhunā pūrṇāṃstāmrakumbhān saratnakān
śilānāmatha sarvāsāṃ saṃsmaredadhidaivatāḥ
vidyārūpāḥ kṛtasnānā hemavārṇāḥ śilāmbarāḥ
nyūnādidoṣamoṣārthaṃ vāstubhūmeś ca śuddhaye
yajedastreṇa mūrdhāntamāhutīnāṃ śataṃ śataṃ
vāstupūjādividhānam
īśvara uvāca
tataḥ prāsādamāsūtrya vartayedvāstumaṇḍapaṃ
kuryāt koṣṭhacatuḥṣaṣṭiṃ kṣetre vedāsrake same
koṇeṣu vinyased vaṃśau rajjavo 'ṣṭau vikoṇagāḥ
dvipadāḥ ṣaṭpadāstāstu vāstuntatrārcayed yathā
ākuñcitakacaṃ vāstumuttānamasurākṛtiṃ
smaret pūjāsu kuḍyādiniveśe uttarānanaṃ
jānunī kūrparau śakthi diśi vātahutāśayoḥ
paitryāṃ pādapuṭe raudryāṃ śiro 'sya hṛdaye 'ñjaliḥ
asya dehe samārūḍhā devatāḥ pūjitāḥ śubhāḥ
aṣṭau koṇādhipāstatra koṇārdheṣvaṣṭasu sthitāḥ
ṣaṭpadāstu marīcyādyā dikṣu pūrvādiṣu kramāt
madhye catuṣpado brahmā śeṣāstu padikāḥ smṛtāḥ
samastanāḍīsaṃyoge mahāmarmānujaṃ phalaṃ
trikuṭuṃ maṇibandhaṃ ca suviśuddhaṃ padaṃ tathā
iti dvādaśa marmāṇi vāstorbhittyādiṣu tyajet
sājyamakṣatamīśāya parjanyāyāmbujodakaṃ
dadītātha jayantāya patākāṃ kuṅkumojjvalāṃ
satyāya ghṛtagodhūmamājyabhaktaṃ bhṛśāya ca
vimāṃsamantarīkṣāya śuktuntebhyastu pūrvataḥ
madhukṣīrājyasampūrṇāṃ pradadyādvahnaye śrucaṃ
lājān pūrṇaṃ suvarṇāmbu vitathāya nivedayet
dadyād gṛhakṣate kṣaudraṃ yamarāje palaudanaṃ
gandhaṃ gandharvanāthāya jihvāṃ bhṛṅgāya pakṣiṇaḥ
mṛgāya padmaparṇāni yāmyāmityaṣṭadevatāḥ
pitre tilodakaṃ kṣīraṃ vṛkṣajaṃ dantadhāvanaṃ
sugrīvāya diśet pūpān puṣpadantāya darbhakaṃ
ghṛtaṃ guḍaudanaṃ śeṣe rogāya ghṛtamaṇḍakān
lājān vā paścimāśāyāṃ devāṣṭakamitīritaṃ
mārutāya dhvajaṃ pītaṃ nāgāya nāgakeśaraṃ
mukhye bhakṣyāṇi bhallāṭe mudgasūpaṃ susaṃskṛtaṃ
somāya pāyasaṃ sājyaṃ śālūkamūṣaye diśet
modakān brahmaṇaḥ prācyāṃ ṣaṭpādāya marīcaye
savitre raktapuṣpāṇi vahnyadhaḥkoṇakoṣṭhake
tadadhaḥkoṣṭhake dadyāt sāvitryai ca kuśodakaṃ
dakṣiṇe candanaṃ raktaṃ ṣaṭpadāya vivasvate
haridraudanamindrāya rakṣodhaḥkrīṇakoṣṭhake
varuṇyāṃ ṣaṭpadāsīne mitre saṅuḍamodanaṃ
rudrāya ghṛtasiddhānnaṃ vāyukoṇādhare pade
dadīta māṣanaivedyaṃ ṣaṭpadasthe dharādhare
āpāya śivakoṇādhaḥ tadvatsāya ca tatsthale
kramāddadyāddadhikṣīraṃ pūjayitvā vidhānataḥ
catuṣpade niviṣṭāya brahmaṇe madhmadeśataḥ
pañcagavyākṣatopetañcaruṃ sājyaṃ nivedayet
īśādivāyuparyantakoṇeṣvatha yathākramaṃ
vāstuvāhye carakyādyāś catasraḥ pūjayed yathā
carakyai saghṛtaṃ māṃsaṃ vidāryai dadhipaṅkaje
tato māṣaudanaṃ prācyāṃ skandāya vinivedayet
aryamṇe dakṣiṇāśāyāṃ pūpān kṛsarayā yutān
jambhakāya ca vāruṇyāmāmiṣaṃ rudhirānvitaṃ
udīcyāṃ pilipiñjāya raktānnaṃ kusumāni ca
yajedvā sakalaṃ vāstuṃ kuśadadhyakṣaterjalaiḥ
tripadā rajjavaḥ kāryāḥ ṣaṭpadāś ca vikoṇake
īśādyāḥ pādikāstasminnāgadyāś ca dvikoṣṭhagāḥ
ṣaṭpadasthā marīcyādyā brahmā navapadaḥ smṛtaḥ
nagaragrāmakheṭādau vāstuḥ śatapado 'pi vā
vaṃśadvayaṃ koṇagataṃ durjayaṃ durdharaṃ sadā
grahāḥ skandādayastatra vijñeyāś caiva ṣaṭpadāḥ
carakyādyā bhūtapadā rajjuvaṃśādi pūrvavat
catuḥṣaṣṭipado brahmā marīcyādyāś ca devatāḥ
catuḥpañcāśatpadikā āpādyaṣṭau rasāgnibhiḥ
īśānādyā navapadāḥ skandādyāḥ śaktikāḥ smṛtāḥ
jñeyo vaṃśasahasraistu vāstumaṇḍalagaḥ padaiḥ
pañcaciṃśatpado vāsturvaitālākhyaścitau smṛtaḥ
anyo navapado vāstuḥ ṣoḍaśāṅghris tathāparaḥ
khāte vāstoḥ samaṃ pṛṣṭhe nyāse brahmaśilātmake
śāṣākasya niveśe ca mūrtisaṃsthāpane tathā
pāyasena tu naivedyaṃ sarveṣāṃ vā pradāpayet
uktānukte tu vai vāstuḥ pañcahastapramāṇataḥ
gṛhaprāsādamānena vāstuḥ śreṣṭhastu sarvadā
śilāvinyāsavidhānaṃ
īśvara uvāca
īśādiṣu carakyādyāḥ pūrvavat pūjayedvahiḥ
datvā bhūtabaliṃ lagne śilānyāsamanukramāt
nakārārūḍhamūlena kumbhe 'smin dhārayecchilāṃ
kumbhānaṣṭau sabhadrādīn dikṣu pūrvādiṣu kramāt
lokapālāṇubhirnyasya śvabhreṣu nyastaśaktiṣu
śilāsteṣvatha nandādyāḥ krameṇa viniyojayet
śambarair mūrtināthānāṃ yathā syurbhittimadhyataḥ
tāsu dharmādikānaṣṭau koṇāt koṇaṃ vibhāgaśaḥ
subhadrādiṣu nandādyāś catasro 'gnyādikoṇagāḥ
ajitādyāś ca pūrvādijayādiṣvatha vinyaset
brahmāṇaṃ copari masya vyāpakaṃ ca maheśvaraṃ
śilāpañcakapakṣe 'pi manāguddiśyate yathā
madhye pūrṇaśilānyāsaḥ subhadrakalaśe 'rdhataḥ
padmādiṣu ca nandādyāḥ koṇeṣvagnyādiṣu kramāt
oṃ pūrṇe tvaṃ mahāviśve sarvasandohalakṣaṇe
sarvasampūrṇamevātra kuruṣvāṅgirasaḥ sute
oṃ nande tvaṃ nandinī puṃsāṃ tvāmatra sthāpayāmyahaṃ
prāsāde tiṣṭha santṛptā yāvaccandrārkatārakaṃ
āyuḥ kāmaṃ śriyannande dehi vāsiṣṭha dehināṃ
asmin rakṣā sadā kāryā prāsāde yatnatastvayā
oṃ bhadre tvaṃ sarvadā bhadraṃ lokānāṃ kuru kāśyapi
āyurdā kāmadā devi śrīpradā ca sadā bhava
oṃ jaye 'tra sarvadā devi śrīdāayurdā ca sadā bhava
oṃ jaye 'tra sarvadā devi tiṣṭha tvaṃ sthāpitā maya
sarvadā sarvadeśasthe tiṣṭhāsmin viśvarūpiṇi
pratiṣṭhā sāmagrīvidhānaṃ
īśvara uvāca
vakṣye liṅgapratiṣṭhāṃ ca prāsāde bhuktimuktidāṃ
vinā caitreṇa māghādau pratiṣṭhā māsapañcake
śuklapakṣe viśeṣeṇa kṛṣṇe vā pañcamandinaṃ
caturthīṃ navamīṃ ṣaṣṭhīṃ varjayitvā caturdaśīṃ
śobhanāstithayaḥ śaṣāḥ krūravāravivarjitāḥ
śatabhiṣā dhaniṣṭhārdrā anurodhottaratrayaṃ
rohiṇī śravaṇaśceti sthirārambhe mahodayāḥ
lagnañca kumbhasiṃhālitulāstrīvṛṣadhanvināṃ
śasto jīvo navarkṣeṣu saptasthāneṣu sarvadā
budhaḥ ṣaḍaṣṭadiksaptaturyeṣu vinartuṃ śitaḥ
saptartutridaśādisthaḥ śaśāṅkobaladaḥ sadā
ravirdaśatriṣaṭsaṃstho rāhustridaśaṣaḍgataḥ
ṣaṭtristhānagatāḥ śastā mandāṅgārārkaketavaḥ
śubhrāḥ krūraś ca pāpāś ca sarva ekādaśasthitāḥ
eṣāṃ dṛṣṭirmunau pūrṇā tvārdhikī grahabhūtayoḥ
pādikī rāmadiksthāne caturaṣṭau pādavarjitā
pādānyūnacaturnāḍī bhogaḥ syānmīnameṣayoḥ
vṛṣakumbhau ca bhuñjāte catasraḥ pādavarjitāḥ
makaro mithunaṃ pañca cāpāliharikarkaṭāḥ
pādīnāḥ ṣaṭ tulākanye ghaṭikāḥ sārdhapañca ca
keśarī vṛṣabhaḥ kumbhaḥ sthirāḥ syuḥ siddhidāyakāḥ
carā dhanustulāmeṣā dviḥsvabhāvāstṛtīyakāḥ
śubhaḥ śubhagrahair dṛṣṭaḥ śasto lagnaḥ śubhāśritaḥ
rājyaṃ śauryaṃ balaṃ putrān yaśodharmādikaṃ bahu
tryekādaśacaturthasthā lagnāt pāpagrahāḥ śubhāḥ
dhāmnaḥ pañcaguṇāṃ bhūmiṃ tyaktvā vā dhānasammitāṃ
hastād dvādaśasopānāt kuryānmaṇḍamagrataḥ
ekāsyaṃ caturāsyaṃ vā raudryāṃ prācyuttarethavā
dvihastottarayā vṛddhyā śeṣaṃ syānmaṇḍapāṣṭakaṃ
vedīpādāntaraṃ tyaktvā kuṇḍāni nava pañca vā
ekaṃ vā śivakāṣṭhāyāṃ prācyāṃ vā tadguroḥ paraṃ
muṣṭimātraṃ śatārdhe syācchate cāratrimātrakaṃ
lakṣe catuṣkāraṃ kuṇḍaṃ koṭihome 'ṣṭahastakaṃ
ṣaḍasraṃ vāyave padmaṃ saumye cāṣṭāsrakaṃ śive
tiryakpātaśivaṃ khātamūrdhvaṃ mekhalayā saha
aṅgulaiḥ ṣaḍbhirekā vā kuṇḍākārāstu mekhalāḥ
tāsāmupari yoniḥ syānmadhye 'śvatthadalākṛtiḥ
ucchrāyeṇāṅgulaṃ tasmādvistāreṇāṅgulāṣṭakaṃ
dairghyaṃ kuṇḍārdhamānena kuṇḍakaṇṭhasamo 'dharaḥ
pūrvāgniyāmyakuṇḍānāṃ yoniḥ syāduttarānanā
pūrvānanā tu śeṣāṇāmaiśānye 'nyatarā tayoḥ
kuṇḍānāṃ yaś caturviṃśo bhāgaḥ soṅgula ity ataḥ
plakṣodumvarakāśvatthavaṭajāstoraṇāḥ kramāt
śāntibhūtibalārogyapūrvādyā nāmataḥ kramāt
indrāyudhopamā raktā kṛṣṇā dhūmrā śaśiprabhā
śuklābhā hemavarṇā ca patākā sphāṭikopamā
pañcahastāstadardhāś ca dhvajā dīrghāś ca vistarāḥ
hastapradeśitā daṇḍā dhvajānāṃ pañcahastakāḥ
valmīkāddantidantāgrāttathā vṛṣabhaśṛṅgataḥ
padmaṣaṇḍādvarāhāñca goṣṭhādapi catuṣpathāt
mṛttikā dvādaśa grāhyā vaikuṇṭheṣṭau pinākini
kaṣāyapañcakaṃ grāhyamārtavañca phalāṣṭakaṃ
tīrthāmbhāṃsi sugandhīni tathā sarvauṣadhījalaṃ
śastaṃ puṣpaphalaṃ vakṣye ratnagośṛṅgavāri ca
snānāyāpāharet pañca pañcagavyāmṛtaṃ tathā
sahasraśuṣiraṃ kumbhaṃ maṇḍalāya ca rocanā
śatamoṣadhimūlānāṃ vijayā lakṣmaṇā balā
guḍūcyatibalā pāṭhā sahadevā śatāvarī
ṛddhiḥ suvarcasā vṛddhiḥ snāne proktā pṛthak pṛthak
yavagodhūmavilvānāṃ cūrṇāni ca vicakṣaṇaḥ
vilepanaṃ sakarpūraṃ snānārthaṃ kumbhagaṇḍakān
khaṭvāñca tūlikāyugmaṃ sopadhānaṃ savastrakaṃ
ghṛtakṣaudrayutaṃ pātraṃ kuryāt svarṇaśalākikāṃ
vardhanīṃ śivakumbhañca lokapālaghaṭānapi
ekaṃ nidrākṛte kumbhaṃ śāntyarthaṃ kuṇḍasaṅkhyayā
dvārapālādidharmādipraśāntādighaṭānapi
vastulakṣmīgaṇeśānāṃ kalaśānaparānapi
dhānyapuñjakṛtādhārān savastrān sragvibhūṣitān
kumbhasaṇḍakāniti cha kumbhakhaṇḍakāniti ja
sahiraṇyān samālabdhān gandhapānīyapūritān
pūrṇapātraphalādhārān pallavādyān salakṣaṇān
vikirārthantathā lājān jñānakhaḍgañca pūrvavat
sāpidhānāṃ carusthālīṃ darvīṃ ca tāmranirmitāṃ
ghṛtakṣaudrānvitaṃ pātraṃ pādābhyaṅgakṛte tathā
viṣṭarāṃstriśatādarbhadalair bāhupramāṇakān
tilapātraṃ haviḥpātramardhapātraṃ pavitrakaṃ
phalaviṃśāṣṭamānāni ghaṭo dhūpapradānakaṃ
śrukśruvau piṭakaṃ pīṭhaṃ vyajanaṃ śuṣkamindhanaṃ
puṣpaṃ patraṃ gugglañca ghṛtair daupāṃś ca dhūpakaṃ
akṣatāni trisūtrīñca gavyamājyaṃ yavāṃstilān
kuśāḥ śāntyai trimadhuraṃ samidho daśaparvikāḥ
bāhumātraśruvaṃ hastam arkādigrahaśāntaye
samidho 'rkapalāśotthāḥ khādirāmārgapippalāḥ
udumvaraśamīdūrvākuśotthāḥ śatamaṣṭa ca
tadabhāve yavatilā gṛhopakaraṇaṃ tathā
sthālīdarvīpidhānādi devādibhyo 'ṃśukadvayaṃ
mudrāmukuṭavāsāṃsi hārakuṇḍalakaṅkaṇān
kuryādācāryapūjārthaṃ vittaśāṭhyaṃ vivarjayet
tatpādapādahīnā ca mūrtibhṛdastrajāpināṃ
pūjā syājjāpibhistulyā vipradaivajñaśilpināṃ
vajrārkaśāntau nīlātinīlamuktāphalāni ca
puṣpapadmādirāgañca vaidūryaṃ ratnamaṣṭamaṃ
uṣīramādhavakrāntāraktacandanakāguruṃ
śrīkhaṇḍaṃ sārikaṅkuṣṭhaṃ śaṅkṣinī hy oṣadhīguṇaḥ
hematāmramayaṃ raktaṃ rājatañca sakāṃsyakaṃ
śīsakañceti lohāni haritālaṃ manaḥśilā
gairikaṃ hemamākṣīkaṃ pārado vahnigairikaṃ
godhūmān satilānmāṣānmudgānapyāharedyavān
nīvārān śyāmakānevaṃ brīhayo 'pyaṣṭa kīrtitāḥ
īśvara uvāca
snātvā nityadvayaṃ kṛtvā praṇavārghakaro guruḥ
kṣāntyāditoraṇāṃstatra pūrvavat pūjayet kramāt
pradakṣiṇakramādeṣāṃ śākhāyāṃ dvārapālakān
prāci nandimahākālau yāmye bhṛṅgivināyakau
vāruṇe vṛṣabhaskandau devīcaṇḍau tatottare
tacchākhāmūladeśasthau praśāntaśiśirau ghaṭau
parjanyāśokanāmānau bhūtaṃ sañjīvanāmṛtau
bhānutrayaṃ yugaṃ vedo lakṣmīrgaṇapatis tathā
iti devāmakhāgāre tiṣṭhanti pratitoraṇaṃ
vighnasaṅghāpanodāya kratoḥ saṃrakṣaṇāya ca
vajraṃ śaktiṃ tathā daṇḍaṃ khaḍgaṃ pāśaṃ dhvajaṃ gadāṃ
oṃ hrūṃ phaṭ namaḥ oṃ hrūṃ phaṭ dvāḥsthaśaktaye hrūṃ phaṭ namaḥ ity ādimantraiḥ
kumudaḥ kumudākṣaś ca puṇḍarīkotha vāmanaḥ
śaṅkukarṇaḥ sarvanetraḥ sumukhaḥ supratiṣṭhitaḥ
dhvajāṣṭadevatāḥ pūjyāḥ pūrvādau bhūtakoṭibhiḥ
kālaṃ karālinaṃ ṣaṣṭhamekāṅghrimbhīmamaṣṭakaṃ
kambalāstṛteṣu varṇeṣu vaṃśasthūṇāsvanukramāt
sadāśivapadavyāpi maṇḍapaṃ dhāma śāṅkaraṃ
patākāśaktisaṃyuktaṃ tattvadṛṣṭyāvalokayet
divyāntarikṣabhūmiṣṭhavighnānutsārya pūrvavat
praviśet paścimadvārā śeṣadvārāṇi darśayet
pradakṣiṇakramādgatvā niviṣṭovedidakṣiṇe
uttarābhimukhaḥ kuryād bhūtaśuddhiṃ yathā purā
antaryāgaṃ viśeṣārghyaṃ mantradravyādiśodhanaṃ
kurvīta ātmanaḥ pūjāṃ pañcagavyādi pūrvavat
lalāṭaskandhapādāntaṃ śivavidyātmakaṃ paraṃ
oṃ haṃ hāṃ
mūrtīstadīśvarāṃstatra pūrvavadviniveśayet
tadvyāpakaṃ śivaṃ sāṅgaṃ śivahastañca mūrdhani
ātmānaṃ mūrtipaiḥ sārdhaṃ sragvastrakusumādibhiḥ
bhūṣayitvā śivosmīti dhyātvā boghāsimuddharet
catuṣpadāntasaṃskāraiḥ saṃskuryānmakhamaṇḍapaṃ
āsanīkṛtya vardhanyāṃ vāstvādīn pūrvavadyajet
svadikṣu kalaśārūḍhāṃllokapālānanukramāt
vāhāyudhādisaṃyuktān pūjayedvidhinā yathā
airāvatagajārūḍhaṃ svarṇavarṇaṃ kirīṭinaṃ
sahasranayanaṃ śakraṃ vajrapāṇiṃ vibhāvayet
saptārciṣaṃ ca vibhrāṇamakṣamālāṃ kamaṇḍaluṃ
jvālāmālākulaṃ raktaṃ śaktihastamajāsanaṃ
mahiṣasthaṃ daṇḍahastaṃ yamaṃ kālānalaṃ smaret
raktanetraṃ svarārūḍhaṃ khaḍgahastañca nairṛtaṃ
varuṇaṃ makare śvetaṃ nāgapāśadharaṃ smaret
vāyuṃ ca hariṇe nīlaṃ kuveraṃ meghasaṃsthitaṃ
triśūlinaṃ vṛṣe ceśaṃ kūrmenantantu cakriṇaṃ
brāhmāṇaṃ haṃsagaṃ dhyāyeccaturvaktraṃ caturbhujaṃ
śivājñāṃ śrāvayet kumbhaṃ bhrāmayedātmapṛṣṭhagaṃ
śivaṃ sthirāsanaṃ kumbhe śastrārthañca dhruvāsanaṃ
pūjayitvā yathāpūrvaṃ spṛśedudbhavamudrayā
ebhiḥ saṃśrāvya rakṣārthaṃ kumbhe khaḍgaṃ niveśayet
dīkṣāsthāpanayoḥ kumbhe sthaṇḍile maṇḍale 'thavā
kuṇḍanābhiṃ puraskṛtya niniṣṭhā mūrtidhāriṇaḥ
gurorādeśataḥ kuryur nijakuṇḍeṣu saṃskṛtiṃ
paṭheyurbrāhmaṇāḥ śāntiṃ svaśākhāvedapāragāḥ
śrīsūktaṃ pāvamānīś ca maitrakañca vṛṣākapiṃ
devavratantu bhāruṇḍaṃ jyeṣṭhasāma rathantaraṃ
puruṣaṃ gītimetāni sāmavedī tu dakṣiṇe
rudraṃ puruṣasūktañca ślokādhyāyaṃ viśeṣataḥ
brāhmaṇañca yajurvedī paścimāyāṃ samuccaret
nīlarudraṃ tathātharvī sūkṣmāsūkṣmantathaiva ca
ācāryaścāgnimutpādya pratikuṇḍaṃ pradāpayet
vahneḥ pūrvādikān bhāgān pūrvakuṇḍāditaḥ kramāt
dhūpadīpacarūṇāñca dadītāgniṃ samuddharet
homaṅkṛtvā tu mantrajñaḥ pūrṇāṃ dattvā śubhāvahāṃ
pūrvavaccarukaṃ kṛtvā pratikuṇḍaṃ nivedayet
yajamānālaṅkṛtāstu vrajeyuḥ snānamaṇḍapaṃ
bhadrapīṭhe nidhāyeśaṃ tāḍayitvāvaguṇṭhayet
snāpayet pūjayitvā tu mṛdā kāṣāyavāriṇā
gomūtrair gomayenāpi vāriṇā cāntarāntarā
bhasmanā gandhatoyena phaḍantāstreṇa vāriṇā
deśiko mūrtipaiḥ sārdhaṃ kṛtvā kāraṇaśodhanaṃ
dharmajaptena sañchāṭya pītavarṇena vāsasā
tatra dattāsanāyāñca śayyāyāṃ sanniveśya ca
śalākayā suvarṇasya akṣiṇī śastrakarmaṇā
añjayellakṣmakṛt paścācchāstradṛṣṭena karmaṇā
kṛtakarmā ca śastreṇa lakṣmī śilpī samutkṣipet
tryaṃśādardhotha pādārdhādardhāyā
sarvakāmaprasiddhyarthaṃ śubhaṃ lakṣmāvatāraṇaṃ
liṅgadīrghavikārāṃśe tribhaktaṃ bhāgavarṇanāt
yavasya navabhaktasya bhāgair aṣṭābhirāvṛtā
evamaṣṭāṃśavṛddhyā tu liṅge sārdhakarādike
bhavedaṣṭayavā pṛthvī gambhīrātra ca hāstike
evamaṣṭāṃśa vṛddhyā tu liṅge sārdhakarādike
bhavedaṣṭayavā pṛthvī gambhīrānnavahāstike
śāmbhaveṣu ca liṅgeṣu pādavṛddheṣu sarvataḥ
gambhīratvaṣṭayuvābhyāṃ rekhāpi tryaṃśavṛddhitaḥ
sarveṣu ca bhavet sūkṣmāṃ liṅgamastakamastakaṃ
lakṣmakṣetreṣṭadhābhakte mūrdhnibhāgadvaye śubhe
rekhātrayeṇa sambaddhaṃ kārayet pṛṣṭadeśagaṃ
svarūpaṃ lakṣaṇanteṣāṃ prabhā ratneṣu nirmalā
lakṣmaṇoddhārarekhāñca ghṛtena madhunā tathā
arcayecca tato liṅgaṃ snāpayitvā mṛdādibhiḥ
śilpinantoṣayitvā tu dadyādgāṃ gurave tataḥ
liṅgaṃ dhūpādibhiḥ prācyaṃ gāyeyurbhartṛgāstrayaḥ
savyena cāpasavyena sūtreṇātha kuśena vā
smṛtvā ca rocanaṃ datvā kuryānnirmañjanādikaṃ
guḍalavaṇadhānyākadānena visṛjecca tāḥ
gurumūrtidharaiḥ sārdhaṃ hṛdā vā praṇavena vā
snāpayet pañcagavyena pañcāmṛtapuraḥsaraṃ
virūkṣaṇaṃ kaṣāyaiś ca sarvauṣadhijalena vā
śubhrapuṣpaphalasvarṇaratnaśṛṅgayavodakaiḥ
tīrthodakena gāṅgena candanena ca vāriṇā
kṣīrārṇavādibhiḥ kumbhaiḥ śivakumbhajalena ca
virūkṣaṇaṃ vilepañca sugandhaiś candanādibhiḥ
raktarūpeṇa nīrājya rakṣātilakapūrvakaṃ
dravyaiḥ stutyādibhistuṣṭamarcayet puruṣāṇunā
samācamya hṛdā devaṃ brūyādutthīyatāṃ prabho
maṇḍape paścimadvāre śayyāyāṃ viniveśayet
paścime piṇḍikāntasya nyasedbrahmaśalāntadā
utthāpyoktāsane liṅgaṃ śirasā pūrvamastakaṃ
dadyāddhūpañca sampūjya tathā vāsāṃsi varmaṇā
gṛhopakṛtinaivedyaṃ hṛdā dadyāt svaśaktitaḥ
ghṛtakṣaudrayutaṃ pātramabhyaṅgāya padāntike
deśikaś ca sthitastatra ṣaṭtriṃśattattvasañcayaṃ
māyāpadeśaśaktyantanturyāśāṣṭāṃśavartulaṃ
tatrātmatattvavidyākhyaṃ śivaṃ sṛṣṭikramaṇa tu
ekaśaḥ pratibhāgeṣu brahmaviṣṇuharādhipān
vinyasya mūrtimūrtīśān pūrvādikramato yathā
kṣmāvahniryajamānārkajalavāyuniśākarān
ākāśamūrtirūpāṃstān nyasettadadhināyakān
mahādevañca bhīmañca mantrāstadvācakā ime
lavaśaṣacayasāś ca hakāraś ca trimātrikaḥ
praṇavo hṛdayārṇurvā mūlamantro 'thavā kvacit
pañcakuṇḍātmake yāge mūrtīḥ pañcāthavā nyaset
pṛthivījalatejāṃsi vāyumākāśameva ca
kramāttadadhipān pañca brahmāṇaṃ dharaṇodharaṃ
rudramīśaṃ sadākhyañca sṛṣṭinyāyena mantravit
mumukṣorvā nivṛttādyāḥ ajātādyāstadīśvarāḥ
śuddhe cātmani vidyeśā aśuddhe lokanāyakāḥ
draṣṭavyā mūrtipāś caiva bhoginī mantranāyakāḥ
pañcaviṃśattathaivāṣṭapañcatrīṇi yathākramaṃ
eṣāntattvaṃ tadīśānāmindrādīnāṃ tato yathā
oṃ hāṃ śaktitattvāya nama ity ādi oṃ hāṃ śaktitattvādhipāya nama ity ādi oṃ hāṃ kṣmāmūrtaye namaḥ oṃ hāṃ kṣmāmūrtyadhīśāya
śivāya nama ity ādi oṃ hāṃ pṛthivīmūrtaye namaḥ oṃ hāṃ mūrtyadhipāya brahmaṇe nama ity ādi oṃ hāṃ śivatattvādhipāya rudrāya nama ity ādi
nābhikandātsamuccārya ghaṇṭānādavisarpaṇaṃ
brahmādikāraṇatyāgād dvādaśāntasamāśritaṃ
dvādaśāntātsamānīya niṣkalaṃ vyāpakaṃ śivaṃ
aṣṭatriṃśatkalopetaṃ sahasrakiraṇojjvalaṃ
sarvaśaktimayaṃ sāṅgaṃ dhyātvā liṅge niveśayet
jīvanyāso bhavedevaṃ liṅge sarvārthasādhakaḥ
piṇḍikādiṣu tu nyāsaḥ procyate sāmprataṃ yathā
piṇḍikāñca kṛtasnānāṃ viliptāñcandanādibhiḥ
pañcaratnādisaṃyuktāṃ liṅgasyottarataḥ sthitāṃ
kṛtasnānādikāntatra liṅgamūle śilāṃ nyaset
kṛtasnānādisaṃskāraṃ śaktyantaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ tathā
praṇavapūrvaṃ huṃ pūṃ hrīṃ madhyādanyatamena ca
kriyāśaktiyutāṃ piṇḍīṃ śilāmādhararūpiṇīṃ
rakṣāyai lokapālāṃś ca sāyudhānyājayedvahiḥ
oṃ hūṃ hraṃ kriyāśaktaye namaḥ oṃ hūṃ hrāṃ haḥ mahāgaurī rudradayite svāheti ca piṇḍikāyāṃ oṃ hāṃ ādhāraśaktaye namaḥ oṃ hāṃ vṛṣabhāya namaḥ
dhārikāṃ dīptimatyugrā jyotsnā caitā balotkaṭāḥ
tathā dhātrī vidhātrī ca nyasedvā pañcanāyikāḥ
vāmā jyeṣṭhā kriyā jñānā bedhā tisrīthavā nyaset
kriyājñānā tathecchā ca pūrvavacchāntimūrtiṣu
tamo mohā kṣamī niṣṭhā mṛtyurmāyābhavajvarāḥ
tisrothavā kriyājñānā tathā bādhādhināyikā
ātmāditriṣu tattveṣu tīvramūrtiṣu vinyaset
atrāpi piṇḍikā brahmaśilādiṣu yathāvidhi
evaṃ vidhāya vinyāsaṃ gatvā kuṇḍāntikaṃ tataḥ
kuṇḍamadhye maheśānaṃ mekhalāsu maheśvaraṃ
kriyāśaktiṃ tathānyāsu nādamoṣṭhe ca vinyaset
ghaṭaṃ sthaṇḍilavahnīśaiḥ nāḍīsandhānakantataḥ
viśantī sūryamārgeṇa niḥsarantīṃ samudgatāṃ
punaś ca śūnyamārgeṇa viśatīṃ svasya cintayet
sampūjya dhārikāṃ śaktiṃ kuṇḍe santarpya ca kramāt
tattvatattveśvarā murtīrmūrtīrśāṃś ca ghṛtādibhiḥ
śataṃ sahasramardhaṃ vā pūrṇayā saha homayet
tattvatattveśvarā mūrtirmūrtīśāṃś ca kareṇukān
santarpya śaktiṃ kumbhāmbhaḥprokṣite kuśamūlataḥ
liṅgamūlaṃ ca saṃspṛśya japeyurhomasaṅkhyayā
sannidhānaṃ hṛdā kuryurvarmaṇā cāvaguṇṭhanaṃ
evaṃ saṃśodhya brahmādi viṣṇvantādi viśuddhaye
kuśamadhyāgrayogena liṅgamadhyāgrakaṃ spṛśet
oṃ hāṃ haṃ oṃ oṃ oṃ eṃ oṃ bhūṃ bhūṃ vāhyamūrtaye namaḥ
hāṃ vāṃ āṃ oṃ āṃ ṣāṃ oṃ bhūṃ bhūṃ vā vahnimūrtaye namaḥ
pañcamūrtyātmakepyevaṃ sandhānaṃ hṛdayādibhiḥ
śilāpiṇḍo vṛṣeṣvevaṃ pūrṇāchinnaṃ susaṃvaraiḥ
bhāgābhāgaviśuddhyarthaṃ homaṃ kuryācchatādikaṃ
nyūnādidoṣamoṣāya śivenāṣṭādhikaṃ śataṃ
vidhipūrṇamapūrṇaṃ vā svaśaktyāpūrya gṛhyatāṃ
oṃ hrīṃ śāṅkari pūraya svāhā iti piṇḍikāyāṃ
atha liṅge nyasej jñānī kriyākhyaṃ pīṭhavigrahe
ādhārarūpiṇīṃ śaktiṃ nyased brahmaśilopari
nibadhya saptarātraṃ vā pañcarātraṃ trirātrakaṃ
vinādhivāsanaṃ yāgaḥ kṛto 'pi phalapradaḥ
svamantraiḥ pratyahaṃ deyamāhutīnāṃ śataṃ śataṃ
śivapratiṣṭhākathanaṃ
īśvara uvāca
prātar nitpavidhiṃ kṛtvā dvārapālaprapūjanaṃ
aṣṭamuṣṭikayā liṅgaṃ vahniṃ sanparpya ca kramāt
śivājñātastato gacchet prāsādaṃ śastramuccaran
tadgatān prakṣipedvighnān humphaḍantaśarāṇunā
na madhye sthāpayelliṅgaṃ bedhadoṣaviśaṅkayā
kiñcidīśānamāśritya śilāṃ madhye niveśayet
mūlena tāmanantākhyāṃ sarvādhārasvarūpiṇīṃ
sarvagāṃ sṛṣṭiyogena vinyasedacalāṃ śilāṃ
athavānena mantreṇa śivasyāsanarūpiṇīṃ
hraṃ laṃ hrīṃ svāhā
tvayā śivājñayā śakte sthātavyamiha santataṃ
vajrādīni ca ratnāni tathośīrādikauṣadhīḥ
lohān hemādikāṃsyantān haritālādikāṃs tathā
dhānyaprabhṛtiśastrāṃś ca pūrvamuktānanukramāt
pūrvādiṣu ca garteṣu nyasedekaikaśaḥ kramāt
hemajaṃ tārajaṃ kūrmaṃ vṛṣaṃ vā dvārasammukhaṃ
sarittaṭamṛdā yuktaṃ parvatāgramṛdāthavā
pṛthivīṃ rājatīṃ yadvā yadvā hemasamudbhavāṃ
sarvavījasuvarṇābhyāṃ samāyuktāṃ vinikṣipet
suvarṇaṃ kṛśarāyuktaṃ padmanālaṃ tato nyaset
śvabhramācchādya vastreṇa tanutreṇāstrarakṣitaṃ
śevena vā śilāśvabhrasaṅgadoṣanivṛttaye
śastreṇa vā śataṃ samyag juhuyāt pūrṇayā saha
samutthāpya hṛdādevamāsanaṃ maṅgalādibhiḥ
caturbhiḥ saha kartavyā devayajñasya pṛṣṭhataḥ
liṅgaṃ saṃsthāpya datvārghyaṃ prāsādaṃ sanniveśayet
dvārabandhe śikhāśūnye tadardhenātha tadṛte
varjayan dvārasaṃsparśaṃ dvāreṇaiva maheśvaraṃ
atha pīṭhe ca saṃsthāpya liṅgaṃ dvārasya sammukhaṃ
tūryamaṅgalanirgheṣair dūrvākṣatasamanvitaṃ
samuttiṣṭhaṃ hṛdetyuktvā mahāpāśupataṃ paṭhet
apanīya ghaṭaṃ śvabhrād deśiko mūrtipaiḥ saha
layāntaṃ mūlamuccārya spṛṣṭvā śvabhre niveśayet
ardhena vāṣṭamāṃśena sarvasyātha praveśanaṃ
vidhāya sīsakaṃ nābhidīrghābhiḥ susamāhitaḥ
śvabhraṃ vālukayāpurya brūyāt sthirībhaveti ca
tato liṅge sthirībhūte dhyātvā sakalarūpiṇaṃ
mūlamuccārya śaktyantaṃ sṛṣṭyā ca niṣkalaṃ nyaset
sthāpyamānaṃ yadā liṅgaṃ yāmyāṃ diśamathāśrayet
tattaddigīśamantreṇa pūrṇāntaṃ dakṣiṇānvitaṃ
juhuyān mūlamantreṇa bahurūpeṇa vā śataṃ
kuñcānyeṣvapi doṣeṣu śivaśāntiṃ samāśrayet
yuktaṃ nyāsādibhirliṅgaṃ kurvannevaṃ na doṣabhāk
pīṭhabandhamataḥ kṛtvā lakṣaṇasyāṃśalakṣaṇaṃ
gaurīmantraṃ layaṃ nītvā sṛṣṭyā piṇḍīñca vinyaset
sampūrya pārśvasaṃsiddhiṃ vālukāvajralepanaṃ
tato mūrtidharaiḥ sārdhaṃ guruḥ śāntiṃ ghaṭordhvataḥ
saṃsthāpya kalaśair anyaistadvat pañcāmṛtādibhiḥ
umāmaheśamantrābhyāṃ tau spṛśelliṅgamudrayā
tatastritattvavinyāsaṃ ṣaḍarcādipuraḥsaraṃ
kṛtvā mūrtiṃ tadīśānāmaṅgānāṃ brahmaṇāmatha
jñānī liṅge kriyāpīṭhe vināsya snāpayettataḥ
candrārkatārakaṃ yāvan mantreṇa śaivamūrtipaiḥ
praṇamyeva vahirgatvā hṛdā vā praṇavena vā
saṃsthāpya vṛṣabhaṃ paścāt pūrvavadvalimācaret
nyūnādidoṣamoṣāya tato mṛtyujitā śataṃ
śivena saśivo hutvā śāntyarthaṃ pāyasena ca
jñānājñānakṛtaṃ yacca tat pūraya mahāvibho
hiraṇyapaśubhūmyādi gītavādyādihetave
dānaṃ mahotsavaṃ paścāt kuryāddinacatuṣṭayaṃ
caturthehani pūrṇāñca carukaṃ bahurūpiṇā
dinacatuṣṭayaṃ yāvattannirmālyantadūrdhataḥ
nirmālyāpanayaṃ kṛtvā snāpayitvā tu pūjayet
pūjā sāmānyaliṅgeṣu kāryā sādhāraṇāṇubhiḥ
vihāya liṅgacaitanyaṃ kuryāt sthāṇuvisarjanaṃ
asādhāraṇaliṅgeṣu kṣamasveti visarjanaṃ
nityotha sarvagaś caivāvināśī dṛṣṭa eva ca
ete guṇā maheśasya sannidhānāya kīrtitāḥ
oṃ namaḥ śivāya sthiro bhavetyāhutīnāṃ kramaḥ
saṃsnāpya tad dvitīyantu kartṛsnānāya dhārayet
datvā baliṃ samācamya vahirgacchet śivājñayā
jagatīvāhyataś caṇḍamaiśānyāndiśi mandire
pūrvavan nyāsahomādi vidhāya dhyānapūrvakaṃ
aṅgāni pūrvayuktāni brahmāṇī tvarcanā yathā
evaṃ sadyojātāya oṃ hrūṃ phaṭ namaḥ oṃ viṃ vāmadevāya hrūṃ phaṭ namaḥ oṃ buṃ aghorāya hrūṃ phaṭ namaḥ oṃ tatpuruṣāya vaumīśānāya ca hrūṃ phaṭ
nyūnādhikañca yatkiñcit kṛtamajñānato mayā
abhyarcya caṇḍaṃ sasutaṃ yajamānaṃ hi bhāryayā
vittaśāṭhyaṃ vinā dadyād bhūhiraṇyādi dakṣiṇāṃ
mūrtimān vidhivat paścāt jāpakān brāhmaṇāṃs tathā
devajñaṃ śilpinaṃ prārcya dīnānāthādi bhojayet
kṣamasva nātha tat sarvaṃ kāruṇyāmbunidhaṃ mama
pratiṣṭhāpuṇyasadbhāvaṃ sphurattārakasaprabhaṃ
tataḥ pāśapatopetaṃ praṇamya parameśvaraṃ
gururvastrādisaṃyuktaṃ gṛhṇīyādyāgamaṇḍapaṃ
sarvopakaraṇaṃ śilpī tathā snāpanamaṇḍapaṃ
ādivarṇasya bhedādvā sutattvavyāptibhāvitāḥ
kṣetrapāḥ kinnarādyāś ca pṛthivītattvamāśritāḥ
snānaṃ sarasvatīlakṣmīnadīnāmambhasi kvacit
aṇḍavṛddhipradhānāntaṃ tritattvaṃ brahmaṇaḥ padaṃ
tanmātrādipradhānāntaṃ padametat trikaṃ hareḥ
nāṭyeśagaṇamātṝṇāṃ yakṣeśaśarajanmanāṃ
aṇḍajāḥ śuddhavidyāntaṃ padaṃ gaṇapates tathā
māyāṃśadeśaśaktyanataṃ śivā śivoptarociṣāṃ
padamīśvaraparyantaṃ vyaktārcāsu ca kīrtitaṃ
kūrmādyaṃ kīrtitaṃ yacca yacca ratnādipañcakaṃ
pratikṣipet pīṭhagarte ca pañcabrahmaśilāṃ vinā
ṣaḍbhirvibhājite garte tyaktvā bhāvañca pṛṣṭhataḥ
sthāpanaṃ pañcamāṃśe ca yadi vā vasubhājite
dhāraṇābhirviśuddhiḥ syāt sthāpane lepacitrayoḥ
snānādi mānasantatra śilāratnādiveśanaṃ
netrodghāṭanamantreṣṭamāsanādiprakalpanaṃ
pūjā nirambubhiḥ puṣpair yathā citraṃ na duṣyati
bhagatrayeṇa bhāgāṃśo bhavedbhāgadvayena vā
sṛṣṭimantreṇa saṃskāro vidhivat sphāṭikādiṣu
kiñca brahmaśilāratnaprabhūteścānivedanaṃ
yojanaṃ piṇḍikāyāś ca manasā parikalpayet
svayambhūvāṇaliṅgādau saṃskṛtau niyamo na hi
snāpanaṃ saṃhitāmantrair nyāsaṃ homañca kārayet
nadīsamudrarohāṇāṃ sthāpanaṃ pūrvavan mataṃ
aihikam mṛṇmayaṃ liṅgaṃ piṣṭakādi ca takṣaṇāt
kṛtvā sampūjayecchuddhaṃ sīkṣaṇādividhānataḥ
samādāya tato mantrānātmānaṃ sannidhāya ca
viṣṇvādisthāpanaṃ caiva pṛyaṅmantraiḥ samācaret
gaurīpratiṣṭhākathanaṃ
īśvara uvāca
vakṣye gaurīpratiṣṭhāñca pūjayā sahitāṃ śṛṇu
maṇḍapādyaṃ puro yacca saṃsthāpya cādhiropayet
śayyāyāntāṃś ca vinyasya mantrānmūrtyādikān guha
ātmavidyāśivāntañca kuryādīśaniveśanaṃ
śaktiṃ parāṃ tato nyasya hutvā japtvā ca pūrvavat
sandhāya ca tathā piṇḍīṃ kriyāśaktisvarūpiṇīṃ
sadeśavyāpikāṃ dhyātvā nyastaratnādikāṃ tathā
evaṃ saṃsthāpya tāṃ paścāddevīntasyānniyojayet
paraśaktisvarūpāntāṃ svāṇunā śaktiyogataḥ
tato nyaset kriyāśaktiṃ pīṭhe jñānañca vigrahe
tatopi vyāpinīṃ śaktiṃ samāvāhya niyojayet
ambikāṃ śivanāmnīñca samālabhya prapūjayet
oṃ ādhāraśaktaye namaḥ oṃ kūrmāya namaḥ oṃ skandāya ca tathā namaḥ oṃ hrīṃ nārāyaṇāya namaḥ oṃ aiśvaryāya namaḥ
oṃ aṃ adhaśchadanāya namaḥ oṃ padmāsanāya namaḥ oṃ ūrdhvacchadanāya namaḥ oṃ padmāsanāya namaḥ atha sampūjyāḥ keśavās tathā oṃ hrīṃ karṇikāya namaḥ oṃ kṣaṃ puṣkarākṣebhya ihārcayet oṃ hāṃ puṣṭyai hrīṃ ca jñānāyai hrūṃ kriyāyai tato namaḥ oṃ nālāya namaḥ ruṃ dharmāya namaḥ ruṃ jñānāya vai namaḥ oṃ vairāgyāya vai namaḥ oṃ vai adharmāya namaḥ oṃ ruṃ ajñānāya vai namaḥ oṃ avairāgyāya vai namaḥ aṃ anaiśvaryāya namaḥ huṃ vāce huṃ ca rāgiṇyai kraiṃ jvālinyai tato namaḥ oṃ hrauṃ śamāyai ca namaḥ hruṃ jyeṣṭhāyai tato namaḥ oṃ hrauṃ rauṃ krauṃ navaśaktyai gauṃ ca gauryāsanāya ca gauṃ gaurīmūrtaye namaḥ gauryā mūlamathocyate oṃ hrīṃ saḥ mahāgauri rudradayite svāhā gauryai namaḥ gāṃ hrūṃ hrīṃ śivo gūṃ syāt śivāyai kavacāya ca goṃ netrāya ca goṃ astrāya oṃ gauṃ vijñānaśaktaye oṃ gūṃ kriyāśaktaye namaḥ pūrvādau śākrādikān oṃ suṃ subhāgāyai namaḥ hrīṃ vījalalitā tataḥ oṃ hrīṃ kāminyai ca namaḥ oṃ hrūṃ syāt kāmaśālinīmantrair gaurīṃ pratiṣṭhāpya prārcya japtvātha sarvabhāk
sūryapratiṣṭhākathanaṃ
īśvara uvāca
vakṣye sūryapratiṣṭhāñca pūrvavanmaṇḍapādikaṃ
snānādikañca samyādya pūrvoktavidhinā tataḥ
vidyāmāsanaśayyāyāṃ sāṅgaṃ vinyasya bhāskaraṃ
śuddhyādi pūrvavat kṛtvā piṇḍīṃ saṃśodhya pūrvavat
svāṇunā vidhivat sūryaṃ śaktyantaṃ sthāpayedguruḥ
svāmyantamathavādityaṃ pādāntannāma dhārayet
sūryamantrāstu pūrvoktā draṣṭavyāḥ sthāpanepi ca
dvārapratiṣṭhākathanaṃ
īśvara uvāca
dvārāśritapratiṣṭhāyā vakṣyāmi vidhimapyatha
dvārāṅgāni kaṣāyādyaiḥ saṃskṛtya śayane nyaset
mūlamadhyāgrabhāgeṣu trayamātmādiseśvaraṃ
ratnādipañcakaṃ nyasya śāntihomaṃ vidhāya ca
yavasiddhārthakākrāntā ṛddhivṛddhimahātilāḥ
gomṛtsarṣaparāgendramohanīlakṣaṇāmṛtāḥ
rocanā rug vaco dūrvā prāsādadhaś ca poṭalīṃ
dvāramuttarataḥ kiñcidāśritaṃ sanniveśayet
śivamakāśadeśe ca vyāpakaṃ sarvamaṅgale
dvārāśritāṃś ca talpādīn kṛtayuktaiḥ svanāmabhiḥ
juhuyācchatamardhaṃ vā dviguṇaṃ śaktitothavā
nyūnādidoṣamoṣārthaṃ hetito juhuyāccchataṃ
prāsādapratiṣṭhā
īavara uvāca
śukanāśāsamāptau tu pūrvavedyāś ca madhyataḥ
cūtādipallavānāñca kṛtī kṛtyañca vinyaset
pūrakeṇa samādāya sakalīkṛtavigrahaḥ
sarvātmabhinnātmānaṃ svāṇunā svāntamārutaḥ
dvādaśāntāt samādāya sphuradvahnikaṇopamaṃ
vigrahantadguṇānāñca bodhakañca kalādikaṃ
kṣāntaṃ vāgīśvaraṃ tattu brātaṃ tatra niveśayet
daśa nāḍīrdaśa prāṇānindriyāṇi trayodaśa
tadadhipāṃś ca saṃyojya praṇavādyaiḥ svanāmabhiḥ
svakāryakāraṇatvena māyākāśaniyāmikāḥ
vidyeśān prerakān śambhuṃ vyāpinañca susamvaraiḥ
suvarṇādyudbhavaṃ yadvā puruṣaṃ puruṣānugaṃ
pañcagavyakaṣāyādyaiḥ pūrvavat saṃskṛtantataḥ
śayyāyāṃ kumbhamāropya dhyātvā rudramumāpatiṃ
sannidhānāya homañca praokṣaṇaṃ sparśanaṃ japaṃ
dhvajāropaṇaṃ
īśvara uvāca
pratiṣṭhā ca yathoddiṣṭā tathā skanda vadāmi te
taḍāgārdhapraveśādvā yadvā savārdhaveśanāt
aiṣṭake dārujaḥ śūlaḥ śailaje dhāmni śailajaḥ
vaiṣṇavādau ca cakrāḍhyaḥ kumbhaḥ syānmūrtimānataḥ
īśaśūlaḥ samākhyāto mūrdhni liṅgasamanvitaḥ
vījapūrakayukto vā śivaśāstreṣu tadvidhaḥ
bhavedvā daṇḍamānastu yadi vā tadyadṛcchayā
mahādhvajaḥ samākhyāto yastu pīṭhasya veṣṭakaḥ
uttamādikrameṇaiva vijñeyaḥ śūribhistataḥ
vaṃśajaḥ śālajātirvā sa daṇḍaḥ sarvakāmadaḥ
ayamāropyamāṇastu bhaṅgamāyāti vai yadi
rājñoniṣṭaṃ vijānīyādyajamānasya vā tathā
dvārapālādipūjāñca mantrāṇāntarpyaṇantathā
vidhāya cūlakaṃ daṇḍaṃ snāpayedastramantrataḥ
mṛdu kaṣāyādibhiḥ snānaṃ prāsādaṅkārayettataḥ
vilipya rasamācchādya śayyāyāṃ nyasya pūrvavat
cūḍake liṅgavaṇanyāso na ca jñānaṃ na ca kriyā
viśeṣārthā caturthī ca na kuṇḍasya kalpanā
daṇḍe tayārthatattvañca vidyātattvaṃ dvitīyakaṃ
niṣkalañca śivantatra nyasyāṅgāni prapūjayet
anyathāpi kṛtaṃ yacca dhvajasaṃskāraṇaṃ kvacit
prāsāde kārite sthāne sragvastrādivibhūṣite
homādikaṃ vidhāyātha śivaṃ sampūjya pūrvavat
kuṣmāṇḍahāṭakau pīṭhe pātālanarakaiḥ saha
brahmāṇdakamidaṃ dhyātvā jaṅghātāñca vibhāvayet
sarvāvaraṇasañjñañca vṛddhayonyavṛkānvitaṃ
yogāṣṭakasamāyuktaṃ nāśāvidhi guṇatrayaṃ
paṭasthaṃ puruṣaṃ siṃhaṃ vāmañca paribhāvayet
mañjarīvedikāyāñca vidyādikacatuṣṭayaṃ
kaṇṭhe māyāṃ sarudrāñca vidyāścāmalasārake
jaṭājūṭañca taṃ vidyācchūlaṃ candrārdharūpakaṃ
śaktitrayaṃ ca tatraiva daṇḍe nādaṃ vibhāvya ca
dhvaje ca kuṇḍalīṃ śaktimiti dhāmni vibhāvayet
jagatyā vātha sandhāya liṅgaṃ piṇḍikayāthavā
dhāma pradakṣiṇīkṛtya labhate phalamīhitaṃ
adhipān śastrayuktāṃś ca rakṣaṇāya nibodhayet
nyūnādidoṣaśāntyarthaṃ hutvā datvā ca digbaliṃ
gurave dakṣiṇāṃ dadyād yajamāno divaṃ vrajet
pratimāliṅgavedīnāṃ yāvantaḥ paramāṇavaḥ
jīrṇoddhāraḥ
īśvara uvāca
jīrṇādīnāñca liṅgānāmuddhāraṃ vidhinā vade
saṃpuṭaṃ sphuṭitaṃ vyaṅgaṃ liṅgamityevamādikaṃ
ityādiduṣṭaliṅgānāṃ yojyā piṇḍī tathā vṛṣaḥ
cālitañcalitaṃ liṅgamatyarthaṃ viṣamasthitaṃ
diḍmūḍhaṃ pātitaṃ liṅgaṃ madhyasthaṃ patitaṃ tathā
tato 'nyatrāpi saṃsthāpya vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā
susthitaṃ dusthitaṃ vāpi śivaliṅgaṃ na cālayet
śatena sthāpanaṃ kuryāt sahasreṇa tu cālanaṃ
pūjādibhiś ca saṃyuktaṃ jīrṇādyamapi susthitaṃ
yāmye maṇḍapamīśe vā pratyagdvāraikatoraṇaṃ
vidhāya dvārapūjādi sthaṇḍile mantrapūjanaṃ
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā tu śambhuṃ vijñāpayettataḥ
duṣṭaliṅgamidaṃ śaṃbhoḥ śāntiruddhāraṇasya cet
rusistavādividhinā adhitiṣṭhasva māṃ śiva
evaṃ vijñāpya deveśaṃ śāntihomaṃ samācaret
madhvājyakṣīradūrvābhirmūlenāṣṭādhikaṃ śataṃ
tato liṅgaṃ ca saṃsthāpya pūjayet sthiṇḍile tathā
oṃ vyāpakeśvarāyeti nāṭyantaṃ śivavādinā
oṃ vyāpakaṃ hṛdayeśvarāya namaḥ oṃ vyāpakeśvarāya śirase namaḥ ity ādyaṅgamantrāḥ
sattvaḥ kopīha yaḥ kopiliṅgamāśritya tiṣṭhati
liṅgantyaktvā śivājñābhiryatreṣṭaṃ tatra gacchatu
sahasraṃ pratibhāge ca tataḥ pāśupatāṇunā
hutvā śāntyambunā prokṣya spṛṣṭvā kuśair japettataḥ
aṣṭamūrtīśvarān liṅga piṇḍikāsaṃsthitān guruḥ
visṛjya svarṇapāśena vṛṣaskandhasthayā tathā
rajvā vadhvā tayā nītvā śivamantaṃ gṛṇan janaiḥ
tṛptaye dikpatīnāñca vāstuśuddhau śataṃ śataṃ
rakṣāṃ vidhāya taddhāmni mahāpāśupatā tataḥ
jīrṇaṃ vāpyathavā bhagnaṃ vidhināpi nacālayet
eṣa eva vidhiḥ kāryojīrṇadhāmasamuddhṛtau
saṅkoce maraṇaṃ proktaṃ vistāro tu dhanakṣayaḥ
taddravyaṃ śreṣṭhadravyaṃ vā tat sakāryaṃ tatpramāṇakaṃ
prāsādalakṣaṇaṃ
īśvara uvāca
vakṣye prāsādasāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ te śikhadhvaja
adribhāgena garbhaḥ syāt piṇḍikā pādavistarāt
pañcabhāgīkṛte kṣetrentarbhāge tu piṇḍikā
suṣiraṃ bhāgavistīrṇaṃ bhittayo bhāgavistarāt
garbho bhāgena vistīrṇo bhāgadvayena piṇḍikā
vistārād dviguṇo vāpi sapādadviguṇo 'pi vā
nemiḥ pādonaviestīrṇā prāsādasya samantataḥ
cāmuṇḍaṃ bhairavaṃ teṣu nāṭyeśaṃ ca niveśayet
prāsādārdhena devānāmaṣṭau vā caturo 'pi vā
pradakṣiṇāṃ vahiḥ kuryāt prāsādādiṣu vā navā
ādityāḥ pūrvataḥ sthāpyāḥ skandognirvāyugocare
evaṃ yamādayo nyasyāḥ svasyāḥ svasyāṃ diśi sthitāḥ
caturdhā śikharaṃ kṛtvā śukanāsā dvibhāgikā
tṛtīye vedikā tvagneḥ sakaṇṭho malasārakaḥ
vairājaḥ puṣpakaścānyaḥ kailāso maṇikas tathā
triviṣṭhapañca pañcaiva merumūrdhani saṃsthitāḥ
vṛtto vṛttāyataścānyo hy aṣṭāsraścāpi pañcamaḥ
śrīvatsaśceti vairājyānvavāye ca samutthitāḥ
balabhī gṛharājaś ca śālāgṛhañca mandiraṃ
prabhavaḥ śivikā veśma navaite puṣpakodbhavāḥ
vardhanī vānya uṣṇīṣaḥ śaṅkhaś ca kalasas tathā
svavṛkṣaś ca tathāpyete vṛttāḥ kailāsasambhavāḥ
gajotha vṛṣabho haṃso garutmānnṛkṣanāyakaḥ
bhūṣaṇo bhūdharaścānnye śrījayaḥ pṛthavīdharaḥ
vṛttāyatāt samudbhūtā navaite maṇikāhvayāt
citraṃ svastikakhaḍgañca gadā śrīkaṇṭha eva ca
nagarāṇāmimāḥ sañjñā lāṭādīnāmimās tathā
grīvārdhenonnatañcūlampṛthulañca vibhāgataḥ
daśadhā vedikāṅkṛtvā pañcabhiḥ skandhavistaraḥ
tribhiḥ kaṇṭhaṃ tu kartavyaṃ caturbhistu pracaṇḍakaṃ
dikṣu dvārāṇi kāryāṇi na vidikṣu kadācana
piṇḍikā koṇavistīrṇā madhyamāntā hy udāhṛtā
ucchrāyā dviguṇāsteṣāmanyathā vā nigadyate
ṣaṣṭyādhikāt samārabhya aṅgulānāṃ śatādiha
uttamānyapi catvāri dvārāṇi daśahānitaḥ
ucchrāyāt pādavistīrṇā viśākhāstaduduṃvare
dvipañcasaptanavabhiḥ śākhābhirdvāramiṣṭadaṃ
adhaḥśākhācaturthāṃśe pratīhārau niveśayet
mithunaiḥ pādavarṇābhiḥ śākhāśeṣaṃ vibhūṣayet
prāsādagṛhaśilādimārgaviddheṣu bandhanaṃ
sabhābiddhe na dāridryaṃ varṇabiddhe nirākṛtiḥ
ulūkhalena dāridryaṃ śilābiddhena śatrutā
chedādutpāṭanādvāpi tathā prākāralakṣaṇāt
sīmāyā dviguṇatyāgād bedhadoṣo na jāyate
īśvara uvāca
nagaragrāmadurgādyā gṛhaprāsādavṛddhaye
prāgāsyā daśadhā nāḍyāstāsāṃ nāmāni ca bruve
śāntā yaśovatī kāntā viśālā prāṇavāhinī
uttarā dvādaśānyāś ca ekāśītyaṅghrikārikā
hariṇī suprabhā lakṣmīrvibhūtirvimalā priyā
jayā jvālā viśokā ca smṛtāstatrapādataḥ
īśādyaṣṭāṣṭakaṃ dikṣu yajedīśaṃ dhanañjayaṃ
śakramarkaṃ tathā satyaṃ bhṛśaṃ vyoma ca pūrvataḥ
kṛtāntamatha gandharvaṃ bhṛgaṃ mṛgañca dakṣiṇe
pitaraṃ dvārapālañca sugrīvaṃ puṣpadantakaṃ
varuṇaṃ daityaśeṣau ca yakṣmāṇaṃ paścime sadā
navāntaḥ padago brahmā pūjyordhe ca ṣaḍaṅghigāḥ
brahmeśāntarakoṣṭhastha māyākhyāntu paddvaye
tadadhaścāpavatsākhyaṃ kendrantareṣu ṣaṭpade
sāvitrī tadadho dvyaṃśe vivasvān ṣaṭpade tvadhaḥ
tadadho dvyaṅghrigaṃ yakṣma ṣaṭsaumyeṣu dharādharaṃ
carakīṃ skandavikaṭaṃ vidārīṃ pūtanāṃ kramāt
jammaṃ pāpaṃ pilipicchaṃ yajedīśādivāhyataḥ
ekāśīpadaṃ veśma maṇḍapaś ca śatāṅghrikaḥ
pūrvavaddevatāḥ pūjyā brahmā tu ṣoḍaśāṃśake
marīciś ca vivasvāṃś ca mitraṃ pṛthvīdharas tathā
daśakoṣṭhasthitā dikṣu tvanye beśādikoṇagāḥ
daityamātā tatheśāgnī mṛgākhyau pitarau tathā
pāpayakṣmānilau devāḥ sarve sārdhāṃśake sthitāḥ
yatpādyokaḥ pravakṣyāmi saṅkṣepeṇa kramād guha
sadigviṃśatkarair dairghyādaṣṭāviṃśati vistarāt
śiśirāśrayaḥ śivākhyaś ca rudrahīnaḥ sadobhayoḥ
rudradviguṇitā nāhāḥ pṛthuṣṇobhirvinā tribhiḥ
sāvitraḥ sālayaḥ kuḍyā anyeṣāṃ pṛthak striṃśāṃśataḥ
kuḍyasūtrasamā pṛthvī vīthī bhedādanekadhā
bhadre tulyañca vīthībhirdvāravīthī vināgrataḥ
śrījayaṃ pṛṣṭhato hīnaṃ bhadroyaṃ pārś cayorvinā
sāmānyānātha gṛhaṃ vakṣye sarveṣāṃ sarvakāmadaṃ
ekadvitricatuḥśālamaṣṭaśālaṃ yathākramāt
śivāsyamambupāsyaiṣa indrāsye yamasūryakaṃ
prāksaumyasthe ca daṇdākhyaṃ prāgyāmye vātasañjñakaṃ
āpyendau gṛhavalyākhyaṃ triśūlaṃ tadvinardhikṛt
pūrvaśalāvihīnaṃ syāt sukṣetraṃ vṛddhidāyakaṃ
yāmye hīne bhavecchūlī triśālaṃ vṛddhikṛt paraṃ
indrādikramato vacmi dhvajādyaṣṭau gṛhāṇyahaṃ
prakṣālānusragāvāsamagnau tasya mahānasaṃ
yāmye rasakriyā śayyā dhanuḥśastrāṇi rakṣasi
saumye dhanapaśū kuryādīśe dīkṣāvarālayaṃ
svāmihastamitaṃ veśma vistārāyāmapiṇḍikaṃ
triguṇaṃ hastasaṃyuktaṃ kṛtvāṣṭāṃśaihṛtaṃ tathā
sarvanāśakaraṃ veśma madhye cānte ca saṃsthitaṃ
tanmadhe maṇḍapaḥ śastaḥ samo vā dviguṇāyataḥ
pratyagāpye cenduyame haṭṭa eva gṛhāvalī
ekaikabhavanākhyāni dikṣvaṣṭāṣṭakasaṅkhyayā
īśādyaditikāntāni phalānyeṣāṃ yathākramaṃ
bhayaṃ nārī calatvaṃ ca jayo vṛddhiḥ pratāpakaḥ
dharmaḥ kaliś ca naisvyañca prāgdvāreṣvaṣṭasu dhruvaṃ
dāho 'sukhaṃ suhṛnnāśo dhananāśo mṛtirdhanaṃ
śilpitvaṃ tanayaḥ syācca yāmyadvāraphalāṣṭakam
āyuḥprāvrājyaśasyāni dhanaśāntyarthasaṅkṣayāḥ
śoṣaṃ bhogaṃ cāpatyañca jaladvāraphalāni ca
rogo madārtimukhyatvaṃ cārthāyuḥ kṛśatā matiḥ
mānaś ca dvārataḥ pūrva ūtarasyāndiśi kramāt
nagarādivāstuḥ
īśvara uvāca
nagarādikavāstuś ca vakṣye rājyādivṛddhaye
yojanaṃ yojanārdhaṃ vā tadarthaṃ sthānamāśrayet
īśāditriṃśatpadake pūrvadvāraṃ ca sūryake
gandharvābhyāṃ dakṣiṇe syādvāruṇye paścime tathā
saumyadvāraṃ saumyapade kāryā haṭṭāstu vistarāḥ
yenebhādi sukhaṃ gacchet kuryād dvāraṃ tu ṣaṭkaraṃ
vajrasūcīmukhaṃ neṣṭaṃ sakṛd dvitrisamāgamaṃ
cāpābhaṃ vajranāgābhaṃ purārambhe hi śāntikṛt
prārcya viṣṇu harārkādīnnatvā dadyād baliṃ balī
dakṣiṇe nṛtyavṛttīnāṃ veśyāstrīṇāṃ gṛhāṇi ca
naṭānāñcakrikādīnāṃ kaivartādeś ca nairṛte
rathānāmāyudhānāñca kṛpāṇāñca vāruṇe
śauṇḍikāḥ karmādhikṛtā vāyavye parikarmaṇaḥ
brāhmaṇā yatayaḥ siddhāḥ puṇyavantaś ca cottare
phalādyādivikrayiṇa īśāne ca vaṇigjanāḥ
pūrvataś ca balādhyakṣā āgneye vividhaṃ balaṃ
strīṇāmādeśino dakṣe kāṇḍārānnairṛte nyaset
paścime ca mahāmātyān koṣapālāṃś ca kārukān
uttare daṇḍanāthāṃś ca nāyakadvijasaṅkulān
pūrvataḥ kṣatriyān dakṣe vaiśyāñchūndrāṃś ca paścime
dikṣu vaidyān vājinaś ca balāni ca caturdiśaṃ
pūrveṇa caraliṅgyādīñchmaśānādīni dakṣiṇe
paścime godhanādyañca kṛṣikartṝṃstathottare
nyasenmlecchāṃś ca koṇeṣu grāmādiṣu tathā smṛtiṃ
śriyaṃ vaiśravaṇaṃ dvāri pūrve tau paśyatāṃ śriyaṃ
devādīnāṃ paścimataḥ pūrvāsyāni gṛhāṇi hi
pūrvataḥ paścimāsyāni dakṣiṇe cottarānanān
nākeśaviṣṇvādidhāmāni rakṣārthaṃ nagarasya ca
pūrvāyāṃ śrīgṛhaṃ proktamāgneyyāṃ vai mahānasaṃ
śanayaṃ dakṣiṇasyāntu nairṛtyāmāyudhāśrayaṃ
bhojanaṃ paścimāyāntu vāyavyāṃ dhānyasaṅgrahaḥ
uttare dravyasaṃsthānamaiśānyāṃ devatāgṛhaṃ
catuḥśālaṃ triśālaṃ vā dviśālaṃ caikaśālakaṃ
catuḥśālagṛhāṇāntu śālālindakabhedataḥ
śatadvayantu jāyante pañcāśat pañca teṣvapi
triśālāni tu catvāri dviśālāni tu pañcadhā
ekaśālāni catvāri ekālindāni vacmi ca
aṣṭāviṃśadalindāni gṛhāṇi nagarāṇi ca
ṣaḍalindāni viṃśaiva aṣṭābhirviṃśa eva hi
aṣṭālindaṃ bhavedevaṃ nagarādau gṛhāṇi hi
vakṣye bhuvanakoṣañca pṛthvīdvīpādilakṣaṇaṃ
agnidhraścāgnibāhuś ca vapuṣmāndyutimāṃs tathā
jyotiṣmān daśamasteṣāṃ satyanāmā suto 'bhavat
priyabratasutāḥ khyātāḥ saptadvīpāndadau pitā
vapuṣmate śālmalañca jyotiṣmate kuśāhvayaṃ
krauñcadvīpaṃ dyutimate śākaṃ bhavyāya dattavān
puṣkaraṃ savanāyādādagnīdhre 'dāt sute śataṃ
jambūdvīpaṃ pitā lakṣaṃ nābherdattaṃ himāhvayaṃ
hemakūṭaṃ kimpuruṣe harivarṣāya naiṣadhaṃ
ilāvṛte merumadhye ramye nīlācalaśritaṃ
bhadrāśvāya ca bhadrāśvaṃ ketumālāya paścimaṃ
śālagrāme tapastaptvā yayau viṣṇorlayaṃ nṛpaḥ
yāni kumpuruṣādyāni hy aṣṭavarṣāṇi sattama
teṣāṃ svābhāvikī siddhiḥ sukhaprāyā hy ayatnataḥ
jarāmṛtyubhayaṃ nāsti dharmādharmau yugādikaṃ
nādhamaṃ madhyamantulyā himāddeśāttu nābhitaḥ
ṛṣabho merudevyāñca ṛṣabhād bharato 'bhavat
ṛṣabho dattaśrīḥ putre śālagrāme hariṅgataḥ
bharato dattalakṣmīkaḥ śālagrāme hariṃ gataḥ
parameṣṭhī tatastasmāt pratīhārastadanvayaḥ
tasya putro mahāvīryo dhīmāṃstasmādajāyata
tvaṣṭā tvaṣṭuś ca virajārajastasyāpyabhūt sutaḥ
kṛtatretādisargeṇa sargaḥ svāyambhuvaḥ smṛtaḥ
bhuvanakoṣaḥ
jambūplakṣāhvayau dvīpau śālmaliścāparo mahān
kuśaḥ krauñcas tathā śākaḥ puṣkaraśceti saptamaḥ
ete dvīpāḥ samudraistu sapta saptabhirāvṛtāḥ
caturaśītisāhasro bhūyiṣṭhaḥ ṣoḍaśādvirāṭ
dvātriṃśanmūrdhni vistarāt ṣoḍaśādhaḥ sahasravān
bhūyastasyāsya śailo 'sau karṇikākārasaṃsthitaḥ
himavān hemakūṭaś ca niṣadhaścāsya dakṣiṇe
nīlaḥ śvetaś ca śṛṅgo ca uttare varṣaparvatāḥ
lakṣapramāṇau dvau madhye daśahīnās tathāpare
bhārataṃ prathamaṃ varṣantataḥ kimpuruṣaṃ smṛtaṃ
uttarāḥ kuravaś caiva yathā vai bhārataṃ tathā
ilāvṛtaṃ mahābhāga catvāraścātra parvatāḥ
viṣkambhā racitā meroryojanāyutavistṛtāḥ
pūrveṇa mandaro nāma dakṣiṇe gandhamādanaḥ
vipulaḥ paścime pārśve supārśvaścottare smṛtaḥ
ekādaśaśatāyāmāḥ pādapā giriketavaḥ
jambūdvīpeti sañjñā syāt phalaṃ jambā gajopamaṃ
jambūnadīrasenāsyāstvidaṃ jāmbūnadaṃ paraṃ
supārśvaḥ pūrvato meroḥ ketumālastu paścime
vanaṃ caitrarathaṃ pūrve dakṣiṇe gandhamādanaḥ
aruṇodaṃ mahābhadraṃ saṃśitodaṃ samānasaṃ
śitābhaś cakramuñjādyāḥ pūrvataḥ keśarācalāḥ
dakṣiṇendrestrikūṭādyāḥ śiśivāsamukhā jale
śaṅkhakūṭādayaḥ saumye merau ca brahmaṇaḥ purī
caturdaśasahasrāṇi yojanānāñca dikṣu ca
indrādilokapālānāṃ samantāt brahmaṇaḥ puraḥ
viṣṇupādāt plāvayitvā candraṃ svargāt patantyapi
pūrveṇa śītā bhadrāśvācchailācchailādgatārṇavaṃ
prayāti sāgaraṃ kṛtvā saptabhedātha paścimaṃ
ānīlaniṣadhāyāmau mālyavadgandhamādanau
bhāratāḥ ketumālāś ca bhadrāśvāḥ kuravas tathā
patrāṇi lokapadmasya maryādāśailavāhyataḥ
jaṭharo devakūṭaś ca maryādāparvatāvubhau
tau dakṣiṇottarāyāmāvānīlaniṣadhāyatau
aśītiyojanāyāmāvarṇavāntarvyavasthitau
niṣadhaḥ pāripātraś ca maryādāparvatāvubhau
pūrvapañcāyatāvetāvarṇavāntarvyavasthitau
jāṭharādyāś ca maryādāśailā meroś caturdiśaṃ
keśarādiṣu yā droṇyastāsu santi purāṇi hi
lakṣmīviṣṇvagnisūryādidevānāṃ munisattama
bhaumānāṃ svargadharmāṇāṃ na pāpāstatra yānti ca
bhārate kūrmarūpī ca matsyarūpaḥ kuruṣvapi
kimpuruṣādyaṣṭasu kṣudbhītiśokādikaṃ na ca
catturviṃśatisāhasraṃ prajā jīvantyanāmayāḥ
kṛtādikalpanā nāsti bhaumānyambhāṃsi nāmbudāḥ
sarveṣveteṣu varṣeṣu sapta sapta kulācalāḥ
nadyaś ca śataśastebhyastīrthabhūtāḥ prajajñire
bhārate yāni nīrthāni tāni tīrthāni vacmi te
tīrthamāhātmyaṃ
māhātmyaṃ sarvatīrthānāṃ vakṣye yadbhaktimuktidaṃ
pratigrāhādupāvṛtto laghvāhāro jitendriyaḥ
adatvā kāñcanaṃ gāś ca daridro nāma jāyate
puṣkaraṃ paramaṃ tīrthaṃ sānnidhyaṃ hi trisandhyakaṃ
daśakoṭisahasrāṇi tīrthānāṃ vipra puṣkare
devāḥ prāptāḥ siddhimatra snātāḥ pitṛsurārcakāḥ
puṣkare duṣkaraṃ gantuṃ puṣkare duṣkaraṃ tapaḥ
duṣkaraṃ puṣkare dānaṃ vastuṃ caiva suduṣkaraṃ
tatra vāsājjapacchrāddhāt kulānāṃ śatamuddharet
jambumārgaṃ ca tatraiva tīrthantaṇḍulikāśramaṃ
karṇāśramaṃ koṭitīrthaṃ narmadā cārvudaṃ paraṃ
tīrthañcarmaṇvatī sindhuḥ somanāthaḥ prabhāsakaṃ
piṇḍārakaṃ dvārakā ca gomatī sarvasiddhidā
bhūmitīrthaṃ brahmatuṅgaṃ tīrthaṃ pañcanadaṃ paraṃ
bhīmatīrthaṃ girīndrañca devikā pāpanāśinī
tīrthaṃ vinaśanaṃ puṇyaṃ nāgodbhedamaghārdanaṃ
tīrthaṃ kumārakoṭiś ca sarvadānīritāni ca
kurukṣetraṃ gamiṣyāmi kurukṣetre vasāmyahaṃ
ya evaṃ satataṃ brūyātso 'malaḥ prāpnuyāddivaṃ
tatra viṣṇvādayo devāstatra vāsāddhariṃ vrajet
pāṃśavopi kurukṣetre nayanti paramāṃ gatiṃ
dharmatīrthaṃ suvarṇākhyaṃ gaṅgādvāramanuttamaṃ
tīrthaṃ kaṇakhalaṃ puṇyaṃ bhadrakarṇahradantathā
gaṅgāsasvatīsaṅgaṃ brahmāvartamaghārdanaṃ
bhṛgutuṅgañca kubjāmraṃ gaṅgodbhedamaghāntakaṃ
kapālamocanaṃ tīrthantīrtharājaṃ prayāgakaṃ
gomatīgaṅgayoḥ saṅgaṃ gaṅgā sarvatra nākadā
tīrthaṃ rājagṛhaṃ puṇyaṃ śālagrāmamaghāntakaṃ
vaṭeśaṃ vāmanntīrthaṃ kālikāsaṅgamuttamaṃ
lauhityaṃ karatoyākhyaṃ śoṇañcātharṣabhaṃ paraṃ
godāvarī tuṅgabhadrā kāvero varadā nadī
tāpī payoṣṇī revā ca daṇḍakāraṇyamuttamaṃ
kālañjaraṃ muñjavaṭantīrthaṃ sūrpārakaṃ paraṃ
mandākinī citrakūṭaṃ śṛṅgaverapuraṃ paraṃ
avantī paramaṃ tīrthamayodhyā pāpanāśanī
gaṅāmāhātmyaṃ
gaṅāmāhātmyamākhyāsye sevyā sā bhuktimuktidā
yeṣāṃ madhye yāti gaṅgā te deśā pāvanā varāḥ
gatirgaṅgā tu bhūtānāṃ gatimanveṣatāṃ
sadā
gaṅgā tārayate cobhau vaṃśau nityaṃ hi sevitā
cāndrāyaṇasahasrācca gaṅgāmbhaḥpānamuttamaṃ
gaṅāṃ māsantu saṃsevya sarvayajñaphalaṃ labhet
yāvadasthi ca gaṅgāyāṃ tāvat svarge sa tiṣṭhati
gaṅgātīrthasamudbhūtamṛddhārī so 'ghahārkavat
darśanāt sparśanāt pānāttathā gaṅgetikīrtanāt
punāti puṇyapuruṣān śataśītha sahasraśaḥ
prayāgamāhātmyaṃ
prayāge brahmaviṣṇvādyā deva munivarāḥ sthitāḥ
saritaḥ sāgarāḥ siddhā gandharvasarāpsas tathā
tatra trīṇyagnikuṇḍāni teṣāṃ madhye tu jāhnavī
gaṅgāyamunayormadhyaṃ pṛthivyā jaghanaṃ smṛtaṃ
prayāgaṃ sapratiṣṭhānam kambalāśvatarāvubhau
tīrthaṃ bhogavatī caiva vedī proktā prajāpateḥ
tatra vedāś ca yajñāś ca mūrtimantaḥ prayāgake
prayāge saṅgate dānaṃ śrāddhaṃ japyādi cākṣayaṃ
daśatīrthasahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭikoṭyas tathāparāḥ
teṣāṃ sānnidhyamatraiva prayāgaṃ paramantataḥ
gavāṃ koṭipradānādyat tryahaṃ snānasya tatphalaṃ
prayāge māghamāse tu evamāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ
sarvatra sulabhā gaṅgā triṣu sthāneṣu durlabhā
gaṅādvāre prayāge ca gaṅgāsāgarasaṅgame
vaṭamūle saṅgamādau mṛto viṣṇupurīṃ vrajet
urvaśīpulinaṃ ramyaṃ tīrthaṃ sandhyāvatas tathā
koṭītīrthañcāśvamedhaṃ gaṅgāyamunamuttamaṃ
mānasaṃ rajasā hīnaṃ tīrthaṃ vāsarakaṃ paraṃ
vārāṇasīmāhātmyam
vārāṇasī paraṃ tīrthaṃ gauryai prāha maheśvaraḥ
bhuktimuktipradaṃ puṇyaṃ vasatāṃ gṛṇatāṃ hariṃ
gaurīkṣetraṃ na muktaṃ vai avimuktaṃ tataḥ smṛtaṃ
aśmanā caraṇau hatvā vasetkāśīnna hi tyajet
hariś candraṃ paraṃ guhyaṃ guhyamāmnātakeśvaraṃ
japyeśvaraṃ paraṃ guhyaṃ guhyaṃ śrīparvataṃ tathā
mahālayaṃ paraṃ guhyaṃ bhṛguś caṇḍeśvaraṃ tathā
varaṇā ca nadī cāsīt tayormadhye vārāṇasī
atra snānaṃ japo homo maraṇaṃ devapūjanaṃ
śrāddhaṃ dānaṃ nivāsaś ca yadyat syādbhuktimuktidaṃ
narmadādimāhātmyam
narmadādikamāhātmyaṃ vakṣyehaṃ narmadāṃ parāṃ
sadyaḥ punāti gāṅgeyaṃ darśanādvāri nārmadaṃ
ṣaṣṭistīrthasahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭikoṭyas tathāparāḥ
kāverīsaṅgamaṃ puṇyaṃ śrīparvatamataḥ śṛṇu
gaurī śrīrūpiṇī tepe tapastāmabravīddhariḥ
samantādyojanaśataṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ bhaviṣyati
atra dānantapo japyaṃ śrāddhaṃ sarvamathākṣayaṃ
maraṇaṃ śivalokāya sarvadaṃ tīrthamuttamaṃ
gayāmāhātmyam
gayāmāhātmyamākhyāsye gayātīrthottamottamaṃ
uktaḥ kṣīrābdhigo viṣṇuḥ pālayāsmān gayāsurāt
tathetyuktvā gato viṣṇurdaityaṃ dṛṣṭvā na vā hariṃ
gatāḥ śūnyā mahī svarge devā brahmādayaḥ surāḥ
gatā ūcurhariṃ devāḥ śūnyā bhūstridivaṃ hare
yāgārthaṃ daityadehaṃ tvaṃ prārthaya tridaśaiḥ saha
atithiḥ prārthayāmi tvāndehaṃ yāgāya pāvanaṃ
yāgaṃ cakāra calite dehi pūrṇāhutiṃ vibhuḥ
punarbrahmābravīdviṣṇuṃ pūrṇakāle 'suro 'calat
śiṣṇurdharmamathāhūya prāha devamayīṃ śilām
gadādharo madīyātha mūrtiḥ sthāsyati sāmaraiḥ
dharmaḥ śilāṃ devamayīṃ tac chrutvādhārayat parāṃ
yā dharmāddharmavatyāñca jātā dharmavratā sutā
marīcirbrahmaṇaḥ putrastāmuvāha taponvitāṃ
yathā hariḥ śriyā reme gauryā śambhus tathā tayā
kuśapuṣpādyaraṇyācca ānīyātiśramānvitaḥ
bhuktvā dharmavratāṃ prāha pādasaṃvāhanaṃ kuru
pādasaṃvāhanaṃ kurve brahmā pūjyo gurorguruḥ
vicintya pūjayāmāsa brahmāṇaṃ cārhaṇādibhiḥ
marīcistāmapaśyat sa śaśāpoktivyatikramāt
pādābhyaṅgaṃ parityajya tvadguruḥ pūjito mayā
adoṣāhaṃ yatastvaṃ hi śāpaṃ prāpsyasi śaṅkarāt
dharmavratā pṛthak śāpaṃ dhārayitvāgrimadhyagāt
tapaś cacāra varṣāṇāṃ sahasrāṇyayutāni ca
tato viṣṇvādayo devā varaṃ brūhīti cābruvan
devā ūcuḥ
datto marīcinā śāpo bhaviṣyati na cānyathā
śilā pavitrā devāṅghrilakṣitā tvaṃ bhaviṣyasi
devavratā devaśilā sarvadevādirūpiṇī
sarvadevamayī puṇyā niś calāyārasusya hi
brahmā viṣṇuś ca rudrādyā gaurīlakṣmīmukhāḥ surāḥ
devavratāvacaḥ śrutvā tathetyuktvā divaṅgatāḥ
sā dharmaṇāsurasyāsya dhṛtā devamayī śilā
kṣīrābdhigo hariḥ prādāt svamūrtiṃ śrīgadādharaṃ
niś calārthaṃ svayaṃ devaḥ sthita ādigadādharaḥ
gado nāmāsuro daityaḥ sa hato viṣṇunā purā
tadasthinirmitā cādyā gadā yā viśvakarmaṇā
ādyayā gadayā hetipramukhā rākṣasā hatāḥ
devamayyāṃ śilāyāṃ ca sthite cādigadādhare
gayāsure niś caleya brahmā pūrṇāhutiṃ dadau
viṣṇorvacanamātreṇa kinnasyānniś calohyahaṃ
devā ūcuḥ
tīrthasya karaṇe yat tvamasmābhir niś calīkṛtaḥ
viṣṇoḥ śambhorbrahmaṇaś ca kṣetraṃ tava bhaviṣyati
ityuktvā te sthitā devā devyastīrthādayaḥ sthitāḥ
yāgaṃ kṛtvā dadau brahmā ṛtvigbhyo dakṣiṇāṃ tadā
pañcakrośaṃ gayākṣetraṃ pañcāśat pañca cārpayet
grāmān svarṇagirīn kṛtvā nadīrdugdhamadhuśravāḥ
kāmadhenuṃ kalpataruṃ svarṇarūpyagṛhāṇi ca
sthitā yadā gayāyānte śaptāte brahmaṇā tadā
vidyāvivarjitā yūyaṃ tṛṣṇāyuktā bhaviṣyatha
dugdhādivarjitā nadyaḥ śailāḥ pāṣāṇarūpiṇaḥ
brahmāṇaṃ brāhmaṇaścocur naṣṭaṃ śāpena śākhilaṃ
jīvanāya prasādannaḥ kuru viprāṃś ca so 'bravīt
tīrthopajīvikā yūyaṃ sacandrārkaṃ bhaviṣyatha
ye yuṣmān pūjayiṣyanti gayāyāmāgatā narāḥ
gayopi cākarodyāgaṃ bahvannaṃ bahudakṣiṇaṃ
gayā purī tena nāmnā pāṇḍavā ījire hariṃ
agnipurāṇam
maharṣiśrīmadvedavyāsena praṇītam
śrīlaśrī vaṅgadeśīyāsiyātiksamājānujñayā
śrīrājendralālamitreṇa pariśodhitam
kalikātārājadhānyāṃ gaṇeśayantre mudritañca
saṃvat
athāgnipurāṇasya dvitīyakhaṇḍasyānukramaṇikā
agnipurāṇaṃ
gayāyātrāvidhiḥ
udyataścedgayāṃ yātuṃ śrāddhaṃ kṛtvā vidhānataḥ
vidhāya kārpaṭīveśaṃ grāmasyāpi pradakṣiṇaṃ
kṛtvā pratidinaṅgacchet saṃyataścāpratigrahī
svargārohaṇasopānaṃ pitṝṇāntu pade pade
brahmajñānena kiṃ kāryaṃ gogṛhe maraṇena kiṃ
gayāprāptaṃ sutaṃ dṛṣṭvā pitṝṇāmutsavo bhavet
padbhyāmapi jalaṃ spṛṣṭvā asmabhyaṃ kinna dāsyati
brahmajñānaṃ gayāśrāddhaṃ gogṛhe maraṇaṃ tathā
vāsaḥ puṃsāṃ kurukṣetre muktireṣā caturvidhā
kāṅkṣanti pitaraḥ putraṃ narakādbhayabhīravaḥ
gayāṃ yāsyati yaḥ putraḥ sa nastrātā bhaviṣyati
muṇḍanañcopavāsaś ca sarvatīrtheṣvayaṃ vidhiḥ
na kālādirgayātīrthe dadyāt piṇḍāṃś ca nityaśaḥ
pakṣatrayanivāsī ca punātyāsaptatamaṃ kulaṃ
aṣṭakāsu ca vṛddhauca gayāyāṃ mṛtavāsare
divyāntarīkṣabhaumādi pitṛmātrādi tarpayet
mātā pitāmahī caiva tathaiva prapitāmahī
mātāmahaḥ pramātāmaho vṛddhapramātāmahaḥ
tebhyonyebhya imān piṇḍānuddhārāya dadāmyahaṃ
oṃ namaḥ sūryadevāya somabhaumajñarūpiṇe
jīvaśukraśanaiścārirāhuketusvarūpiṇe
sūryaṃ natvā vrajenmaunī naro dakṣiṇamānasaṃ
dakṣiṇe mānase snānaṃ karomi pitṛtṛptaye
gayāyāmāgataḥ svargaṃ yāntu me pitaro 'khilāḥ
śrāddhaṃ piṇḍantataḥ kṛtvā sūryaṃ natvā vadedidaṃ
bhuktimuktipradaḥ sarvapitṝṇāṃ bhavabhāvitaḥ
kavyavālānalaḥ somo yamaś caivāryamā tathā
agniṣvāttā varhiṣada ājyapāḥ pitṛdevatāḥ
āgacchantu mahābhāgā yuṣmābhī rakṣitāstviha
madīyāḥ pitaro ye ca mātṛmātāmahādayaḥ
teṣāṃ piṇḍapradātāhamāgato 'smi gayāmimāṃ
udīcyāṃ muṇḍapṛṣṭhasya devarṣigaṇapūjitaṃ
nāmnā kanakhalaṃ tīrthaṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutaṃ
siddhānāṃ prītijananaiḥ pāpānāñca bhayaṅkaraiḥ
tatra snātvā divaṃ yānti krīḍante bhuvi mānavāḥ
nāgājjanārdanāt kūpādvaṭāccottaramānasāt
muṇḍapṛṣṭhanāgādyāś ca sārāt sāramathāntaraṃ
dṛṣṭiramyādikaṃ yasmāt phalgutīrthaṃ na phalguvat
phalgutīrthe naraḥ snātvā dṛṣṭvā devaṃ gadādharaṃ
etena kiṃ na paryāptaṃ nṛṇāṃ sukṛṭakāriṇāṃ
pṛthivyāṃ yāni tīrthāni āsamudrātsarāṃsi ca
phalgutīrthe tīrtharāje karoti snānamādṛtaḥ
snātvā śrāddhī piṇḍado 'tha nameddevaṃ pitāmahaṃ
kalau māheśvarā lokā atra devī gadādharaḥ
pitāmaho liṅgarūpī tannamāmi maheśvaraṃ
gadādharaṃ balaṃ kāmamaniruddhaṃ narāyaṇaṃ
brahmaviṣṇunṛsiṃhākhyaṃ varāhādiṃ namāmyahaṃ
tato gadādharaṃ dṛṣṭvā kulānāṃ śatamuddharet
dharmāraṇyaṃ dvitīye 'hni mataṅgasyāśrame vare
mataṅgavāpyāṃ saṃsnāya śrāddhakṛt piṇḍado bhavet
mataṅgeśaṃ suddheśaṃ natvā cedamudīrayet
pramāṇaṃ devatāḥ santu lokapālāś ca sākṣiṇaḥ
mayāgatya mataṅge 'smin pitṝṇāṃ niṣkṛtiḥ kṛtā
pitṝṇāṃ brahmalokāya brahmarṣigaṇasevite
tarpaṇaṃ śrāddhakṛt piṇḍaṃ pradadyāttu prasecanaṃ
kuryācca vājapeyārthī brahmayūpapradakṣiṇaṃ
āmnāya siktāḥ pitaraś ca tṛptā ekā kriyā dvyarthakarī prasiddhā
brahmāṇañca namaskṛtya kulānāṃ śatamuddharet
kṛtvā śrāddhaṃ sapiṇḍañca gayāśirasi kārayet
pañcakrośaṃ gayākṣetraṃ krośamekaṃ gayāśiraḥ
tatra piṇḍapradānena kulānāṃ śatamudharet
muṇḍapṛṣṭhe padaṃ nnyāstaṃ mahādevena dhīmatā
muṇḍapṛṣṭhe śiraḥ sākṣād gayāśira udāhṛtaṃ
sākṣād gayāśirastatra phalgutīrthāśramaṃ kṛtaṃ
amṛtaṃ tatra vahati pitṝṇāndattamakṣayaṃ
snātvā daśāśvamedhe tu dṛṣṭvā devaṃ pitāmahaṃ
rudrapādaṃ naraḥ spṛṣṭvā neha bhūyo 'bhijāyate
śamīpatrapramāṇena piṇḍaṃ datvā gayāśire
pāyasenātha piṣṭena śaktunā caruṇā tathā
piṇḍadānaṃ taṇḍulaiś ca godhūmaistilamiśritaiḥ
piṇḍaṃ datvā rudrapade kulānāṃ śatamuddharet
tathā viṣṇupade śrāddhapiṇḍado hy ṛṇamuktikṛt
pitrādīnāṃ śatakulaṃ svātmānaṃ tārayennaraḥ
pade vāhavanīyasya śrāddhī yajñaphalaṃ labhet
ādityasya rathaṃ natvā karṇādityaṃ namīnnaraḥ
kanakeśapadaṃ natvā gayākedārakaṃ namet
viśālo 'pi gayāśīrṣe piṇḍado 'bhūcca putravān
viśālāyāṃ viśālo 'bhūdrājaputro 'bravīd dvijān
kathaṃ putrādayaḥ syurme dvijā ūcurviśālakaṃ
gayāyāṃ piṇḍadānena tava sarvaṃ bhaviṣyati
viśālo 'pi gayāśīrṣe pitṛpiṇḍāndadau tataḥ
dṛṣṭvākāśe sitaṃ raktaṃ puruṣāṃstāṃś ca pṛṣṭavān
mama raktaḥ pitā putra kṛṣṇaś caiva pitāmahaḥ
abravīt narakaṃ prāptā tvayā muktīkṛtā vayaṃ
piṇḍadānād brahmalokaṃ brajāma iti te gatāḥ
viśālaḥ prāptaputādī rājyaṃ kṛtvā hariṃ yayau
śravaṇadvādaśīyoge kumbhaḥ sānnaś ca sodakaḥ
dattaḥ purā sa madhyāhne jīvanāyopatiṣṭhate
dhanaṃ gṛhītvā me gaccha gayāyāṃ piṇḍado bhava
vaṇigdhanaṃ gṛhītvā tu gayāyāṃ piṇḍado 'bhavat
gayāśīrṣe piṇḍadānādātmānaṃ svapitṝṃs tathā
pitṛvaṃśe sutā ye ca mātṛvaṃśe tathaiva ca
guruśvaśurabandhūnāṃ ye cānye bāndhavā mṛtāḥ
ye me kule luptapiṇḍāḥ putradāravivarjitāḥ
kriyālopagatā ye ca jātyandhāḥ puṅgavas tathā
virūpā āmagarbhā ye jñātājñātāḥ kule mama
teṣāṃ piṇḍo mayā datto hy akṣayyamupatiṣṭhatāṃ
te sarve tṛptimāyāntu piṇḍadānena sarvadā
gadāprakṣālane tīrthe gadālole 'tipāvane
snānaṃ karāmi saṃsāragadaśāntyai janārdana
pitrādīnāmakṣayāya sarvapāpakṣayāya ca
śrāddhaṃ vaṭatale kuryād brāhmaṇānāñca bhojanaṃ
gayāyāmannadātā yaḥ pitarastena putriṇaḥ
vaṭaṃ vaṭeśvaraṃ natvā pūjayet prapitāmahaṃ
akṣayāṃllabhate lokān kulānāṃ śatamuddharet
gayāyātrāvidhiḥ
gāyatryaiva mahānadyāṃ snātaḥ sandhyāṃ samācaret
gāyatryā agrataḥ prātaḥ śrāddhaṃ piṇḍamathākṣayaṃ
sāvitrīpurataḥ sandhyāṃ piṇḍadānañca tatpade
baliṃ kākaśilāyāñca kumārañca namettataḥ
svargadvāryāṃ somakuṇḍe vāyutīrthe 'tha piṇḍadaḥ
bhavedākaśagaṅgāyāṃ kapilāyāñca piṇḍadaḥ
kapileśaṃ śivaṃ natvā rukmikuṇḍe ca piṇḍadaḥ
koṭītīrthe ca koṭīśaṃ natvāmoghapade naraḥ
gadālole vānarake gopracāre ca piṇḍadaḥ
natvā gāvaṃ vaitaraṇyāmekaviṃśakuloddhṛtiḥ
śrāddhapiṇḍapradātā syāt krauñcapade ca piṇḍadaḥ
tṛtīyāyāṃ viśālāyāṃ niścirāyāñca piṇḍadaḥ
ṛṇamokṣe pāpamokṣe bhasmakuṇḍe 'tha bhasmanā
gayāyāṃ pitṛrūpeṇa svayameva janārdanaḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ mucyate vai ṛṇatrayāt
mārkaṇḍeyeśvaraṃ natvā namedgṛdhreśvaraṃ naraḥ
mūlakṣetre maheśasya dhārāyāṃ piṇḍado bhavet
gṛdhrakūṭe gṛdhravaṭe dhautapāde ca piṇḍadaḥ
puṣkariṇyāṃ kardamāle rāmatīrthe ca piṇḍadaḥ
prabhāseśannamet pretaśilāyāṃ piṇḍado bhavet
divyāntarīkṣabhūmiṣṭhāḥ pitaro bāndhavādayaḥ
pretādirūpā muktāḥ syuḥ piṇḍair dattair mayākhilāḥ
sthānatraye pretaśilā gayāśirasi pāvanī
gayānābhau suṣumṇāyāṃ mahākoṣṭyāñca piṇḍadaḥ
gadādharāgrato muṇḍapṛṣṭhe devyāś ca sannidhau
muṇdapṛṣṭhaṃ namedādau kṣetrapālādisaṃyutam
pūjayitvā bhayaṃ na syādviṣarogādināśanam
hṛṣīkeśaṃ namaskṛtya tadagre piṇḍado bhavet
mahālakṣmīṃ prārcya gaurīṃ maṅgalāñca sarasvatīm
somanāthañca kāleśaṅkedāraṃ prapitāmaham
siddheśvarañca rudreśaṃ rāmeśaṃ brahmakeśvaram
aṣṭaliṅgāni guhyāni pūjayitvā tu sarvabhāk
nārāyaṇaṃ varāhañca nārasiṃhaṃ namecchriye
brahmaviṣṇumaheśākhyaṃ tripuraghnamaśeṣadam
sītāṃ rāmañca garuḍaṃ vāmanaṃ samprapūjya ca
devarūpā śilā puṇyā tasmāddevamayī śilā
gayāyāṃ nahi tat sthānaṃ yatra tīrthaṃ na vidyate
yannāmnā pātayet piṇḍaṃ tannayedbrahma śāśvatam
phalgvīśaṃ phalgucaṇḍīṃ ca praṇamyāṅgārakeśvaram
haṃsatīrthe koṭitīrthe yatra pāṇḍuśilānnadaḥ
tatra syādagnidhārāyāṃ madhusravasi piṇḍadaḥ
sarvān pitṝṃstārayecca sarasvatyāñca piṇḍadaḥ
sandhyāmupāsya sāyāhne nameddevīṃ sarasvatīm
gayāṃ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya gayāviprān prapūjya ca
annadānādikaṃ sarvaṃ kṛtantatrākṣayaṃ bhavet
gadādharaṃ gayāvāsaṃ pitrādīnāṃ gatipradam
dharmārthakāmamokṣārthaṃ yogadaṃ praṇamāmyaham
āgato 'smi gayāṃ deva pitṛkārye gadādharaḥ
tvaṃ me sākṣī bhavādyeha anṛṇo 'hamṛṇatrayāt
sākṣiṇaḥ santu me devā brahmeśānādayas tathā
mayā gayāṃ samāsādya pitṝṇāṃ niṣkṛtiḥ kṛtā
gayāmāhātmyapaṭhanācchrāddhādau brahmalokabhāk
pitṝṇāmakṣayaṃ śrāddhamakṣayaṃ brahmalokadam
śrāddhakalpaḥ
kātyāyanī munīnāha yathā śrāddhaṃ tathā vade
gayādau śrāddhaṃ kurvīta saṅkrāntyādau viśeṣataḥ
yatīn gṛhasthasādhūn vā snātakāñchrotriyān dvijān
anavadyān karmaniṣṭhān śiṣṭānācārasaṃyutān
varjayecchitrikuṣṭhyādīnna gṛhṇīyānnimantritān
snātāñchucīṃs tathā dāntān prāṅmukhān devakarmaṇi
evaṃ mātāmahādeś ca śākair api ca kārayet
sarvāṃś ca paṅktimūrdhanyān pṛcchet praśne tathāsane
darbhānāstīrya dviguṇān pitre devādikañcaret
